1a1(phal chen): (cha) @#/ ! /sangs rgyas phal po che bzhugs so/ /
1a2(phal chen): (黃) 大方廣佛華嚴經第六部
1b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po dang po/
1b2(phal chen): de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs mtshan mo'i lha mo rab tu dga' ba'i
1b3(phal chen): m ig 'gro bar rnam par snang ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa kun tu bzang po'i
1b4(phal chen): dga' ba shin tu yangs shing dri ma med pa'i shugs kyi rgyal mtshan de la mos par bya ba dang / khong du chud par bya ba dang /
1b5(phal chen): rtogs par bya ba dang / shes par bya ba dang / yid ches par bya ba
1b6(phal chen): dang / rab tu gzhol bar bya ba dang / rgyas par dgang ba dang / rjes su shes par bya ba dang /
1b7(phal chen): rjes su dran par bya ba dang / rjes su gzhol bar bya ba dang / bsgom pa byed cing / dge ba'i
1b8(phal chen): bshes gnyen gyi gdams ngag la nan tan du bya ba dang / gdams ngag rjes su bstan pa la
2a1(phal chen): bar chad med par bya ba'i phyir mtshan mo'i lha mo rab tu dga' ba'i mig 'gro bar rnam par snang bas/ 'gro bar gtams pa rjes su dran par byed cing / dge ba'i bshes gnyen
2a2(phal chen): blta ba'i rjes su sems dpa'i dbang po'i dkyil 'khor dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen mthong ba thob par bya ba la yang dag par spyod pa/ phyogs kun tu mngon par ltas pa dang / dge ba'i bshes
2a3(phal chen): gnyen btsal bar yid la bya ba dang / nga rgyal thams cad dang bral ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsnyen bkur ba'i tshogs chen pos yongs su bsgrub par zhe non pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang /
2a4(phal chen): rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pa'i dge ba'i rtsa bas dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi thabs mkhas pa'i spyod pa thams cad la bsam pa mi phyed pas zhugs pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen la brten pa yongs su 'phel
2a5(phal chen): bar bya ba la brtson 'grus kyi shugs chen po'i rgya mtsho yongs su skyes pa/ bskal pa thams cad du dge ba'i bshes gnyen mnyam pa nyid khong du chud par gnas par bya ba'i smon lam dang ldan pa de/
2a6(phal chen): mtshan mo'i lha mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi drung du song ngo / /de de ltar 'gro ba'i tshe/ mtshan mo'i lha mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi byang chub sems dpa'i rnam
2a7(phal chen): par thar pa 'jig rten thams cad mngon du gyur pas 'gro ba rnam par 'dul ba ston pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba yongs su bstan pa'i phyir/ mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos yongs su grub pa'i lus
2a8(phal chen): bstan te/ mdzod spu nas 'od zer ye shes kyi 'od kun tu snang ba dri ma med pa'i mdangs kyi rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba 'od zer gyi 'khor mtha' dang dbus med pa dang ldan pa bkye'o/ /des 'jig rten
2b1(phal chen): thams cad snang bar byas nas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyi spyi bor 'dus te lus thams cad du khyab par gyur to/ /tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'od zer des reg par gyur ma thag tu
2b2(phal chen): de nyid kyi mod la ting nge 'dzin shin tu rdul dang bral ba zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor thob par gyur to/ /de thob pas mtshan mo'i lha mo rab tu dga' ba'i mig 'gro bar rnam par snang ba dang / mtshan mo'i
2b3(phal chen): lha mo sems can kun nas skyong ba'i gzi brjid kyi dpal gnyis kyi bar gyi lam na sa'i dkyil 'khor yod pa de la me'i rdul shin tu phra ba 'am/ chu'i rdul shin tu phra ba 'am/ sa'i rdul shin tu phra ba 'am/
2b4(phal chen): rdo rje'i rdul shin tu phra ba 'am/ nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po dam pa sna tshogs kyi rdul shin tu phra ba dang / me tog dang / spos dang / phye ma'i rdul shin tu phra ba 'am/ rgyan thams cad kyi rdul
2b5(phal chen): shin tu phra ba 'am/ dmigs pa thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba ji snyed cig yod pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba de dag thams cad la rdul phra mo re re zhing yang / 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi
2b6(phal chen): zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed/ chu'i phung po dang bcas/ me'i phung po dang bcas/ rlung gi phung po dang bcas/ sa'i phung po dang bcas/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi mtshams
2b7(phal chen): dang bcas/ gzhi dang bcas/ rten dang bcas/ dbyibs sna tshogs can sa'i gzhi rnam pa tha dad pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i ri'i 'khor sna tshogs can/ chu klung dang mtsho sna
2b8(phal chen): tshogs kyis brgyan pa rgya mtsho sna tshogs kyi kun nas 'khor ba/ lha rdzas kyi khyim sna tshogs kyi rgyan dang ldan pa/ shing sna tshogs kyis yongs su gang ba/
3a1(phal chen): nam mkha'i dbyings kyi rgyan sna tshogs can/ lha'i grongs khyer gyi khyim gyi rgyan dang bcas pa/ klu'i grong khyer gyi khyim gyi rgyan dang bcas pa/ gnod sbyin gyi grong khyer gyi khyim gyi rgyan dang bcas pa/
3a2(phal chen): dri za'i grong khyer gyi khyim gyi rgyan dang bcas pa/ lha ma yin gyi grongs khyer gyi khyim gyi rgyan dang bcas pa/ nam mkha' lding gi grong khyer gyi khyim gyi rgyan dang bcas pa/ mi 'am ci'i grong khyer gyi khyim gyi rgyan dang bcas pa/
3a3(phal chen): lto 'phye chen po'i grong khyer gyi khyim gyi rgyan dang bcas pa/ mi'i grong khyer gyi khyim gyi rgyan dang bcas pa/ phyogs dang phyogs mtshams thams cad na rnam par gnas pa'i sems can thams cad kyi grong khyer gyi gnas
3a4(phal chen): dang / sems can dmyal ba'i 'jig rten gyi yul dang / byol song gi skye gnas kyi 'jig rten gyi yul dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyis yul dang / mi dang mi ma yin gyi lam gyi rgyud kyi shi 'pho ba dang / skye ba'i yul dang bcas pa
3a5(phal chen): skye ba sna tshogs kyis ma 'dres pa'i rgyud mtha' yas pa'i bye brag la yongs su gzhol ba rnams 'du zhing 'jig par gyur pa mthong ngo / /'jig rten gyi khams de dag kyang rnam pa sna tshogs su mthong ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams
3a6(phal chen): la la ni kun nas nyon mongs par mthong ngo / /la la ni yongs su dag par mthong ngo / /la la ni shin tu kun nas nyon mongs par mthong ngo / /la la ni lam gyi rgyud yongs su dag par mthong ngo / /la la ni kun nas
3a7(phal chen): nyon mongs pa yongs su dag par mthong ngo / /la la ni rnam par dag pa la kun nas nyon mongs par mthong ngo / /la la ni shin tu yongs su dag par mthong ngo / /la la ni gzhi mnyam par mthong ngo / /la la ni
3a8(phal chen): spyi 'u tshugs su gnas par mthong ngo / /la la ni snrel gzhir 'dug par mthong ngo / /'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi sems can gyi lam gyi rgyud dang / sems can gyi skye gnas thams cad na mtshan mo'i lha
3b1(phal chen): mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal sems can so so nas 'dul ba'i rkyen bzhin du 'jig rten thams cad la ma 'dres par yongs su bstan pa'i phyir/ sems can thams cad la mngon du gyur par
3b2(phal chen): gnas par mthong ngo / /sems can tshe'i tshad rnam pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa dang / mos pa'i spyod yul rnam pa sna tshogs can dang / lus rnam pa sna tshogs can dang lus rnam pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa dang / ngag gi rnam
3b3(phal chen): par phye ba dang / nges pa'i tshig gi 'du byed kyi tha snyad rnam pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa dang / sbyor ba'i rnam pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa dang / dbang gi rnam pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa rnams yongs su smyin par bya ba dang gdul ba'i don
3b4(phal chen): du sems can thams cad la ma 'dres par mngon sum du gnas par mthong ngo / /de yang 'di lta ste/ sems can dmyal ba'i lam gyi rgyud du gtogs pa'i sems can rnams kyi sems can dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal
3b5(phal chen): dang / 'jig pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / byol song gi skye gnas sna tshogs su skyes pa'i sems can rnams kyi gcig la gcig za ba'i 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi lam gyi
3b6(phal chen): rgyud du gtogs pa'i sems can rnams kyi bkres pa dang / skom pa la stsogs pa'i sdug bsngal gyi 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / klu'i 'jig rten gyi lam gyi rgyud du gtogs pa'i sems can rnams kyi
3b7(phal chen): klu'i sdug bsngal dang / 'jigs pa thams cad rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'dod pa'i khams su gtogs pa'i sems can thams cad kyi 'dod pa'i sdug bsngal dang / 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / mi'i
3b8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi lam gyi rgyud du gtogs pa'i sems can rnams kyi mtshan mo'i mun pa mun nag gis chod pa'i mun pa'i 'jigs pa thams cad rnam par bzlog pa dang / mi snyan pa dang / bsngags pa ma yin pa dang /
4a1(phal chen): grags pa ma yin pa'i sgra dang / tshigs su bcad pa la mngon par zhen pa'i sems can rnams kyi grags pa ma yin pa dang / bsngags pa ma yin pa'i 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'khor gyi 'jigs
4a2(phal chen): par ltung ba'i sems can rnams kyi 'khor tu bag tsha ba'i 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'chi bas 'jigs shing sngang ba'i sems can rnams kyi 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / ngan song gi
4a3(phal chen): g.yang sas 'jig shing sngang ba'i sems can rnams kyi ngan song gi g.yang sas 'jig pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'chi ba med pas 'jigs shing skrag pa'i sems can rnams kyi 'khor du 'chi ba med pa'i
4a4(phal chen): bag tsha ba'i 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba chud zos kyis 'jigs shing bag tsha ba'i sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba chud zos kyi 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / byang chub kyi
4a5(phal chen): sems nyams kyis 'jigs shing bag tsha ba'i sems can rnams kyi byang chub kyi sems nyams kyi 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / sdig to'i grogs po dang phrad kyis 'jigs shing bag tsha ba'i sems can
4a6(phal chen): r nams sdig to'i grogs po dang phrad pa'i 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang bral gyis dogs shing bag tsha ba'i sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang bral ba'i 'jig
4a7(phal chen): pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi sar ltung gis 'jigs shing bag tsha ba'i sems can rnams kyi nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi sar ltung ba'i 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang /
4a8(phal chen): 'khor ba'i gnas sna tshogs kyi sdug bsngal gyis 'jigs shing skrag pa rnams kyi 'khor ba'i gnas sna tshogs kyi sdug bsngal gyis 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / sems can skal ba mi mnyam pa dang phrad
4b1(phal chen): kyis 'jigs shing bag tsha ba rnams kyi sems can bskal pa mi mnyam pa dang phrad pa'i 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / dus mi zad par skyes gyis 'jigs shing bag tsha ba rnams kyi dus myi zad par skye ba'i 'jigs
4b2(phal chen): pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / rigs ngan par skyes kyi 'jigs shing bag tsha ba rnams kyi rigs ngan par skye ba'i 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / sdig to'i las byas kyis 'jigs shing bag tsha ba rnams kyis sdig to'i las
4b3(phal chen): byed pa'i 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / las dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pas 'jigs shing sngang ba rnams kyi las dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa'i 'jig pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'du shes kyi rnam pa sna tshogs kyis gnas dang
4b4(phal chen): 'ching bas 'jigs shing sngang ba rnams kyi 'du shes rnam pa sna tshogs kyi gnas dang / 'ching ba'i 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir sems can them kas gcig la so sor mngon tu gyur par gnas pa mthong ngo / /'di lta
4b5(phal chen): ste sgo nga las skyes pa'i sems can dang / mngal nas skyes pa dang / drod gsher las skyes pa dang / rdzus te skyes pa dang / gzugs yod pa dang / gzugs med pa dang / 'du shes yod pa dang / 'du shes med pa dang /
4b6(phal chen): 'du shes yod pa 'ang ma yin/ 'du shes med pa yang ma yin pa'i sems can thams cad yongs su skyob pa'i smon lam gyi stobs mngon par bsgrub pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi shugs drag po dang /
4b7(phal chen): rnam par gnon pa shin tu yangs pa'i stobs dang / byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa chen po'i stobs dang mthu dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa dang / smon lam mngon par sgrub pa'i stobs
4b8(phal chen): kyis snying rje chen po'i tshul rgya mtsho'i shugs drag po shin tu skyes pa'i phyir 'gro ba thams cad du thogs pa med pa'i byams pa chen pos rgyas par dgang ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi bde ba yongs su
5a1(phal chen): bsgrub pa dang / dga' ba'i shugs rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang / sems can thams cad yongs su bsdu ba'i ye shes rab tu bsgrub pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa rgya chen po'i
5a2(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa dang / khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang ldan pas/ zhing thams cad yongs su dag par bya ba la mngon tu gyur par mthong ngo / /chos thams cad kyi rgyus shes par bya ba la mngon tu gyur pa dang /
5a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad mchod cing rim gror bya ba la mngon du gyur pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bstan pa yongs su gzung ba la mngon du gyur pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad bstsags pa la mngon du
5a4(phal chen): gyur pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad rnam par 'phel bar bya ba la mngon du gyur pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi sems la sgrib pa med par mngon du gyur par gnas pa dang / sems can thams
5a5(phal chen): cad kyi dbang po yongs su smin par bya ba la mngon du gyur par gnas pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi mos pa rgya mtsho rnam par sbyang ba la mngon du gyur pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi sgrib pa'i chos
5a6(phal chen): rnam par bzlog pa la mngon du gyur pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi mi shes pa'i mun pa rnam par bstsal ba la mngon du gyur cing thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes snang ba yongs su bskyed pa'i don du gnas pa
5a7(phal chen): mthong ngo / /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs gyis mtshan mo'i lha mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / rnam par 'phrul
5a8(phal chen): pa 'jig rten thams cad la mngon par gnas shing / 'gro ba rnam par 'dul ba ston pa bsam gyi mi khyab pa de lta bur mthong nas rab tu dga' ba skyes te/ spro ba chen po'i shugs drag po rgya mtsho rab tu thob nas/
5b1(phal chen): mtshan mo'i lha mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal la lus thams cad kyis phab ste phyag byas nas ngor gyen du bltaso/ /de nas mtshan mo'i lha mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal
5b2(phal chen): gyis byang chub sems dpa'i gzugs dang / mtshan rnam par dag pa de mi snang bar byas te/ mtshan mo'i lha mo'i gzugs su byas te/ rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad 'byin cing 'dug par gnas so/ /de nas tshong
5b3(phal chen): dpon gyi bu nor bzangs gyis mtshan mo'i lha mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi mdun du 'dug ste/ thal mo sbyar nas de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /khyod kyi sku yangs mtshan rab
5b4(phal chen): rgyan gyis brgyan/ /shin tu bzang zhing mdzes pa bdag gis mthong / /nam mkha' skar ma'i tshogs kyis brgyan pa bzhin/ /dpe byad bzang pos rnam par bris pa mthong / /'od kyi 'khor can sku bzang dam pa'i
5b5(phal chen): mchog / mtha' yas zhing gi rdul khams mang po snyed/ /kha dog sna tshogs rnam pa'i dpe tshul du/ /phyogs rnams kun gyi dbyings su khyab par gang / /'od zer dra ba mang po 'gro sems mnyam/ /khyod kyi ba
5b6(phal chen): spu'i sgo nas 'gyed pa mdzad/ /'od gzer sgo la pad mo yid 'ong gnas/ /khyod kyi sprul pa 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal sel/ /spos kyi na bun sprin du chags pa 'gyed/ /'gro ba'i gzugs su gnas te kun nas
5b7(phal chen): mdzes/ /me tog sgo rnams kun nas dgyes mdzad pas/ /chos dbyings bzhugs pa'i rgyal ba kun tu khyab/ /khyod kyi phrag pa'i lhun yangs 'phags pa ni/ /rin chen 'od 'phro ri bo ri rab 'dra/ /
5b8(phal chen): dri med de ni 'gro ba kun tu gsal/ /gti mug mun nag rnam par bzlog pa mdzad/ /khyod kyi dri med zhal mdog bzang ba las/ /na bun sprin dang nyi ma yangs pa 'byung / /khyod kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor 'dra 'od
6a1(phal chen): bzang / rnam par snang mdzad spyod yul yangs pa 'byin/ khyod kyi spyan nas zla skar 'od 'byung ba/ /rtag tu dri med sprin ltar mang ba ste/ de dag phyogs bcur bkang zhing 'gro ba rnams/ /rab tu snang byed 'jig
6a2(phal chen): rten rab rib sel/ /khyod kyi mtshan las 'gro ba'i lus mnyam pa'i/ /sprul pa rgya mtsho phyogs su khyab par 'phro/ /da dag chos dbyings yangs par rgyas 'gengs shing / /sems can tshad med tshogs rnams yongs
6a3(phal chen): su 'dul/ /khyod kyi sku ni 'byam klas nga phyogs su snang / /'gro ba kun la mngon 'byung dga' ba bskyed/ /rgyal po mye dang rkun po chus bskyed pa'i/ /'jigs pa thams cad rnam sel zhi bar mdzad/ /gang tshe khyod kyi spyan
6a4(phal chen): sngar bdag btang nas/ /yon tan rnam par sems shing nyer phyin pa/ /de'i tshe 'od gzer dri med 'khor bzang ba/ /khyod kyi zhal gyi smin mtshams gseb nas 'thon/ /phyogs rnams rgya mtsho brgya mang snang mdzad nas/ /
6a5(phal chen): 'jig rten snang ba rgya che yongs bskyed de/ /rnam 'phrul rnam pa mang po rnam bstan nas/ /de tshe bdag gi lus kyi gseb tu zhi/ /gang tshe 'od kyi 'khor gyis bdag reg pa/ /de tshe bde ba rmad byung yangs pa myong / /gzungs dang
6a6(phal chen): ting 'dzin brgya mang yongs su gnon/ /phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba dpag yas mthong bar 'gyur/ /gom pa rnam bor gyen du bteg pa la 'ang / /rdul phran grangs snyed tshul ni bdag gis rig /rdul phran shin tu phra ba
6a7(phal chen): gcig la yang / /zhing gi rdul snyed zhing rnams mthong bar gyur/ /rdul la gnas kyang rnam pa tha gu ste/ /zhing mang brgya ni shin tu nyon yang mongs/ /de yi 'gro ba sdug bsngal nyams su myong / /cho nger ngu zhing smre sngags
6a8(phal chen): yongs su 'don/ /zhing mang la la kun nas nyon mongs dag /de na sdug bsngal mang zhing bde ba chung / /rgyal ba thugs rje can yang der skyes ste/ /rgyal ba'i nyan thos rang rgyal de bzhin no/ /zhing tshul la la yongs dag
6b1(phal chen): nyon mongs ste/ /byang chub sems dpa'i gnas bzangs mang pos brgyan/ /skyes pa bud med yongs brgyan blta na sdug /skyon med rgyal ba'i gdung yang rgyun mi 'chad/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho yangs shing dri myed pa/ /
6b2(phal chen): rdul la gnas shing mnyam pa'i gzhi dang ldan/ /de dag bskal pa brgya mang sngon gyi tshe/ /rnam par snang mdzad spyod mdzad yongs su mdzad/ /zhing rnams 'byam klas kun na rgyal ba dag /shing dbang dam pa'i drung
6b3(phal chen): du gshegs pa bstan/ /rnam par 'phrul zhing byang chub 'tshang yang rgya/ /chos kyi 'khor lo bskor cing 'dul ba ston/ /rnam par snang mdzad spyod yul yangs pa la/ /khyod kyang kun tu rjes su zhugs
6b4(phal chen): par mthong / /mchod pa stong phrag tshad med khrag khrig gis/ /rgyal ba kun la mngon par mchod mdzad do/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis tshigs su bcad pa de dag smras nas/ mtshan mo'i lha mo sems
6b5(phal chen): can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal la 'di skad ces smras so/ /lha mo byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa de/ de lta bu zab pa ni ngo mtshar che na/ rnam par thar pa de'i ming ni ci zhes bgyi/ de khyod kyis brnyes nas
6b6(phal chen): yun ni ji srid cig lags/ byang chub sems dpas ji ltar nan tan du bgyis na rnam par thar pa de yongasu dag par 'gyur/ smras pa rigs kyi bu gnas 'di ni lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten dang / nyan thos dang rang
6b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas su bcas pas yid ches par dka' ba ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa dang / smon lam khong du chud pa rnams kyi spyod yul te/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'
6b8(phal chen): snying rje chen po lhur len pa/ 'gro ba thams cad yongs su skyob pa la zhugs pa/ mi khom pa dang ngan song dang / ngan 'gro'i lam thams cad rnam par bzlog pa la zhugs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad sangs rgyas
7a1(phal chen): kyi zhing yongs su dag pa/ bla na med par bya ba la zhugs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rgyun mi gcod pa la zhugs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa yongasu
7a2(phal chen): gzung ba la zhugs pa/ bskal pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la gnas pas/ gnas par bya ba'i smon lam chen po rgya mtsho la zhugs pa/ chos rgya mtsho thams cad la sgrib pa med pa'i ye shes
7a3(phal chen): snang ba rnam par sbyang ba la zhugs pa/ skad cig re re zhing dus gsum gyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad du ye shes snang bas/ rnam par gnas pa rab tu thob pa rnams kyi yul te/ 'on kyang de bzhin gshegs
7a4(phal chen): pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis bstan par bya'o/ /rigs kyi bu sngon 'das pa'i dus bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed gcig gi pha rol tu 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par snang mdzad gzi brjid
7a5(phal chen): dpal zhes bya bar bskal pa rdul dang bral ba'i dkyil 'khor ces bya ba byung ste/ bskal pa de dag la sangs rgyas ri rab gyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed cig byung bar gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi khams rnam par snang
7a6(phal chen): mdzad gzi brjid dpal zhes bya ba de ni rin po che thams cad kyi sprin gyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa ste/ rdo rje las byas pa'i gzhal med khang dang / gnas kyis yongs su mdzes par byas pa'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams
7a7(phal chen): de'i gzhi ni rin po che'i rgyal po dri ma med pa'i 'od kyi rgya mtsho las blangs pa ste/ lhun dang lus ni nor bu rin po che'i spos thams cad kyi rgyal po las gyur pa'o/ /de ni dbyibs kun tu zlum pa ste/ rnam par dag
7a8(phal chen): cing kun nas nyon mongs pa/ lhab lhub thams cad kyi sprin gyi bla res kun nas khyab pa/ rin po che'i khor yug rgyan thams cad dang ldan pa/ rim pa stong gis yongs su bskor ba/ gling bzhi pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya
7b1(phal chen): phrag stong gis shin tu rgyas par brgyan pa ste/ de la gling bzhi pa la la ni kun nas nyon mongs pa ste/ sems can kun nas nyon mongs pa'i las dang ldan pa rnams kyi gnas so/ /la la ni kun nas
7b2(phal chen): nyon mongs shing rnam par dag pa ste/ sems can las 'dren ma dang ldan pa rnams kyi gnas so/ /la la ni rnam par dag cing kun nas nyon mongs pa ste/ sems can yongs su dag cing kun nas nyon mongs
7b3(phal chen): pa dge ba'i rtsa ba sbyangs pa/ kha na ma tho ba nyung ba rnams kyi gnas so/ /la la ni shin tu yongs su dag pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa' dag pa rnams kyi gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rnam par snang
7b4(phal chen): mdzad gzi brjid dpal zhes bya ba de'i shar phyogs kyi 'khor yug gi mtshams na gling bzhi pa'i rin po che'i me tog sgrol ma'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba rnam par dag cing kun nas nyon mongs pa/ ma rmos
7b5(phal chen): ma bskyed pa'i 'bras la yongs su spyod pa/ sngon gyi las kyi rnam par smin pas mngon par grub pa'i khang pa brtseg pa'i gnas dang / gzhal med khang la yongs su spyod pa/ 'khor kun nas yid bzhin gyi shing
7b6(phal chen): gis 'khor ba/ spos kyi shing sna tshogs kyi lhun las spos kyi sprin rgyun mi 'chad par 'byung ba/ phreng ba sna tshogs kyi shing las phreng ba'i sprin rgyun mi 'chad par 'byung ba/ me tog sna tshogs kyi shing las me
7b7(phal chen): t og kha dog dang dri bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sprin rgya mtsho rgyun mi 'chad par 'bab pa phye ma dang kha dog sna tshogs kyi shing gi lhun la spos rin po che'i rgyal po thams cad kyi phye ma'i char rgyun mi 'chad par 'bab pa
7b8(phal chen): rin po che'i shing sna tshogs las rin po che'i 'bru mang po 'bul ba'i kha dog snang bas shin tu snang bar byas pa/ lha rdzas kyi rol mo sna tshogs kyi shing las sil snyan sna tshogs kyi sprin rlung gis bskyod cing nam
8a1(phal chen): mkha'i dbyings las sgra dbyangs snyan pa 'byung ba/ nyin mtshan gyi bde ba nyi ma dang zla bas 'byung ba/ nor bu rin po che kun tu snang bas gzhi byas pa'i sa rab tu mnyam par gyur pa ste/ gling bzhi po der
8a2(phal chen): rgyal po'i pho brang bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong byung bar gyur te/ rgyal po'i pho brang de dag re re zhing yang chu klung stong gis yongs su bskor ba'o/ /chu klung de dag thams cad kyang lha rdzas kyi me tog sil mas gang ba'o/ /
8a3(phal chen): lha rdzas kyi rol mo dang glu'i sgra skad snyan cing yid du 'ong ba 'byin pa'o/ /chu 'gram rin po che'i shing yid du 'ong bas rnam par brgyan pa'o/ /rin po che sna tshogs kyi shin tu brgyan pa'i gru phan tshun rgyu ba'o/ /bde ba
8a4(phal chen): sna tshogs ci dga' bar yongs su spyad du yod pa'o/ /chu klung gi mtshams kyi gzhi re re dag na 'ang grong khyer bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag bcu kun nas gnas pa ste/ grong khyer de dag re re zhing yang grong brdal
8a5(phal chen): bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag stong gis yongs su bskor ba'o/ /grong dang grong khyer dang grong brdal de dag thams cad kyang lha rdzas kyi bza' shing gi ra ba dang / gzhal med khang dang / khang pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya
8a6(phal chen): phrag stong gi 'khor gyis yongs su bskor ba'o/ /gling bzhi pa'i de'i 'dzam bu'i gling gi dbus na rgyal po'i pho brang dbu ma rin po che'i me tog sgron ma zhes bya ba yod par gyur to/ /de ni bskyid cing longs spyod
8a7(phal chen): phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan la/ rtag du lo legs shing bde ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang ldan pa'o/ /lha dang mi mang pos yongasu gang ba'o/ /sems can dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam dang ldan pa rnams kyi gnas
8a8(phal chen): su gyur pa ste/ rgyal po'i pho brang rin po che'i me tog sgron ma zhes bya ba de na rgyal po rnam par snang ba rin chen pad mo dpal gyi gtsug phud snying po zhes bya ba 'khor los bsgyur ba/ gling bzhi la dbang ba pad mo'i
8b1(phal chen): snying po las rdzus te byung ba/ mi chen po'i mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis kyis lus shin tu brgyan pa chos dang ldan pa/ chos kyi rgyal po rin po che sna bdun dang ldan pa gnas par gyur to/ /de'i bu dpa' zhing rdul phod
8b2(phal chen): la yan lag dam pa'i gzugs dang ldan pa/ gzhan gyi 'khor rab tu 'joms pa/ rnam pa thams cad yongs su tshang ba'i yan lag dam pa dang ldan pa stong tshang bar byung ngo / /de'i btsun mo'i 'khor gyi
8b3(phal chen): bud med kyang bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag bcu yod par gyur to/ /de dag kun kyang 'khor los bsgyur ba'i bskal pa dang mnyam pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba las byung ba mthun par spyod pa rin po che'i rgyan rang 'khrungs
8b4(phal chen): su byung ba/ dge ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ lha'i bu mo dang khyad par med par 'dra ba'i gzugs can/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi kha dog dang ldan pa'i lus can/ lus kyi ba spu las lha rdzas kyi spos sna
8b5(phal chen): tshogs 'byung ba/ lus las lha rdzas kyi 'od dri zhim po dri ma med par rab tu 'gyed pa sha stag go/ /de'i blon po bye ba phrag bcu byung ste blon po rin po che la stsogs pa dag go/ /'khor los bsgyur ba'i
8b6(phal chen): rgyal po rnam par snang ba rin chen pad mo dpal gyi gtsug phud snying po de'i btsun mo dam pa bud med rin po che dpal gyi bzhin yongs su rgyas pa zhes bya ba gzugs mdzes shing sdug la/ blta na yid
8b7(phal chen): du 'ong ba kha dog bzang po shin tu rgyas pa'i dam pa dang ldan pa skra mthon ting du 'dug pa/ mig dkar nag 'byes pa/ mdog gser gyi kha dog du 'dug pa/ tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang ldan pa/ lus las
8b8(phal chen): 'od rtag tu 'byung ba/ 'khor kun tu dpag tshad stong gi tshad du 'od kha dog du ma dang ldan pa/ lha rdzas kyi dri zhim po can 'gyed pa byung ngo / /rgyal po'i btsun mo dpal gyi bzhin yongs su rgyas pa zhes bya ba de
9a1(phal chen): las bu mo pad mo bzang mo mig yid du 'ong ba'i dpal gyi zla ba zhes bya ba yan lag thams cad tshang ba/ gzugs mdzes shing sdug pa/ blta na yid du 'ong ba 'jig rten thams
9a2(phal chen): cad kyis blta na mi ngoms pa byung bar gyur te/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po la blta na su yang ngoms par mi 'gyur ba de bzhin du 'khor los bsgyur ba'i bu mo pad mo
9a3(phal chen): bzang mo'i mig yid du 'ong ba'i dpal de la blta bas kyang su yang ngoms par mi 'gyur te/ shes rab kyis yongs su ngoms par 'gyur ba ni ma gtogs so/ /de'i tshe de'i dus na/ sems can rnams kyang tshe dpag tu
9a4(phal chen): med par gyur te/ de la gcig tu nges pa med pas bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de'i dus na sems can rnams kyi dbyibs sna tshogs dang / kha dog sna tshogs dang / dbyangs sna tshogs dang / ming sna tshogs dang /
9a5(phal chen): rigs sna tshogs dang / tshe'i tshad sna tshogs dang / chu zheng rnam pa tha dad pa dang / mos pa dang stobs dang / brtson 'grus dang / mthu rnam pa tha dad pa dang / yid du 'ong ba dang yid du mi 'ong ba rnam pa tha dad pa dang /
9a6(phal chen): yangs pa dang dma' ba la mos pa sna tshogs kyang yod par gyur te/ de la sems can ji snyed cig mdog bzang ba dang / yangs pa la mos pa dang / yan lag tshang ba dang / blta na sdug cing yid du 'ong bar gyur
9a7(phal chen): pa de dag ni 'di skad ces 'dzer te/ kye mi dag nga ni kha dog med pas ches bzang ngo zhes zer ro/ /de bzhin du sems can ji snyed cig lus kyi dbyibs legs pa dang ldan par gyur pa de dag kyang / sems can
9a8(phal chen): lus kyi dbyibs mi sdug par 'gyur ba rnams la rlom zhing khyad du gsod do/ /de dag de ltar gcig la gcig khyad du gsod pa las byung ba'i mi dge ba'i rtsa bas tshe'i tshad las kyang yongs su bri bar gyur te/
9b1(phal chen): kha dog dang stobs dang bde ba las kyang yongs su bri bar gyur to/ /rgyal po'i pho brang rin po che'i me tog sgron ma de'i byang phyogs logs na/ snying po byang chub kyi shing kun tu grags pa'i chos kyi sprin sgra'i rgyal mtshan
9b2(phal chen): zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po byang chub kyi rgyan skad cig re re la yongs su ston nas/ rtsa ba rin po che'i rgyal po rdo rje ltar sra zhing mi 'jig pa/ nor bu rin po che thams cad las grub pas lhun
9b3(phal chen): shin tu yangs shing rgyas pa/ sdong po dang yal ga dang lo ma dang / mdab ma dang me tog dang / 'bras bu rin po che thams cad gyi rgyu las grub pa/ kun tu cha mnyam par bkod cing / kun tu khyab pa'i yan lag dang
9b4(phal chen): ldan pa/ rgyan kun tu rgyas par 'gengs shing mi zad pa dang ldan pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi 'od 'phro ba dang / 'od gzer kun tu snang bar 'gyed pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul rnam par
9b5(phal chen): 'phrul pa'i dbyangs rjes su sgrog pa yod de/ snying po byang chub de'i mdun rol na/ spos chu'i mtsho rin po che'i me tog dang / klog dang chos kyi 'brug sgra'i sprin gyi dbyangs shes bya ba yod de/ de ni rin po che'i
9b6(phal chen): shing bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas bskor ba/ rin po che'i shing de dag thams cad kyang byang chub kyi shing gi dbyibs su 'khod pa sha stag go/ /spos chu'i mtsho chen po rin po che'i me tog
9b7(phal chen): dang / glog dang chos kyi 'brug sgra'i sprin gyi dbyangs zhes bya ba de'i 'gram thams cad kyang nor bu rin po che thams cad bkram zhing rnam par bkod pa ste/ rin po che thams cad kyi phreng ba sna tshogs su dgrigs pa/
9b8(phal chen): rin po che rnam par dag pa las byas pa'i khang pa sna tshogs kyi rgyan gyis yongs su brgyan pa'o/ /rgyan rnam par dag pa sna tshogs kyi rgyan gyis shin tu brgyan pa'o/ /snying po byang chub de'i 'khor thams
10a1(phal chen): cad kyang nor bu rin po che'i khang pa brtsegs pa chen po bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa/ pad ma'i snying po can sha stag gis yongs su 'khor ba/ spos chu'i mtsho chen po rin po che'i me tog
10a2(phal chen): dang glog dang chos kyi 'brug sgra'i sprin gyi dbyangs zhes bya ba de'i dbus nas/ pad mo'i rgyal po lo ma'i mtshams nas dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul rnam par ston pa'i 'od gzer
10a3(phal chen): gyi sprin gyi rgyan ces bya ba byung bar gyur te/ pad mo chen po de la de bzhin gshegs pa ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed de dag gi nang nas bskal pa'i thog ma pa de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes rin po che'i 'od kun
10a4(phal chen): tu 'phro ba'i dpal ston gyi rgyal po zhes bya bar byung bar gyur te/ de ni bskal pa de la de dag thams cad kyi thog mar bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/
10a5(phal chen): des lo stong phrag du ma zhig du chos bstan pas/ sems can yongs su smin par mdzad nas/ lo stong phrag bcur 'od gzer snang ba'i rnam par 'phrul pas yongs su smin par mdzad do/ /de bzhin
10a6(phal chen): gshegs pa lo stong phrag bcu na 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /zhes bya ba'i tshe pad mo'i rgyal po chen po lo ma'i mtshams nas/ du gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul rnam par ston pa'i 'od
10a7(phal chen): gzer gyi sprin gyi rgyan ces bya ba de las sems can thams cad rdul dang 'byed pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba'i 'od gzer byung bar gyur te/ 'od des phog pa'i sems can rnams kyis kyang lo stong phrag bcu na de
10a8(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes bya bar shes so/ /lo stong phrag dgu na de bzhin gshegs pa de 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tshe/ byang chub kyi shing de las rdul dang bral ba'i dpal gyi
10b1(phal chen): snying po zhes bya ba'i 'od gzer byung ste/ 'od gzer des phog pa'i sems can de dag gis kyang gzugs thams cad shin tu phra bar mthong bar gyur to/ /lo stong phrag brgyad na de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ngo zhes
10b2(phal chen): bya ba'i tshe/ byang chub kyi shing chen po de nyid las 'od gzer sems can thams cad kyi las rnam par smin pa'i dbyings zhes bya ba byung ste/ des phog pa'i sems can de dag thams cad kyis kyang rang rang gi
10b3(phal chen): las rgya mtsho khong du chud par 'gyur te/ las dran pa'i ye shes kyang thob par gyur to/ /lo stong phrag bdun na de bzhin gshegs pa de 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tshe/ byang chub kyi shing de nyid las 'od gzer
10b4(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yang dag par 'byung ba'i dbyangs zhes bya ba byung ste/ 'od gzer des sems can de dag la phog nas dbang po nyams pa med cing yongs su tshang bar gyur to/ /lo stong phrag drug na de
10b5(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tshe/ byang chub kyi shing chen po de nyid las 'od gzer sangs rgyas kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba byung ste/ des sems can de dag
10b6(phal chen): la phog nas bsam pa rgya chen pos rnam par 'phrul bar gyur to/ /lo stong phrag lnga na de bzhin gshegs pa de 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tshe/ byang chub kyi shing chen po de nyid las 'od gzer sangs rgyas
10b7(phal chen): kyi zhing thams cad yongasu dag par sgra 'byin pa'i gzugs brnyan rnam par dmigs pa zhes bya ba byung ste/ des sems can de dag la phog nas sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam pa thams cad du yongs su dag par
10b8(phal chen): mthong bar gyur to/ /lo stong phrag bzhi na de bzhin gshegs pa de 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tshe/ byang chub kyi shing chen po de nyid las 'od gzer de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul tha mi dad
11a1(phal chen): pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba 'byung ste/ des sems can de dag la phog nas de bzhin gshegs pa de'i rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad du song ba la zhugs par gyur to/ /lo stong phrag gsum na de bzhin
11a2(phal chen): gshegs pa de 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tshe/ byang chub kyi shing chen po de las 'od gzer 'gro ba thams cad la mngon tu gyur pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba byung ste/ des sems can de dag la phog nas de bzhin
11a3(phal chen): gshegs pa de yang mngon tu mos pas mthong bar gyur to/ /lo stong phrag gnyis na de bzhin gshegs pa de 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tshe/ byang chub kyi shing chen po de las 'od gzer dus gsum
11a4(phal chen): gyi ye shes kyi glog gi sgron ma zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngon gyi tshul rab tu sgrog pa byung ste/ des sems can de dag la reg nas de bzhin gshegs pa de'i sngon gyi tshul rgya mtsho la rtog
11a5(phal chen): cing 'jug par gyur to/ /lo stong na de bzhin gshegs pa de 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tshe/ byang chub kyi shing chen po de las 'od gzer ye shes rab rib med pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgron
11a6(phal chen): ma zhes bya ba byung ste/ des sems can de dag la phog nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zhing thams cad dang / sems can thams cad kyis mthong bar 'gyur ba'i
11a7(phal chen): mig kun tu lta ba thob par gyur to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de lo brgya na 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tshe/ byang chub kyi shing chen po de nyid las 'od gzer 'gro ba thams cad kyis sangs rgyas mthong
11a8(phal chen): ba rnam par smin pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba las byung ba zhes bya ba byung ste/ des sems can de dag la phog nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa skye ba'i 'du shes thob par gyur to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de zhag
11b1(phal chen): bdun na skye bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tshe/ byang chub kyi shing chen po de nyid las 'od zer sems can thams cad rab tu dga' ba dang / spro ba dang mos pa yongs su 'byung ba'i dbyangs shes bya ba byung ste/ des
11b2(phal chen): sems can de dag la phog nas sangs rgyas mthong bar 'gyur ba'i dga' ba'i shugs chen po skyes par gyur to/ /rigs kyi bu de ltar 'od zer gyi yongasu smin par bya ba'i tshul tshad med pa rnam pa de lta
11b3(phal chen): bus lo stong du sems can rnams yongs su smyin par mdzad nas zhag bdun pa la thug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams de thams cad yongs su ba spyod pa'i tshul tshad med pas yongs su bskyod nas shin tu
11b4(phal chen): dag par byin gyi brlabs so/ /phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa ji snyed pa rgyan bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnam pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa de dag thams cad kyang
11b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sems kyi skad cig re re la yongs su bstan par gyur to/ /de nas zhag bdun pa tha ma la bab pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams de na sems can sangs rgyas mthong bar 'gyur ba yongs su smin
11b6(phal chen): pa de dag thams cad snying po byang chub tu mngon par gzhol bar gyur to/ /de nas 'jig rten gyi khams de'i 'khor yug thams cad dang / ri rab thams cad dang / ri thams cad dang / chu klung thams cad dang /
11b7(phal chen): rgya mtsho thams cad dang shing thams cad dang / sa'i gzhi thams cad dang / grong khyer thams cad dang / ra ba thams cad dang / gnas thams cad dang / gzhal med khang thams cad dang / gos dang rgyan dang longs spyod thams cad dang / rol
11b8(phal chen): mo'i shing thams cad dang / rol mo bdung ba'i dbyangs thams cad dang / sprul pa'i rgyan thams cad kyi dmigs pa re re las kyang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul dang / mthu'i sgra rab tu sgrog pa'i spos
12a1(phal chen): dang / bdug spos thams cad kyi sprin mngon par 'thon te/ rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba'i sprin dang / spos dang bdug spos thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba dam pa dang / spos rin po che thams cad kyi gzugs kyi sprin dang /
12a2(phal chen): gos rin po che dang / rgyan rin po che thams cad kyi sprin dang / rin po che'i me tog sna tshogs kyi ri rab kyi sprin dang phye ma sna tshogs kyi sprin mang po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od gzer gyi sprin rnam par ston
12a3(phal chen): pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin rab tu 'gyed pa/ rol mo brdung ba dang / dkrol ba thams cad kyi sprin yongs su 'khrol zhing rdung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi smon
12a4(phal chen): lam gyi sgra skad kyi sprin rab tu 'byin pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / gsung rgya mtsho'i sprin rab tu sgrog pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mtshan dang dpe byad bzang
12a5(phal chen): po'i gzugs brnyan sna tshogs kyi sprin rab tu ston par byed cing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ltas sngon du byung ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongasu ston te/ rin po che'i rgyal po'i pad mo chen po'i lo ma'i
12a6(phal chen): mtshams nas/ dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul rnam par ston pa'i 'od gzer gyi sprin gyi rgyan de'i pad mo'i 'khor rin po che'i rgyal po las byas pa chen po sha stag tu byas te 'khod do/ /
12a7(phal chen): rin po che'i rgyal po'i pad mo chen po'i 'khor kyi rin po che'i pad mo chen po de dag gi ze ba dang / snying po la seng ge'i khri rin po che'i pad mo chen po'i snying po can/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
12a8(phal chen): dag byung bar gyur te/ rin po che'i snying po can gyi khri de dag la 'ang byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed skyil mo krung bcas te/ 'khod par gyur to/ /bcom ldan 'das ye shes
12b1(phal chen): rin po che'i 'od kun tu 'phro ba'i dpal yon tan dpal gyi rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa de bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas ma thag tu de'i mod la/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi
12b2(phal chen): khams su de bzhin gshegs pa mang po dag kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas te/ sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du mngon sum du chos kyi 'khor lo
12b3(phal chen): bskor bar gyur to/ /de nas kyang 'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi sems can tshad med pa rnams ngan song dang log par ltung ba thams cad las rnam par bzlog go/ /sems can tshad med pa ni mtho ris su skye ba
12b4(phal chen): la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni nyan thos la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni rang sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu yongs su smin par byas so/ /sems can tshad med pa ni shugs drag po'i
12b5(phal chen): 'od kyis 'byung ba'i byang chub tu yongs su smin par byas so/ /sems can tshad med pa ni brtson 'grus dri ma med pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi byang chub tu yongs su smin par byas so/ /sems can tshad med pa ni chos
12b6(phal chen): rab tu bsgom pa'i gnas su 'byung ba'i byang chub la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni dbang po yongs su dag pa rab tu bsgoms pas 'byung ba'i byang chub tu yongs su smin par byas so/ /sems can
12b7(phal chen): tshad med pa ni stobs mnyam pa nyid la yang dag par spyod pa khong du chud pas 'byung ba'i byang chub tu yongs su smin par byas so/ /sems can tshad med pa ni chos kyi grong khyer mngon du 'gyur ba'i yul gyi theg pa
12b8(phal chen): skye bas 'byung ba'i byang chub la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni thams cad du rjes su song ba'i rdzu 'phrul tha mi dad pa'i tshul gyi theg pas 'byung ba'i byang chub la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can
13a1(phal chen): tshad med pa ni spyod pa'i sbyor ba la yang dag par gzhol ba'i tshul gyis 'byung ba'i byang chub la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni ting nge 'dzin gyis 'jug pa'i tshul gyis 'byung ba'i byang chub la
13a2(phal chen): rab tu bkod do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni dmigs pa'i yul thams cad yongs su dag pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi tshul gyis 'byung ba'i byang chub la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i
13a3(phal chen): byang chub tu sems bskyed do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i lam la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni pha rol tu phyin pa'i lam rnam par dag pa la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can
13a4(phal chen): tshad med pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang po la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa gnyis pa dang / gsum pa dang bzhi pa dang lnga pa dang / drug pa dang bdun pa dang / brgyad pa dang
13a5(phal chen): dgu pa la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu pa la rab tu bkod do/ /sems can tshad med pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa smon lam gyi khyad par can la btsud do/ /
13a6(phal chen): sems can tshad med pa ni byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa dang / smon lam rnam par bkod pa la rab tu bkod do/ /de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa des sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang /
13a7(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas sems kyi skad cig re re la sems can gyi khams mtha' dang dbus med pa rnam par 'dul bar gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi khams de'i
13a8(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyis kyang de bzhin gshegs pa de'i sku sna tshogs dang / thabs mkhas pa sna tshogs kyis bsgrubs pa'i chos bstan pa yongs su shes par gyur te/ rgyal po'i pho brang rin po che'i
13b1(phal chen): me tog sgron ma'i sems can gzugs dang / kha dog dang yul dang longs spyod gyis rgyags shing dregs te gcig la gcig khyad du gsod pa de rnams gdul ba'i don du byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang
13b2(phal chen): pos kha dog dang gzugs mchog tu phyin par mngon par sprul te/ rgyal po'i pho brang der phyin to/ /de'i 'od shin tu yangs pas rgyal po'i gnas de dag thams cad du yongs su snang bar gyur te/ rgyal po'i gnas
13b3(phal chen): de'i 'od dang / 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rnam par snang ba rin chen pad mo'i dpal gyi gtsug phud snying po'i lus las byung ba'i 'od dang / bud med rin po che'i 'od dang / rin po che'i shing gi 'od dang /
13b4(phal chen): nor bu rin po che chen po'i 'od dang / nyi zla dang gza' skar dang rgyun skar gyi 'od dang / 'dzam bu'i gling na 'od ji snyed cig yod pa de dag thams cad kyang mi snang bar gyur te/ dper na nyi ma shar te mun pa dang bral
13b5(phal chen): pa dang / zla ba dang gza' skar dang / rgyu skar gyi 'od kyang mi snang la me dang nor bu'i 'od kyang mi snang ngo / /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos zil gyis non nas 'dzam bu'i gling de na 'od yod pa
13b6(phal chen): thams cad kyang mi snang bar gyur to/ /'di lta ste dper na/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi sa le sbram gyi drung du snag tsa'i gzugs bzhag na mdzes par mi rung / lhang nger mi rung / lham mer mi rung / lhang nger mi
13b7(phal chen): rung ngo / /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po'i mdun du sems can de dag gi gzugs kyi lus kyang mdzes par mi rung / lhag ger mi rung / lham mer mi rung / lhang nger mi rung ngo / /de nas
13b8(phal chen): de dag 'di snyam du gyur te/ de lta su zhig de ltar de'i drung du bdag cag gi lus sam/ 'od dam kha dog gam/ gzi brjid kyis kyang mdzes par mi rung / lhag ger ma rung / lham mer mi rung / lhang nger mi rung ba de
14a1(phal chen): lta lha 'am/ tshangs pa 'am/ ci zhig de'i mtshams ni gzung bar mi nus so snyam mo/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos rgyal po'i gnas rin po che'i me tog sgron ma'i dbus 'khor
14a2(phal chen): los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rnam par snang ba rin chen pad mo dpal gyi gtsug phud snying po'i gzhal med khang gi steng gi bar snang la 'dug ste/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rnam par snang ba pad mo dpal gyi
14a3(phal chen): gtsug phud snying po la 'di skad ces smras so/ /rgyal po chen po shes par gyis shig /de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'jig rten du byung ste/ khyod kyi khams 'di
14a4(phal chen): nyid kyi snying po byang chub chos kun tu snang ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi sgra dbyangs rgyal mtshan 'di nyid na rnam par spyod do zhes pa dang / rgyal po'i bu mo ye shes kyi 'od kun tu 'phro ba pad mo bzang po mig yid du
14a5(phal chen): 'ong ba'i dpal gyi zla bas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i gzugs kyi lus dang / 'od rnam par 'phrul pa dang rgyan mthong ste/ dbyangs thos nas dga' ba dang / mos pa'i shugs chen po skyes
14a6(phal chen): te/ de'i tshe sems 'di snyam du bskyed do/ /bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba gang ci bstsags pa des bdag kyang lus 'di 'dra bar thob par shog shig /rgyan 'di 'dra ba dang / mtshan 'di 'dra ba dang / spyod lam 'di
14a7(phal chen): 'dra ba dang / rdzu 'phrul 'di 'dra bar shog shig /ji ltar 'dis mtshan mo mun nag gi nang na sems can rnams la snang ba chen po bskyed de/ sangs rgyas skye ba yongs su brjod pa de bzhin du/ bdag gis
14a8(phal chen): kyang sems can rnams kyi mi shes pa'i mun pa bstsal de ye shes chen po'i snang ba bskyed par bya'o/ /gang dang gang du skyes pa thams cad du 'ang dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'di dang mi 'bral bar shog shig /
14b1(phal chen): de nas rigs kyi bu 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po rnam par snang ba rin chen pad mo dpal gyi gtsug phud snying po yan lag bzhi'i dpung gi tshogs dang lhan cig /rin po che bdun dang lhan cig /bud med kyi tshogs
14b2(phal chen): kyi 'khor dang lhan cig / bu dang blon po dang / ljongs kyi mi dang lhan cig tu rgyal po'i rdzu 'phrul chen po dang / rgyal po'i mthu chen pos rgyal po'i gnas rin po che'i me tog sgron ma de nas 'phags te gyen tu nam
14b3(phal chen): mkha' la dpag tshad gcig tsam du mngon par 'phags nas/ 'dzam bu'i gling thams cad dang / gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang ba chen pos rgyas par bkang ste/ sems can thams
14b4(phal chen): c ad sangs rgyas blta ba la yongs su bskul ba'i don du rin po che'i ri thams cad la gzugs brnyan mngon par bstan cing gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams su gtogs pa'i sems can rnams la
14b5(phal chen): mngon sum du gnas te sangs rgyas la blta ba de tshigs su bcad de glu'i dbyangs kyis bsngags pa/ lus can thams cad skyabs mdzad pa'i/ /sangs rgyas 'jig rten byung bar gyur/ /'jig rten gtso
14b6(phal chen): bo de blta bar/ /kun kyang longs te 'dong bar gyis/ /lus can kun la phan don du/ /chos rab ston par gang mdzad pa'i/ /de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba ni/ /bskal pa bye ba'i brgya lam na'o/ /'jig
14b7(phal chen): rten phyin ci log gyur cing / /mi shes sgrib pas bsgribs gyur te/ /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal myong ba rnams/ /gzigs shing thugs rje che bskyed nas/ /sdug bsngal thams cad gzhil don du/ /
14b8(phal chen): sems can yongs su smin bya'i phyir/ /bskal pa bye ba grangs med du/ /byang chub spyod pa spyad pa mdzad/ /bskal pa mtha' yas mu med par/ /sangs rgyas byang chub mchog don du/ /zhabs dang phyag kyang
15a1(phal chen): yongs su btang / /spyan dang snyan dang dbu yang btang / /mthong zhing bsnyen bkur byas pa dang / /thos pa don yod 'gyur ba yin/ /'jig rten mgon po 'jig rten du/ /'byung ba bskal pa bye bar dkon/ /
15a2(phal chen): de ni byang chub gdan la bzhugs/ /gsung ba'i dam pa ltar yang yod/ /bdud rnams sde dang bcas btul te/ /byang chub mchog tu rnam sangs rgyas/ /'od zer dkyil 'khor mtha' yas pa/ /sangs rgyas sku
15a3(phal chen): las mngon bkye zhing / /'gro ba tshim par mdzad pa yi/ /kha dog snang tshogs 'di la ltos/ /'od zer sprin mang grangs med pa/ /sangs rgyas sku las 'thon pa rnams/ /des ni sems can snang gyur na/ /
15a4(phal chen): bde ba dpe med 'thob par 'gyur/ /brtson 'grus chen po rab rtsom ste/ /rang dang rang gi bsam pa yis/ /mgon po de la mchod pa bgyis/ /tshur shog de yi gan du 'dong / /de nas rgyal po rnam par snang ba
15a5(phal chen): rin chen pad mo dpal gyi gtsug phud snying pos tshigs su bcad pa de dag gi bdag gi khams na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad yongs su bskul te/ mchod pa'i sprin sna tshogs brgya stong phrag bcu 'khor
15a6(phal chen): los bsgyur ba'i dge ba'i rtsa bas yongs su grub pa'i char pa/ snying po byang chub kun nas ldang ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi dbyangs kyi rgyal mtshan gyi 'khor kun tu mngon par 'bebs shing / rin po che'i gdugs kyi
15a7(phal chen): sprin gyi nam mkha' kun nas g.yogs par bya ba dang / me tog thams cad kyi bla re'i sprin gyis nam mkha' nas kheb par bya ba dang / na bza' sna tshogs kyi sprin gyis nam mkha' kun nas yog cing brgyan par bya ba dang /
15a8(phal chen): rin po che sna tshogs kyi dril bu'i dra ba'i sprin gyis nam mkha'i dbyings brgyan par bya ba dang / spos sna tshogs rgya mtshos dri zhim par byas pa'i 'od zer gyi sprin gyi rgyan namakha'i dbyings la byin gyis brlabs par
15b1(phal chen): bya ba dang / rin po che thams cad kyi khri la rin po che'i gdan 'brel bar bting ba'i sprin gyi rgyan nam mkha'i dbyings la byin gyis brlab pa dang / rin po che thams cad kyi rgyal mtshan gyi sprin mngon par bsgreng ba'i rgyan nam
15b2(phal chen): mkha'i dbyings la byin gyis brlabs pa dang / khang pa dang gzhal med khang thams cad kyi sprin gyis kun nas yog pa'i rgyan nam mkha'i dbyings la byin gyis brlab pa dang / me tog sna tshogs kyis kun nas
15b3(phal chen): yog pa'i rgyan nam mkha'i dbyings la byin gyis brlabs pa dang / mchod pa'i rgyan thams cad kyi sprin gyi char rab tu 'bab pa'i rgyan namakha'i dbyings la byin gyi brlab pa byed cing / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
15b4(phal chen): pa ye shes rin po che'i 'od kun tu 'phro ba'i dpal gyi rgyal po gang na ba der song ste/ phyin nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes rin po che'i 'od kun tu 'phro ba'i yon tan dpal gyi rgyal po'i zhabs
15b5(phal chen): gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar stan nor bu rin po che chen po'i phyogs kun tu rnam par snang
15b6(phal chen): ba'i pad mo'i snying po can la 'dug go/ /de nas 'khor los bsgyur ba'i bu mo ye shes rin po che'i 'od kun tu 'phro ba'i pad mo bzang mo mig yid du 'ong ba'i dpal gyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi lus las rgyan
15b7(phal chen): bkrol te/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes kyi 'od kun tu 'phro ba'i dpal yon tan dpal gyi rgyal po la gtor to/ mngon par gtor to/ /de nas rgyan de dag bcom ldan 'das de'i dbu'i
15b8(phal chen): g tsug gi steng gi bar snang la nor bu rin po che'i rgyan gyi gdugs chen po nor bu rin po che sna tshogs kyi dra bas yongs su bskor klu'i dbang po'i lus kyis gzung ba rgyan thams cad kyis lus kyi dbyibs shin tu
16a1(phal chen): legs par kun nas bskor ba/ rgyan gyi gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor bcus yongs su bskor ba/ shin tu dag pa khang pa brtsegs pa'i dbyibs sna tshogs kyis rgyan pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi lhab
16a2(phal chen): lhub kyi sprin gyi kun nas yog pa/ nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po thams cad kyi shing gi rgyan gyis kun nas khebs pa/ nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po spos thams cad kyi rgya mtshos yongs su brgyan par 'dug par gyur te/
16a3(phal chen): de'i dbus na byang chub kyi shing chen po chos kyi dbyings las byung ba'i rin po che thams cad kyi yan lag dang / lhun du ldan pa zhes bya bas rgyan pa'i mdzod mtha' dang dbus med pa skad cig re re zhing rgyan sna tshogs
16a4(phal chen): yongs su ston pa yod pa mthong bar gyur to/ /de'i drung na de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad ces bya ba byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kun kyang byang
16a5(phal chen): chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa dang / smon lam gyis byung ba byang chub sems dpa'i rgyan sna tshogs tha mi dad cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa la rnam par spyod pa sha stag gis bskor cing mdun du byas
16a6(phal chen): pa dang / 'jig rten gyi dbang po thams cad kyang de la mngon tu gyur pa mthong ngo / /bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad de'i sangs rgyas kyis rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' dang dbus med pa yang mthong bar gyur to/ /
16a7(phal chen): sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bskal pa gcig nas gcig tu rgyud pa la 'ang zhugs par gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi khams de'i 'du ba dang 'jig pa'i bskal pa 'ang zhugs par gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi
16a8(phal chen): khams der 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rgyud gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa la 'ang zhugs par gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi khams de na byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po de bzhin gshegs pa thams
16b1(phal chen): cad kyi zhabs drung na sangs rgyas mchod pa la brtson par gnas pa yang mthong ngo / /sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya ba la mngon du gyur par yang mthong ngo / /byang chub
16b2(phal chen): sems dpa' thams cad kyang byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i lus la gzugs brnyan du gyur par 'khod cing bdag nyid kyang rjes su 'brang bar mthong ngo / /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
16b3(phal chen): kyi zhabs kyi drung du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi drung dang / sems can thams cad kyi gnas dang / 'jig rten gyi khams de dang de dag thams cad na 'ang byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i
16b4(phal chen): gzugs brnyan kun tu byung ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag re re na 'ang sangs rgyas kyi zhing rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams mtshams gyi rgyan dang bcas pa/ gzhi dang bcas pa dang / dbyibs
16b5(phal chen): dang bcas pa dang / lhun dang bcas pa dang / rgyan sna tshogs yongs su dag pa dang bcas pa/ rgyan sna tshogs kyi sprin gyis kun nas khebs pa rnam par bkod pa dang / mying dang grangs rnam pa sna tshogs dang
16b6(phal chen): ldan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rgyud sna tshogs las brjod pa dus gsum gyi tshul sna tshogs su gtogs pa dang / phyogs 'byam klas pa sna tshogs su 'du ba chos kyi dbyings 'byam klas pa sna tshogs
16b7(phal chen): kyi khongs su gtogs pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi sna tshogs su 'dus pa/ namakha'i dbyings sna tshogs la rnam par gnas pa/ snying po byang chub sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par
16b8(phal chen): 'phrul pa sna tshogs kyis byung ba sangs rgyas kyi seng ge'i gdan sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sna tshogs dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi
17a1(phal chen): dkyil 'khor gyi rgyud sna tshogs can/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i thabs mkhas pa sna tshogasu brjod pa dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i tshul sna tshogs can
17a2(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / gsung gi nga ro sna tshogs rab tu byung / skad sna tshogs rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa dang ldan pa dang / mdo sde'i sprin sna tshogs rjes su sgrog pa can dag kyang
17a3(phal chen): mthong bar gyur to/ /mthong nas de bas kyang dga' ba dang / mos pa'i shugs chen po thob par gyur te/ de de ltar dga' ba'i shugs chen po skyes par gyur pa la/ bcom ldan 'das ye shes rin po che'i 'od
17a4(phal chen): kun tu 'phro ba'i dpal yon tan dpal gyi rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bsgrags pa zhes bya ba'i mdo sde 'khor gyi mdo sde/ sangs rgyas
17a5(phal chen): kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang bcas pa yang dag par bstan te/ des mdo sde de thos par gyur nas/ ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo stong phrag bcu shin tu phra zhing reg na bde bar thob par gyur te/ de ni
17a6(phal chen): dper na ma'i mngal du rnam par shes pa zhugs par gyur ma thag pa lta bu dang 'di lta ste dper na/ sems can rnams kyi las mngon par bsgrubs pa lta bu dang / 'di lta ste dper na/ zhing bzang po dam
17a7(phal chen): pa'i sa bon btab nas ring por ma lon yang myu gu skye ba'i rgyur gyur pa ste lta bu ste/ de bzhin du ting nge 'dzin de dag kyang 'jam zhing yid du 'ong ba ste/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mngon du rnam
17a8(phal chen): par dmigs pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad du snang ba rjes su song ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / dus gsum gyi tshul thams cad la 'jug pa khong du chud pa zhes
17b1(phal chen): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo sgrog pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi smon lam rgya mtsho rnam par dmigs pa zhes bya ba'i
17b2(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin dang / 'khor ba thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyis gzir ba'i sems can 'byung ba'i nga ro rab tu bsgrags pas rnam par dmyigs par byed pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / sems can
17b3(phal chen): thams cad kyi mun nag rnam par sel ba'i smon lam gyi rgyan ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / sems can thams cad sdug bsngal dang bral ba'i smon lam gyis rnam par dmigs pa zhes bya ba'i
17b4(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin dang / sems can thams cad kyi bde ba 'grub pa yongs su 'byin pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / 'dul bas mi skyo ba'i snying po zhes
17b5(phal chen): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi lam la 'jug pa'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa thams cad yongs su gnon par bsgrub pa'i
17b6(phal chen): rgyan ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / de dag la stsogs pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo stong phrag bcu rnams des thob par gyur to/ /de phra ba la mnyam par bzhag pa'i sems dang / mi g.yo ba'i sems dang /
17b7(phal chen): rab tu dga' ba'i sems dang / dbugs phyin pa'i sems dang / dpag tu med pa'i sems dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rjes su 'brang ba'i sems dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid shin tu zab pa la
17b8(phal chen): dmigs pa'i sems dang / byams pa'i rjes su 'gro ba'i tshul rgya mtsho la zhugs pa'i sems dang / mngon par zhen pa thams cad las gyen du 'phags pa'i sems dang / 'jig rten gyi yul thams
18a1(phal chen): cad la de mi gnas pa'i sems dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul la 'jug pa'i sems dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gzugs dang / kha dog rgya mtshos snang bar gyur pa'i sems dang /
18a2(phal chen): 'khrug pa med pa'i sems dang / g.yo ba med pa'i sems dang / khong khro ba med pa'i sems dang / mthon dman med pa'i sems dang / mi skyo ba'i sems dang / mi zlog pa'i sems dang / zhum pa med
18a3(phal chen): pa'i sems dang / chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin nges par rtogs pa'i sems dang / chos thams cad kyi tshul rgya mtsho'i rjes su song ba'i sems dang / chos thams cad rab tu 'byed pa'i tshul gyi
18a4(phal chen): rjes su song ba'i sems dang / sems can rgya mtsho thams cad la 'jug pa'i sems dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongs su skyob pa'i sems dang / sangs rgyas rgya mtsho mang po'i snang ba yongs su
18a5(phal chen): skyes pa'i sems dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi smon lam rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i sems dang / sgrib pa thams cad kyi ri rnam par 'thor ba'i sems dang / bsod nams kyi tshogs rgya chen po
18a6(phal chen): yang dag par bsgrub pa'i sems dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la spobs pa mngon sum du gyur pa'i sems dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yul thams cad la snang ba thob pa'i sems dang / byang
18a7(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i tshogs thams cad 'phel bar byed pa'i sems dang / phyogs rgya mtsho thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa'i sems dang ldan pas kun tu bzang po'i smon lam chen po la lhag par
18a8(phal chen): dmyigs par bya bas smon lam rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngon gyi smon lam rang gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par bya ba'i
18b1(phal chen): don du mngon par bsgrub ste/ 'di ltar sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings 'byam klas pa yongs su shes par bya ba dang / chos kyi
18b2(phal chen): dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho la 'jug par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du phyi ma'i bskal par byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyad par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor
18b3(phal chen): thams cad la phyi ma'i mtha' bskal par gnas par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi drung du 'gro bar bya ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad bsnyen bkur ba dang / de bzhin
18b4(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad la mchod cing rim gror bya ba yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / sems kyi skad cig re re la thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes rnam par bsgrub pa dang / rnam par 'tshang rgya
18b5(phal chen): bar bya bas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgyun mi gcod par bya ba'i phyir/ de dag la stsogs pa smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa'i sgo rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi byang chub
18b6(phal chen): sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa la smon lam mngon par bsgrub par gyur to/ /de'i byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa dang / smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa'i phyir/ bcom ldan
18b7(phal chen): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes rin po che'i 'od kun tu 'phro ba'i dpal yon tan dpal gyi rgyal pos sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bskul ba mdzad do/ /rab tu bstan pa mdzad do/ /yongs su
18b8(phal chen): bstan pa mdzad do/ /rnam par dbye ba mdzad do/ /rnam par dgrol ba mdzad do/ /yang dag par bstan par mdzad do/ /chud za bar mi 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir rab tu bstan par mdzad do/ /rgya chen por khyab par bya ba'i
19a1(phal chen): phyir shin tu yangs par mdzad do/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid lhur len par bya ba'i phyir rab tu gnas par mdzad do/ de ni 'di lta ste/ thog ma sems bskyed pa nas nye bar bzung ba phyin cad de bzhin
19a2(phal chen): gshegs pa'i sngon gyi smon lam rgya mtsho grangs med pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir ro/ /rigs kyi bu sngon 'das pa'i dus de'i yang pha rol gyi bskal pa bcu pa la 'jig rten gyi khams rin chen nyi ma'i 'khor
19a3(phal chen): lo rnam par snang ba'i 'od ces bya bar de bzhin gshegs pa zla ba'i rgyal mtshan dpal gyi gsung rab la bu mo ye shes kyi 'od kun tu 'phro ba pad mo bzang mo mig yid du 'ong ba'i dpal gyi zla ba de/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yongs su bskul to/
19a4(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs pad mo la bzhugs pa zhig bcos so/ /bcos nas kyang ri mo bris so/ /ri mo bris nas kyang rin po
19a5(phal chen): ches shin tu brgyan to/ /dge ba'i bshes gnyen byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la brten te/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu 'ang sems bskyed do/ /dge ba'i rtsa ba des log par mi
19a6(phal chen): ltung ba'i chos can du gyur to/ /rtag tu lha'i dbang po'i rigs dang mi'i dbang po'i rigasu skyes par gyur to/ /thams cad du yang gzugs mdzes shing sdug la blta na yid du 'ong ba dang / kha dog bzang po shin tu
19a7(phal chen): rgyas pa dam pa dang ldan par gyur te/ rtag tu de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po dang yang bral bar ma gyur to/ /dge ba'i bshes gnyen de nyid kyis tshe rabs de dag du yongasu
19a8(phal chen): smin par byas so/ /dran par byas so/ /de yang des byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po yongs su bsnyen bkur te/ yid 'byung bar ma byas so/ /rigs kyi bu de la ji snyam du sems/ de'i tshe de'i dus na
19b1(phal chen): 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rnam par snang ba rin chen pad mo dpal gyi gtsug phud snying po zhes bya ba de gzhan zhig yin snyam du sems na ni/ rigs kyi bu khyod kyis de ltar mi blta ste/ byang chub sems
19b2(phal chen): dpa' byams pa ni/ de'i tshe de'i dus na 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rnam par snang ba rin chen pad mo dpal gyi gtsug phud snying po zhes bya bar gyur to/ /rigs kyi bu de'i tshe de'i dus na rgyal po'i
19b3(phal chen): btsun mo'i dpal gyi bzhin yongs su rgyas pa zhes bya ba byung ba de/ gzhan zhig yin snyam du sems na yang de ltar mi blta ste/ mtshan mo'i lha mo kho mo'i drung na 'dug pa sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang
19b4(phal chen): ldan pa 'di yin no/ /rig kyi bu de la ji snyam du sems/ de'i tshe de'i dus na rgyal po'i bu mo ye shes kyi 'od kun tu 'phro ba/ pad mo bzang mo mig yid du 'ong ba'i dpal gyi zla ba zhes bya ba de gzhan zhig yin
19b5(phal chen): snyam du sems na ni de ltar mi blta ste/ kho mo ni de'i tshe de'i dus na rgyal po'i bu mo ye shes kyi 'od kun tu 'phro ba/ pad mo bzang mo mig yid du 'ong ba'i dpal gyi zla ba zhes bya bar gyur to/ /kho mo bu mo gzhon nur
19b6(phal chen): gyur to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa dbang po'i rgyal mtshan dpal gyi gsung rab la de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku pad mo la bzhugs pa bcos pa de ni kho mo'i bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi rgyur gyur to/ /
19b7(phal chen): de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos/ kho mo bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bskul ba de ni/ kho mos byang chub tu sems dang po bskyed pa yin no/ /kho mos bcom ldan
19b8(phal chen): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes rin po che'i 'od kun tu 'phro ba'i dpal yon tan dpal gyi rgyal po'i drung du phyin te/ rgyan gyis gtor nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul
20a1(phal chen): mthong bar gyur te/ kho mos bcom ldan 'das de'i drung nas chos thos par gyur pa de'i tshe/ kho mos byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa/ 'jig rten thams cad mngon du gyur pas 'gro
20a2(phal chen): ba rnam par 'dul ba ston pa 'di dag thob po/ /de bzhin gshegs pa ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dag thams cad kyang bsnyen bkur te/ yo byad dang mchod cing rim gror bya ba thams cad kyis kyang
20a3(phal chen): bkur stir byaso/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gis chos bstan pa de dag thams cad kyang kho mos thos te/ de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi gdams ngag dang rjes su bstan pa la 'ang zhugs par gyur to/ /
20a4(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa de dag la kho mos rim gro cher byas te/ rim gro de'i rnam pas sems kyi skad cig gcig la de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil
20a5(phal chen): 'khor de dag dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag thams cad kyang mthong ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par snang ba'i khams de ni 'das par gyur/ bskal pa rdul dang bral ba'i dkyil 'khor de ni
20a6(phal chen): mthar phyin par gyur nas/ de'i rjes la 'jig rten gyi khams ni rin chen 'khor lo sna tshogs kyis klubs shing brgyan pa zhes bya ba/ bskal pa ni 'od chen po zhes bya ba zhig byung ste/ de la sangs
20a7(phal chen): rgyas lnga brgya byung bar gyur to/ /de dag thams cad kyang kho mos bsnyen bkur te/ bskal pa 'od chen po de la de bzhin gshegs pa thugs rje chen po'i sprin gyi rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba bskal pa'i dang
20a8(phal chen): po las grub ste/ de mngon par byung ba'i tshe/ kho mo mtshan mo'i lha mor gyur pas mchod pa byas so/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje mthu bo che'i dpal zhes bya ba byung ste/ de la kho mo 'khor los bsgyur
20b1(phal chen): bar gyur pas mchod pa byas so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa des kho mo la mdo sde sangs rgyas thams cad skye zhing 'byung ba zhes bya ba/ mdo sde sangs rgyas kyis zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor
20b2(phal chen): dang bcas pa yang dag par bstan te/ de yang kho mos thos nas yongs su bzung ngo / /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa me'i 'od 'phro ba ri'i dpal gyis rnam par brgyan pa zhes bya ba byung ste de la kho mo tshong
20b3(phal chen): dpon gyi bu mor gyur pas mchod pa byas so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa des kho mo la mdo sde dus gsum snang ba'i snying po zhes bya ba/ mdo sde 'dzam bu'i gling gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor dang bcas pa yang
20b4(phal chen): dag par bstan te/ de yang kho mos thos nas yongs su bzung ngo / /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa chos rgya mtsho thams cad mngon par 'phags pa'i shugs kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba byung ste/ de la kho mo
20b5(phal chen): lha'i rgyal po gyur pas mchod pa byas so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa des kho mo la mdo sde chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi thams cad shes pa'i bye brag ces bya ba mdo sde lnga brgya'i 'khor dang bcas pa yang dag par
20b6(phal chen): bstan to/ de yang kho mos thos nas yongs su bzung ngo / /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa chos zab mo'i dpal rgya mtshos yang dag par 'byung ba'i 'od ces bya ba byung ste/ de la kho mo klu'i dbang po'i bu
20b7(phal chen): mor gyur pas/ nor bu rin po che yid bzhin gyi rgyal po'i sprin gyi char mngon par phab ste mchod pa byas so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa des kho mo la mdo sde dga' ba rgya mtsho rnam par 'phel ba'i shugs
20b8(phal chen): shes bya ba mdo sde bye ba brgya stong phrag bcu'i 'khor dang bcas pa yang dag par bstan te/ de yang kho mos thos nas yongs su bzung ngo / /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen ri bo'i spo'i
21a1(phal chen): 'od zer sgron ma zhes bya ba byung ste/ de la kho mo rgya mtsho'i lha mor gyur pas/ rin po che'i pad mo'i sprin gyi char gyis nye bar bsnyen te mchod pa byas so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa des kho mo
21a2(phal chen): la mdo sde chos dbyings rgya mtsho'i tshul zhes bya ba mdo sde sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor dang bcas pa yang dag par bstan te/ de'ang kho mos thos nas yongasu blangaso/ /dran pas yang
21a3(phal chen): dag par bzung ngo / /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa yon tan rgya mtsho snang ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi dpal zhes bya ba byung ste/ de la kho mo drang srong mngon par shes pa lnga dang ldan par gyur pa/ drang srong
21a4(phal chen): stong phrag drug bcus kun nas bskor bas rdzu 'phrul chen po'i rnam par 'phrul pa nye bar bstan te/ spos kyi me tog ri bo tsam gyi sprin gyi char mngon par phab ste/ mchod pa byas so/ /de bzhin gshegs
21a5(phal chen): pa des kho mo la mdo sde chos gnas med pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba mdo sde stong phrag bcu'i 'khor dang bcas pa bstan te/ de yang kho mos thos nas yongasu bzung ngo / /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs
21a6(phal chen): pa rnam par snang mdzad dpal gyi snying po zhes bya ba byung ste/ kho mo yang mnyam pa nyid kyi don 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i sa'i lha mo zhig tu gyur nas/ kho mo sa'i lha mo'i 'khor grangs med pa dang bcas
21a7(phal chen): pas rin po che'i shing thams cad kyi lhun las rin po che'i me tog gi sprin gyi char mngon par phab ste rin po che'i phreng ba'i sprin gyi char yang rab tu phab nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa de la mchod
21a8(phal chen): pa bya ba'i phyir spyan sngar phyin to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa des kho mo la mdo sde de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang dag par 'byung ba'i gnas snying po zhes bya ba'i mdo sde grangs med pa'i 'khor
21b1(phal chen): dang bcas pa yang dag par bstan te/ de yang kho mos thos nas bzung ste chud zos par ma byas so/ /rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa lnga brgya po de dag thams cad kyi tha mar de bzhin gshegs pa chos
21b2(phal chen): kyis dbyings namakha' mdzod spus yongasu rgyas pa'i rtse mo dpal gyi sgron ma zhes bya ba 'jig rten du byung ste/ de'i tshe kho mo yang gar mkhan gyi bu mo bzhin mngon par mdzes pa'i dpal zhes bya ba zhig tu
21b3(phal chen): gyur te/ de bzhin gshegs pa de grong khyer du gshegs nas/ gar mkhan gyi tshogs kyis rol mo byas pa'i tshe/ kho mos sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis steng gi namakha'i dbyings las/ tshigasu bcad pa stong gis de bzhin
21b4(phal chen): gshegs pa de la mngon par bstod de/ spyan sngar phyin to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa des mdzod spu nas 'od zer chos kyi dbyings rnam par snang ba'i rgyan ces bya ba bkye ste/ kho mo'i lus thams cad kyang snang bar mdzad
21b5(phal chen): do/ /'od zer des kho mo la phog ma thag tu rnam par thar pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul yongasu 'khyil ba'i snying po zhes bya ba thob par gyur to/ /rigs kyi bu de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa de dag la stsogs pa bskal
21b6(phal chen): pa 'od chen po la 'jig rten gyi khams rin chen 'khor lo sna tshogs kyis klubs shing brgyan par sangs rgyas lnga brgya byung bar gyur pa de dag thams cad kyang mnyes par byas te/ de bzhin gshegs pa de dag
21b7(phal chen): la kho mos mchod pa yang byas so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi kho mo la chos bstan pa de dag thams cad kyang dran te/ chos kyi tshul de dag las yi ge 'ga' 'am/ tshig 'ga' yang brjed par ma gyur to/ /
21b8(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa de dag re re'i drung du 'gro ba'i tshe yang sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su brjod par bya bas sems can tshad med pa'i don byas so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de dag re re la yang kho mos chos
22a1(phal chen): k yi dbyings kyi rang bzhin rgya mtsho dus gsum gyi ye shes kyi snying po chos kyi dbyings shin tu yangs pa zhes bya ba'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i glog mngon par snang ba kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa thams
22a2(phal chen): cad la gnas par yang dag par gzhol ba thob par gyur to/ rigs kyi bu kho mo la ni da ltar yang sems kyi skad cig re re la de bzhin gshegs pa mtha' dang dbus med pa yongasu snang ste/ de bzhin gshegs
22a3(phal chen): pa de dag kho mos mthong bar gyur pas thams cad mkhyen pa'i glog mngon par snang ba/ sngan chad ma thob pa sngan chad ma mthong ba dag kyang kho mo'i sems kyi rgyud la gnas par gyur to/ 'on kyang byang chub sems
22a4(phal chen): dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa las g.yo ba med do/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i glog mngon par snang ba thob pa 'di ni mtha' dang dbus med par bstan pa'o/ /de nas mtshan mo'i lha mo
22a5(phal chen): sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid kyi/ dkyil 'khor de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa 'jig rten thams cad mngon du gyur pas/ 'gro ba rnam par 'dul ba zhes bya ba 'di brten te
22a6(phal chen): bstan pa dang / rnam par dbye bar bya ba'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlab kyis tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la tshigasu bcad de smras pa/ /zab mo blta dka' khong du chud dka' ste/ /dus gsum dbyings kun tha dad
22a7(phal chen): tshul ldan la/ /chos 'od dkyil 'khor kun tu 'od 'byung ba'i/ /kho mo'i tshig 'di nor bzangs mnyan par gyis/ /sangs rgyas yon tan 'dod pas byang chub tu/ /kho mos thog ma ji ltar sems bskyed dang / /
22a8(phal chen): ji ltar kho mos rnam thar 'di thob pa/ /de dag rnam par phye ba'i tshul 'di nyan/ /'di nas sangs rgyas zhing gi rdul snyed kyi/ /bskal pa gcig nas gcig brgyud pha rol tu/ /'jig rten khams yangs
22b1(phal chen): dri ma'i skyon med pa/ /rnam snang rgyal mtshan sgron ma'i dpal byung ste/ /bskal pa rdul dang bral ba'i dkyil 'khor byung / /de la sangs rgyas rigs ni rgyun ma chad/ /de tshe ri rab rdul phran rab snyed kyi/ /
22b2(phal chen): stobs bcu skyon med mang po byung bar gyur/ /de la bde gshegs thog mar rin chen 'od/ /kun tu 'phro dpal yon tan dpal rgyal byung / /rgyal ba chos kyi rgyal mtshan ri rab dpal/ /yon tan seng ge'i
22b3(phal chen): dbang po rgyal ba bzhi/ /rgyal ba zhi ba'i rgyal po skye bcil dang / /grags pa'i ri bo yon tan ri rab dpal/ /rgyal ba nyi ma zla zhal bcom ldan 'das/ /bcu pa 'di dag tshul 'di thog ma'o/ /
22b4(phal chen): rgyal ba nam mkha'i gzhi dang kun nas 'od/ /phyogs su yongs byung dran pa rgya mtsho'i sgo/ /rgyal ba mngon 'phags 'od mnga' ri rab dpal/ /bde gshegs chos kyi 'od 'phro ri bo'i dpal/ /thugs
22b5(phal chen): rje che mnga' dgu pa pad mos 'phags/ /sangs rgyas bcu pa chos dbyings me tog ste/ /sangs rgyas rgya mtsho yongs su brjod pa lags/ /tshul 'di bcu pa gnyis pa 'di yin no/ /'od dpal rgyal po
22b6(phal chen): ye shes blo gros dang / /sna tshogs don dbang dpal gyi blo gros lha/ /rgyal ba shugs kyi rgyal blo ye shes dpal/ /snang ba'i rgyal po 'od kyi rgyal mtshan dpal/ /rgyal ba rnam par gnon pa'i lha stabs dang / /
22b7(phal chen): de bzhin chos dbyings pad mo bcu pa ste/ /rgya chen yongasu bstan nas tshul 'di ni/ /tshul 'dir bcu pa gsum pa bstan pa'o/ /rin chen 'od 'phro ri dpal bcom ldan 'das/ /de yi 'og ma yon tan rgya mtsho
22b8(phal chen): dpal/ /chos kyi 'od dang pad mo snying po dpal/ /'gro ba'i zla ba spyan tshul bde bar gshegs/ /spos kyi 'od dang rin can ri rab dpal/ /rgyal ba dri za lus 'od rgyal po dang / /rin chen snying po rgyal dpal
23a1(phal chen): gzi brjid ldan/ /rgyal ba bcu pa zhi ba'i gzugs kyi stabs/ /de yi 'og ma rgyal ba rgya chen blo/ /rin chen 'od dang nam mkha'i sprin gyi dpal/ /rgyal ba dam pa'i mtshan gyi dpal gyur dang / /
23a2(phal chen): brtul zhugs dkyil 'khor rang gi lus kyi 'od/ /mthu chen brtul zhugs ri rab dpal mnga' dang / /rgyal ba yon tan 'khor yug dpal gyi rgyal/ /bcom ldan mi pham brtul zhugs rgyal
23a3(phal chen): mtshan dang / /shing gi ri bo rgyal ba de dag bcu/ /rgyal ba stsa la'i rgyal po dpal gyi mchog /'jig rten dbang po'i lus ni sna yi 'od/ /mngon par 'phags 'od dpal gyi bcom ldan 'das/ /
23a4(phal chen): rdo rje'i 'od dang sa yi gzi brjid dpal/ /rgyal ba zab chos 'od kyi rgyal po dpal/ /chos kyi rgya mtsho dbyangs kyi blo gros dang / /ri rab rgyal mtshan dpal dang blo gros snang / /rgyal ba bcu pa
23a5(phal chen): rin chen rgyal po dpal/ /tshangs pa'i 'od dang rgyal ba nam mkha' dbyings/ /de bzhin chos kyi dbyings ni gzugs brnyan dpal/ /snang ba'i dkyil 'khor 'od kyi bcom ldan 'das/ /tha dad phyogs
23a6(phal chen): mkhyen ye shes blo gros dang / /nam mkha'i sgron ma mngon par dga' ba'i dpal/ /rnam par snang mdzad 'od dpal bde bar gshegs/ /bsod nams rab tu snang dpal zhi ba'i dpal/ /bcu pa'i snying
23a7(phal chen): rje chen po'i sprin gyi dpal/ /de bzhin nyid 'od stobs snang blo gros dang / /rgyal ba 'gro ba thams cad mngon gzigs dang / /de tshe rgyal ba mngon 'phags 'od mang 'byung / /de yi 'og ma zhi ba'i sku yi
23a8(phal chen): 'od/ /chos 'phags bde gshegs de bzhin byung bar 'gyur/ /de yi 'og ma rlung gi drag shul dpal/ /dpa' bo'i rgyal mtshan rin chen lus kyi dpal/ /dus gsum snang ba'i 'od ni bcu pa'o/ /
23b1(phal chen): smon lam rgya mtsho rab tu snang dpal dang / /gnyis pa dgongs pa rdo rje ri bo dpal/ /rgyal ba gsum pa seng ge ri rab dpal/ /dran pa'i rgyal mtshan rgyal po chos dpal blo/ /shes rab sgron ma 'od
23b2(phal chen): kyi rgyal mtshan dpal/ /de yi 'og ma rgyal ba rgya chen blo/ /rgyal ba chos dbyings tshul gyi ye shes stabs/ /chos kyi rgya mtsho blo gros ye shes dpal/ /chos 'dzin pa dang rin chen sbyin dpal dang / /
23b3(phal chen): rgyal ba yon tan khor yug dpal gyi sprin/ /bzod pa'i sgron ma dpal dang gzi brjid ldan/ /shugs 'od zhi gnas dbyangs kyi rgyal ba dang / /zhi ba'i rgyal mtshan 'gro ba'i sgron ma dpal/ /sangs rgyas
23b4(phal chen): smon lam chen po shugs kyi dpal/ /bcom ldan gzhan gyis mi thub rgyal mtshan stobs/ /rgyal ba ye shes 'od 'phro rgya mtsho dpal/ /rgyal ba chos dbang blo gros chags pa med/ /'gro skad rgya mtsho
23b5(phal chen): dbyangs kyi blo gros dang / /thams cad dbyangs kyi yan lag sgra skad dpal/ /dbang bsgyur mchod sbyin grags pa'i mchod sdong blo/ /phyogs yul 'gro ba mngon sum bcom ldan 'das/ /sems can
23b6(phal chen): bsam par mnyam pa sku yi dpal/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas gnas dang bcas pa'i dpal/ /rgyal ba rang bzhin lus dpal bzang po dang / /der ni rgyal ba de la stsogs pa byung / /de dag byung nas 'gro ba sgron
23b7(phal chen): ma mdzad/ /bskal pa ri rab shin tu phra rdul snyed/ /bdag gis rgyal ba rgya mtsho de dag mchod/ /bskal pa sangs rgyas zhing gi rdul snyed po/ /de dag du ni rgyal ba gang byung ba/ /bde gshegs de dag thams
23b8(phal chen): cad bdag gis mchod/ /rnam par thar pa'i tshul ni 'di la zhugs/ /rnam par thar pa'i tshul 'di sgom byed cing / /bskal pa mtha' yas bdag gis sngon spyad kyis/ /khyod kyis thos nas nan tan myur
24a1(phal chen): gyis shig / tshul 'di ring po mi thogs thob par 'gyur/ /rigs kyi bu kho mos byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa 'jig rten thams cad mngon du gyur pas/ 'gro ba rnam par 'dul
24a2(phal chen): ba ston pa 'di shes par zad na/ kho mos byang chub sems dpa' mtha' dang dbus med pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho la mos pa sna tshogs kyis yang dag par gnas pa/ bsam pa sna
24a3(phal chen): tshogs kyi lus dang ldan pa/ dbang po rgya mtsho sna tshogs yongs su grub pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / smon lam sna tshogs shin tu rtogs pa de dag gi spyod pa shes pa 'am/ yon tan
24a4(phal chen): brjod par nus re skan/ song rigs kyi bu snying po byang chub 'di nyid na kho mo dang rgyang mi ring ba zhig na mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa zhes bya ba pad mo'i khri rin po che'i rgyal po snang
24a5(phal chen): ba'i rgyal mtshan gyis rab tu brgyan pa zhig la 'dug cing / mtshan mo'i lha mo grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu'i 'khor gyis bskor ba 'dug gi/ de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems
24a6(phal chen): dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bya ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bya ba dris shig /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis mtshan mo'i lha mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi
