24a7(phal chen): brjid dpal gyi rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ mtshan mo'i lha mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas yang dang yang
24a8(phal chen): bltas te/ mtshan mo'i lha mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi drung nas song ngo // //sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po gnyis pa/
24b1(phal chen): de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs mtshan mo'i lha mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa 'jig rten thams cad mngon du gyur pas 'gro ba rnam par 'dul
24b2(phal chen): ba de la yongs su sgom zhing khong du chud par bya ba dang / yid ches par bya ba dang / 'jug par bya ba dang / shin tu rgyas par bya ba dang / yongs su khyab par bya ba dang / rab tu mchod par bya ba dang / dbang du bya ba dang /
24b3(phal chen): snang bar bya ba dang / yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba byed cing / mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa gang na ba der phyin te/ mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa'i rkang pa
24b4(phal chen): gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi
24b5(phal chen): ba dang ldan pa'i mdun du 'dug ste/ thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces smras so/ /'phags ma lha mo bdag ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs pa ste/ bdag ni dge
24b6(phal chen): ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rten gyis byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la slob cing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la zhugs te/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la nan tan du bgyi ba dang / byang chub
24b7(phal chen): sems dpa'i spyod pa la rab tu gnas pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'byung bar 'tshal na/ 'phags ma lha mo ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi
24b8(phal chen): ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba bdag la bshad du gsol/ de nas mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smras so/ /rigs kyi bu de
25a1(phal chen): ltar khyod dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rten gyis byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongasu tshol ba legaso legaso/ /rigs kyi bu kho mo ni byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba yangs pa'i shug 'byung bas
25a2(phal chen): sems kyi skad gcig rnam par brgyan pa thob pa'o/ /nor bzangs kyi smras pa/ 'phags ma khyod ni 'phrin las ci mdzad yul gang dang ldan pa sbyor ba gang dang ldan/ ci la rnam par dpyod/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par
25a3(phal chen): thar pa dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa de yul ji lta bu zhig mchis des smras pa/ rigs kyi bu kho mo ni sems dang bsam pa rgya mtsho yongasu dag pa'i mnyam pa nyid la
25a4(phal chen): zhugs pa ste/ 'jig rten gyi rdul dang dri ma thams cad rnam par bsal bas mi phyed pas brgyan pa'i bsam pa la zhugs pa'o/ /brtsam pa las mi ldog mi bzlog pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /rin po che'i
25a5(phal chen): ri bo ltar yon tan gyis brgyan pa'i sems mi skul ba dang ldan pa'o/ /mi gnas mi rten pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /'gro ba thams cad yongasu skyob pa la mngon par phyogs pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /
25a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas rgya mtsho thams cad mthong bas mi ngom pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi stobs kyi bsam pa rnam par dag pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /dran pa'i rgya mtsho ye shes
25a7(phal chen): kyi snang ba chen pos brgyan pa la yang dag par gnas pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /sems can thams cad mya ngan gyi dgon pa las yang dag par zla ba la zhug pa'o sems can thams cad sdug bsngal ba dang yid mi bde ba
25a8(phal chen): las rnam par bzlog pa la mngon par brtson pa'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi yid du mi 'ong ba'i gzugs dang / sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg yongasu rgyu ba rnam par bzlog pa la zhugs pa'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi sdug pa dang /
25b1(phal chen): mi sdug pa dang bral zhing phrad pa'i sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar bya ba la zhugs pa'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi yul gyi rkyen las byung bas mgo rmongs pa'i sdug bsngal rnam par bzlog pa la rab
25b2(phal chen): tu brtson pa'o/ /log par lhung ba'i sems can thams cad kyi rten du gyur pa'o/ /sems can thams cad 'khor ba'i gnas gyi sdug bsngal las 'byung ba yang dag par ston pa la mngon par brtson
25b3(phal chen): pa'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi rga shi dang mya ngan dang smre sngags 'don pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang yid mi bde ba dang / 'khrug pa rnam par bzlog pa la zhugs pa'o/ /sems can thams cad la
25b4(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i bde ba bla na med pa yongs su bsgrub par zhugs pa ste/ grong dang grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / yul dang khams dang / rgyal po'i gnas na 'khod pa'i sems can thams cad
25b5(phal chen): bde bar rim gror bya bas nyams dga' bar 'gyur zhing de dag la chos dang 'thun par bsrung ba dang / bskyab pa dang rim gror bya ba yang legs par byed de/ de dag rim pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du
25b6(phal chen): yongs su smyin par byed do/ /'di lta ste khang khyim dang / gzhal med khang na gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyi mngon par chags pa yongs su bskyed do/ /yid mi bde ba de dang de dag kyang rnam par sel to/ /
25b7(phal chen): mngon par zhen pa thams cad rgyun gcod pa dang / chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /pha ma dang phu nu dang sring mo dang gnyen bshes dang 'grogs pa'i sems can
25b8(phal chen): yun ring po nas bshes shing 'dza' bar gyur pa dag la sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang phrad par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /bu smad dang 'grogs pa'i sems can rnams la 'khor ba'i
26a1(phal chen): sred pa thams cad rab tu spang ba dang / sems can thams cad la mnyam pa nyid kyi sems su bya ba dang / snying rje chen po rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /tshong dus
26a2(phal chen): kyi dbus na 'khod pa'i sems can rnams la 'phags pa'i dge 'dun dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mthong bar bya ba la yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /longs spyod
26a3(phal chen): kyi dregs pas myos pa'i sems can rnams la bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /glu dang gar dang rol mo la mngon par dga' ba'i sems
26a4(phal chen): can rnams la chos kyi dga' ba la mos par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /yul gyi dga' ba la chags pa'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul la yang dag par gzhol bar
26a5(phal chen): bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /khro bas yongs su non pa'i sems can rnams la bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la rab tu dgod par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /sems can le lo can rnams
26a6(phal chen): la brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /sems rnam par mos pa'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa
26a7(phal chen): rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /lta ba'i rnam pa thibs por subs pa'i sems can ma rig pa'i mun nag na 'thoms pa rnams la lta ba'i rnam pa thibs po dang ma rig
26a8(phal chen): pa'i mun pa rnam par bstsal ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /shes rab 'chal ba can gyi sems can rnams la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /
26b1(phal chen): khams gsum pa la mngon par zhen pa'i sems can rnams la 'khor ba las 'byung bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /dma' ba la mos pa'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i
26b2(phal chen): byang chub tu smon lam yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /bdag la phan par brtson pa'i sems can rnams la sems can thams cad la phan par bya ba'i smon lam yongs su
26b3(phal chen): rdzogs par 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /bsam pa nyam chung ba'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston
26b4(phal chen): to/ /ma rig pa'i mun pas sems blong ba'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /gzugs mi sdug pa dang
26b5(phal chen): ldan pa'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i gzugs rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /lus kyi dbyibs mi mdzes pa dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la chos kyi
26b6(phal chen): sku bla na med pa rnam par dag pa'i phyir chos ston to/ /kha dog mi sdug pa dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku mdog gser gyi kha dog lta bu dang shin tu 'jam
26b7(phal chen): zhing ka tsa lin+di ltar reg na bde ba'i lus rnam par dag pa'i phyir chos ston to/ /sdug bsngal ba'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i bden pa dam pa thob par bya ba'i phyir chos
26b8(phal chen): ston to/ /bde ba'i sems can rnams la thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bde ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /nad pa na ba'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems
27a1(phal chen): dpa'i lus gzugs brnyan lta bu yongs su grub par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /dga' ba sna tshogs la brtson pa'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i
27a2(phal chen): dga' ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /phongs pa'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi gter dang mdzod rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /
27a3(phal chen): bza' shing gi ra ba na gnas pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su btsal bar la mngon par brtson pa'i rgyu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /lam du zhugs pa'i
27a4(phal chen): sems can rnams la thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam du 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /grong na gnas pa'i sems can rnams la khams gsum pa thams cad 'byung bar bya
27a5(phal chen): ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /yul gyi mdab na gnas pa'i sems can rnams la nyan thos dang rang byang chub kyi lam las yang dag par 'da' bar bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs
27a6(phal chen): pa'i sa la rab tu dgod par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /grong rdal na 'khod pa'i sems can rnams la chos kyi rgyal po'i pho brang du gnas par 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /
27a7(phal chen): phyogs mtshams na 'khod pa'i sems can rnams la dus gsum mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /phyogs na gnas pa'i sems can rnams la chos
27a8(phal chen): thams cad ye shes mngon par shes par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /'dod chags la gcig tu dga' ba'i sems can rnams la mi sdug pa'i sgos 'khor ba'i sred pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir chos
27b1(phal chen): ston to/ /zhe sdang la spyod pa'i sems can rnams la byams pa chen po'i tshul rgya mtsho la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /gti mug la spyod pa'i sems can rnams la chos thams cad
27b2(phal chen): kyi sgo rgya mtsho rab tu 'byed pa'i ye shes mngon par shes par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /cha mnyam pa la spyod pa'i sems can rnams la theg pa thams cad kyi smon lam gyi tshul rgya mtshos
27b3(phal chen): khyad par du 'gro bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /'khor ba'i yul la dga' ba'i bsam pa can gyi sems can rnams la 'khor ba'i yul la dga' ba rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir chos ston to/ /
27b4(phal chen): 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad kyis gtses pa'i sems can rnams la 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad kyis nye bar nyon mongs pa med par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /de bzhin
27b5(phal chen): gshegs pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mi skye ba'i gnas yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir chos ston to/ /phung po la gnas pa'i bsam pa can gyi sems can rnams la
27b6(phal chen): gzhi med pa'i chos kyi spyod yul la rnam par spyod par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /bsam pa zhum pa'i sems can rnams la lam gyi rgyun gyi khyad par yang dag par bstan par bya ba'i
27b7(phal chen): phyir chos ston to/ /mtho ba'i nga rgyal can gyi sems can rnams la chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi bzod pa yang dag par bstan par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /g.yo sgyu'i yul gyi bsam pa
27b8(phal chen): dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston te/ de ltar rigs kyi bu kho mo ni sems can thams cad chos kyi
28a1(phal chen): sbyin pas yongs su bsdus shing ngan song gi lam gyi rgyud sdug bsngal ba thams cad nas rnam par bzlog pa dang / lha dang mi'i phun sum tshogs pa dang bde ba yongs su bstan pa dang /
28a2(phal chen): khams gsum pa las gyen du bskyod pa dang / /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la rab tu dgod pa dang / thabs rnam pa sna tshogs kyis yongs su smyin par byed pas/ dga' ba chen po'i shugs
28a3(phal chen): rgya mtsho snang ba rab tu thob pas dga' zhing spro la yid bde bar gyur to/ /gzhan yang rigs kyi bu kho mo ni phyogs dang / phyogs mtshams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor
28a4(phal chen): rgya mtsho la rnam par lta zhing smon lam rgya mtsho la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' lus sna tshogs rnam par dag pa/ 'od kyi dkyil 'khor sna tshogs kyi rgyan dang ldan pa/ 'od zer dang 'od
28a5(phal chen): kyi dkyil 'khor kha dog mtha' yas pa rab tu 'gyed pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshul rgya mtsho sna tshogs pa'i ye shes snang ba can/ ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho sna tshogs la zhugs pa'i
28a6(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul ba sna tshogs kyi yul dang ldan pa/ dbyangs kyi yan lag dang skad sna tshogs kyi dbyangs dang ldan pa/ rgyan sna tshogs kyis rnam par glubs pa'i lus can/ de bzhin
28a7(phal chen): gshegs pa'i tshul sna tshogs la zhugs pa/ zhing rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa sna tshogs su zhugs pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho sna tshogs la zhugs pa/ so so yang dag par
28a8(phal chen): rig pa rgya mtsho sna tshogs la zhugs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par mdzad pa dang / ye shes kyi yul sna tshogs kyis snang bar gyur pa/ ye shes rgya mtsho sna tshogs kyi snang ba rab tu
28b1(phal chen): thob pa/ ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho sna tshogs kyi tshul rnam par spyod pa/ sna tshogs kyi rnam par thar pa'i gzhal med khang na rnam par rtse ba'i yul dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi
28b2(phal chen): sgo sna tshogs la mngon du gnas pa/ chos kyi dbyings sna tshogs kyi nam mkha'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ rgyan sna tshogs kyi sprin gyis nam mkha' rgyas par 'gengs pa/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor
28b3(phal chen): rgya mtsho sna tshogs la rnam par lta ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams sna tshogs nas 'dus pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing sna tshogs 'byam klas par rjes su 'dong ba/ phyogs
28b4(phal chen): rgya mtsho sna tshogs nas yongs su 'dus pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa tha dad pas bkye ba/ /de bzhin gshegs pa tha dad pa'i zhabs kyi drung nas lhags pa/
28b5(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs sna tshogs kyi 'khor dang ldan pa/ rgyan sna tshogs kyi sprin gyi char rab tu 'bebs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul sna tshogs la zhugs
28b6(phal chen): pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos rgya mtsho sna tshogs kyi 'khor dang ldan pa/ ye shes sna tshogs rgya mtsho la zhugs pa/ rgyan gyi snying po sna tshogs can gyi stan la 'khod
28b7(phal chen): pa rnams kyi dga' ba sna tshogs kyi shugs rgya mtsho yongs su bskyed de/ de dag dga' ba sna tshogs kyi shugs rgya mtsho yongs su bskyed nas/
29a1(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtshor 'dong ste/ de dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs tshad med pa rjes su sems pas kyang dga' ba'i shugs chen po rgya mtsho yongs su
29a2(phal chen): 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang kho mo ni bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi gzugs kyi sku yongs su dag pa mtshan gyis rab tu brgyan pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa mthong nas dga' ba
29a3(phal chen): chen po dang mos shing bde ba rab tu thob ste/ sems kyi skad cig re re la 'ang 'od kyi dkyil 'khor chos kyi dbyings ltar yangs pa/ kha dog rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus med par snang ba la lta shing sems kyi
29a4(phal chen): skad cig re re la dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho rab tu 'thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku'i ba spu'i sgo re re nas kyang 'od gzer chen po sangs rgyas kyi
29a5(phal chen): z hing mtha' dang dbus med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ste 'od zer re re zhing yang 'od zer rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing mtha' yas pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor dang ldan pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par
29a6(phal chen): 'gengs pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar mdzad pa mthong zhing sems kyi skad cig re re la dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho rab tu 'thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang
29a7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi dbu dang / sku phrag pa gnyis kyi lhun las sems kyi skad cig re re la rin po che thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba'i ri sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi
29a8(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing / chos kyi dbyings rgya mtsho thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa mthong nas/ dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob po/ /rigs kyi
29b1(phal chen): bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku'i ba spu'i sgo re re nas sems kyi skad cig re re la kha dog dri zhim po dang / 'od gzer sna tshogs can gyi sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing
29b2(phal chen): thams cad kyi rdul shin du phra ba snyed byung zhing thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa mthong nas/ dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu thob po/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das
29b3(phal chen): rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na/ sems kyi skad cig re re la mtshan re re nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs mtshan rab tu brgyan pa'i sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad
29b4(phal chen): kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom
29b5(phal chen): l dan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku'i dpe byad bzang po re re las sems kyi skad cig re re la de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa'i sku dpe byad bzang po brgyad bcu shin tu 'bar ba'i sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing
29b6(phal chen): thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ba ste/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rgyas par 'gengs shing de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo'i dbyangs su sgrog pa'i 'brug sgra 'byin pa
29b7(phal chen): mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na/ sems kyi skad cig re re la
29b8(phal chen): ba spu'i sgo thams cad nas sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa'i sku dang po byang chub tu thugs bskyed pa dang bcas/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i lam rnam par dag pa'i rgyan dang bcas/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa yongs su
30a1(phal chen): gnon pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'byung ba mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu thob bo/ /rigs
30a2(phal chen): kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku las sems kyi skad cig re re la lha'i dbang po'i lus kyi sprin lha'i dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul
30a3(phal chen): phra ba snyed byung zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ lha'i dbang po'i lus kyi sprin yongs su bstan pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mngon du gnas shing chos ston pa mthong nas/
30a4(phal chen): dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu thob po/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku las rnam par bltas na/ sems kyi skad cig re re la klu'i dbang po'i lus kyi sprin klu'i dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang
30a5(phal chen): bcas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bkang te/ klu'i dbang po'i lus bstan pa'i 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mngon
30a6(phal chen): du gnas shing chos ston pa mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu thob po/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par
30a7(phal chen): bltas na/ sems kyi skad cig re re la ba spu'i sgo thams cad nas gnod sbyin gyi dbang po'i lus kyi sprin gyi gnod sbyin gyi dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod
30a8(phal chen): du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ gnod sbyin gyi dbang po'i lus yongs su bstan pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnam la mngon du gnas shing chos
30b1(phal chen): ston pa mthong nas/ dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu thob po/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnams par bltas na sems kyi skad
30b2(phal chen): cig re re la ba spu'i sgo thams cad nas/ dri za'i dbang po'i lus kyi sprin dri za'i dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing chos kyi
30b3(phal chen): dbyings thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ dri za'i dbang po'i lus yongs su bstan pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mngon du gnas shing chos ston pa mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs
30b4(phal chen): pa rab tu 'thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na sems kyi skad cig re re la ba spu'i sgo nas lha ma yin gyi dbang po'i lus kyi sprin lha ma yin gyis
30b5(phal chen): dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ lha ma yin gyi dbang po'i lus
30b6(phal chen): yongs su bstan pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mngon par gnas shing / chos ston pa mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan
30b7(phal chen): 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na/ sems kyi skad cig re re la ba spu'i sgo re re nas nam mkha' lding gis dbang po'i lus kyi sprin namakha' lding gi dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa/
30b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ nam mkha' lding gi dbang po'i lus yongs su bstan pas 'dul ba'i sems can
31a1(phal chen): rnams la mngon du gnas shing chos ston pa mthong nas/ dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob bo/ /gzhan yang rigs kyi bu bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang
31a2(phal chen): mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na sems kyi skad cig re re la ba spu'i sgo re re nas mi 'am ci'i dbang po'i lus kyi sprin mi 'am ci'i dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du
31a3(phal chen): med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ mi 'am ci'i dbang po'i lus yongs su bstan pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mngon du gnas shing chos ston pa mthong
31a4(phal chen): nas/ dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na sems kyi skad cig re re la ba spu'i sgo re re
31a5(phal chen): nas lto phye chen po'i lus kyi sprin lto 'phye chen po'i rnam par 'phrul pa bcas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing chos kyi dbyings rgyas par bkang ste/ lto 'phye chen po'i
31a6(phal chen): dbang po'i lus yongs su bstan pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mngon du gnas shing chos ston pa mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob po/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan
31a7(phal chen): yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na/ sems kyi skad cig re re la ba spu'i sgo re re nas mi'i dbang po'i lus kyi sprin mi'i dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa/ sangs
31a8(phal chen): rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ mi'i dbang po'i lus yongs su bstan pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mngon du gnas
31b1(phal chen): shing brjod pa mthong nas/ dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na sems
31b2(phal chen): kyi skad cig re re la ba spu'i sgo re re nas tshangs pa'i dbang po'i lus kyi sprin tshangs pa'i dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa'i yul dang bcas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung
31b3(phal chen): zhing chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ tshangs pa'i dbang po'i lus yongs su bstan pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mngon du gnas shing tshangs pa'i sgra skad dang dbyangs kyi chos ston
31b4(phal chen): pa mthong nas sems kyi skad cig re re la thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho chos kyi dbyings ltar rgya che zhing shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob ste/ sngon thob
31b5(phal chen): par gyur pa 'thob par 'gyur ba ma yin no/ /sngon khong du chud pa khong du chud par 'gyur ba ma yin no/ /sngon zhugs pa la 'jug par 'gyur ba ma yin no/ /sngon khyab par gyur pa khyab par 'gyur ba
31b6(phal chen): ma yin no/ /sngon mthong ba mthong bar 'gyur ba ma yin no/ /sngon thos pa thos par 'gyur ba ma yin no/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ chos kyi rang bzhin gyi mtshan nyid yongs su shes pa ltar na chos thams
31b7(phal chen): cad mtshan nyid gcig pa 'ang ci rob ma yin te/ dus gsum gyi tshul la 'jug pa'i sgo nas chos thams cad kyang mtha' dang dbus med par bstan tu yod pa ste/ 'di ni rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa'i rnam
31b8(phal chen): par thar pa'i tshul dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas sems kyi skad cig rnam par thar pa'i tshul rgya mtsho'i snang ba ste/ rigs kyi bu rnam par thar pa 'di ni chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i phyir
32a1(phal chen): mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa dang / tha mi dad pas zad mi shes pa'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i
32a2(phal chen): ye shes kyang mig gis rnam par shes par bya ba yin pas mu med pa'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni chos kyis dbyings tha mi dad pa'i tshul gtan tu rgyas par 'gengs pas gting zab med pa'o/ /rnam par
32a3(phal chen): thar pa 'di ni dmigs pa cig tu rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su 'du bar byed pas sgo thams cad dang ldan pa'o rnam par thar pa 'di ni chos thams cad kyi lus dang mi gnyis par spyod pas don yod pa'o/ /
32a4(phal chen): rnam par thar pa 'di ni sgyu ma lta bur yongs su spyod pas ma skyes pa'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi smon lam gyi gzugs brnyan du byung bas gzugs brnyan lta bu'o/ /rnam
32a5(phal chen): par thar pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pas shin tu sprul pa'i phyir sprul pa lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni 'gro ba thams cad kyi rten du gyur pas sa chen po lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di
32a6(phal chen): ni 'gro ba thams cad snying rje chen pos mngon par brlan par byed pas chu'i phung po lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni sems can thams cad kyi sred pa'i brlan yongs su skems pas mye'i phung po lta bu'o/ /
32a7(phal chen): rnam par thar pa 'di ni sems can thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du rab tu ston pa'i phyir rlung gi phung po lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni 'gro ba thams cad kyi yon tan gyi rgyan gyi gzhi yin pas rgya
32a8(phal chen): mtsho lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni chos thams cad kyi ye shes rin po che rgya mtsho las mngon par 'phags pas ri rab ri'i rgyal po lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni chos thams cad kyi rnam par thar
32b1(phal chen): pa'i gzhal med khang rnam par spyod pa'i phyir rnam par spyod pa'i rlung gi dkyil 'khor lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni dus gsum du 'byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnams par 'phrul pa thams cad kyi go 'byed
32b2(phal chen): pas nam mkha' lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni sems can thams cad la chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon du 'bebs pas sprin chen po lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni sems can thams cad kyi mi shes pa'i
32b3(phal chen): mun nag rnam par sel bas nyi ma lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni bsod nams dang ye shes kyi rgya mtsho chen pos shin tu bsgrub pa'i phyir ba lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni thams cad du song ba'i phyir de bzhin
32b4(phal chen): nyid lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni las kyi chos kyis shin tu sprul pa'i phyir rang gi grib ma lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni sems can mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi sgra rab tu sgrog pas brag cha lta
32b5(phal chen): bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems can thams cad kyi rnam par dmigs par byed pa'i phyir gzugs brnyan lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par
32b6(phal chen): 'phrul pa'i me tog shin tu rgyas pa'i phyir shing gi rgyal po lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni mi shigs pa'i chos can yin pas rdo rje lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' dang dbus med pa rgya mtsho mngon
32b7(phal chen): par bsgrub pas/ nor bu yid bzhin rin po che'i rgyal po lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rnam par dmigs par bya ba la sgrib pa med pas rin
32b8(phal chen): po che'i rgyal po dri ma med pa'i snying po lta bu'o/ /rnam par thar pa 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad chos kyi 'khor lo mnyam pa nyid du sgrog pas nor bu rin po che dga' ba'i rgyal mtshan lta bu ste/ rigs kyi bu byang
33a1(phal chen): c hub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs shin tu yangs pa 'byung bas sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa 'di ni dpe tshad med pa rnam par 'god pa'i rjes su 'brang bas bstan
33a2(phal chen): par bya'o/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa la 'di skad ces smras so/ /'phags ma lha mo ji ltar nan tan du bgyis na/ byang chub sems
33a3(phal chen): dpa' de lta bu'i rnam par thar pa de yongs su 'grub par 'gyur/ smras pa rigs kyi bu bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshogs chen po'i chos yangs pa dang ldan pa/ rnam par rgya chen po
33a4(phal chen): gsal ba chen po snang ba chen po/ 'od chen po byin chen po rnam par dbye ba chen po 'byung ba chen po phun sum tshogs pa chen po ste/ de dag la nan tan du byed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
33a5(phal chen): rnam par thar pa 'di lta bu phun sum tshogs par 'gyur ba dag go/ /bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i sbyin pa sems can rgya mtsho thams cad kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs
33a6(phal chen): su tshim par byed pa la zhugs pas ni rgya chen po'i chos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i nan tan la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos
33a7(phal chen): so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i bzod pa chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin nges par rtog par bya ba la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i brtson 'grus thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yang dag par
33a8(phal chen): brtsams pa las phyir mi ldog pa las zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i bsam gtan sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i gdung ba rab tu zhi bar bya ba la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so/ /
33b1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab kyi chos rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su shes par bya ba la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i thabs sems can rgya mtsho thams cad yongasu smin par bya ba
33b2(phal chen): dang gdul bar bya ba la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal par sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyad pa'i phyir
33b3(phal chen): rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du skad cig re re la mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar yongs su bstan pa rgyun mi bcad
33b4(phal chen): pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes dus gsum gyi chos thams cad la sgribs pa med pa'i ye shes thob par bya ba'i phyir de
33b5(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so/ /rigs kyi bu chos bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgya chen po'i chos tshogs chen po dang ldan pa rnams te/ de dag la gnas pa'i byang chub

39a2(phal chen): rnam thar tshul 'di la ni 'jug par gyis/ /bdag gi sems dang bsam pa yongs sgyongs zhing / /mos pa'i shugs yangs yongs su bskyed byas te/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes grong bdun pas/ /

39a4(phal chen): par kho mos bkur/ /sngon gyi bde gshegs kho mos mthong gyur nas/ /'gro la phan phyir yun ring mchod byas te/ /spro ba'i stobs ni rnam yangs yongs bskyed nas/ /bdag gis gdung ba med pa'i chos
39a5(phal chen): kyang thos/ /rnam par thar pa 'di la 'jug pa na/ /pha dang ma dang bla ma'i skye ba la/ /de tshe bdag gis phan bdes sti stang byas/ /bsnyen bkur sri zhur gnas pa kun kyang byas/ /rgas pa nad pa nor
39a6(phal chen): med mi rnams dang / /dbang po ma tshang sdug bsngal mgon med pa/ /mang po bdag gis byams sems bde bkod nas/ /tshe rabs brgyar yang nor phyug mgon yong byas/ /rgyal po mi dang rkun chom rkyen
39a7(phal chen): gyur dang / /seng ge glang po pha rol dgras 'jigs dang / /srid pa'i rgya mtsho'i 'jigs dngos sna tshogs las/ /sngon tshe spyod pa'i dus na bdag gis bskyabs/ /rtag tu srid gsum nyon mongs gdungs
39a8(phal chen): gyur te/ /las kyis rab gdungs de bzhin mi dge bas/ /'khor ba'i ri gzar g.yang du lhung ba yi/ /skye bo 'gro ba'i rgyud tu bdag gis bskyabs/ /sdug bsngal ngan song g.yang sas 'jigs
39b1(phal chen): pa dag / rtag tu mi bde shin tu mi zad dang / /skye dga' na zhing 'chi ba'i 'jigs med kun/ /bdag gis 'jig rten spyod tshe zhi bar byas/ /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal zhi bar bya ba dang / /sems can
39b2(phal chen): kun gyi bde ba yongs bskyed cing / /sangs rgyas bde ba dam pa bskyed pa ni/ /bskal pa phyi mthar kho mo'i smon lam mo/ /rigs kyi bu kho mos byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga'
39b3(phal chen): ba yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa 'di shes par zad na/ kho mos byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa
39b4(phal chen): phyi nang gi sdug bsngal ma lus pa las rnam par grol ba/ bskal pa'i ming du bya ba thams cad shes par gyur pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad 'byung ba dang / 'jig pa'i rgyus la mkhas pa
39b5(phal chen): de dag gi spyod pa shes pa 'am yon tan brjod pa nus re skan/ song rigs kyi bu snying po byang chub 'di nyid na bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor na/ mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams
39b6(phal chen): cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal zhes bya ba 'dug gis/ de'i gan tu song la ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bya ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bya ba dris shig /de nas
39b7(phal chen): tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa la tshul dang 'dra ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /dge ba'i bshes gyis ma nor 'thun bstan pas/ /lha mo
39b8(phal chen): khyod kyi drung du nye bar mchis/ /mtha' dang dbus mi mnga' ba'i sku tshul du/ /khyod ni gdan la bzhugs par bdag gis mthong / /kha dog dbyibs dang mtshan ma'i spyod yul ba/ /srid pa gnas dang dngos por 'du shes dang / /
40a1(phal chen): 'du shes dma' dang log par lta ba yis/ /khyod kyi spyod yul 'tshal bar mi nus so/ /khyod kyi sku gzugs blta na mtha' yas pas/ /khyod kyi sku gzugs mdog gi mtshan ma ni/ /bskal
40a2(phal chen): pa mtha' yas dag du yongs brtags kyang / /lha dang 'jig rten bcas pas shes mi nus/ /lha mo khyod ni phung po'i gnas las 'phags/ /skye mched rnams la de bzhin mi gnas te/ /'jig rten
40a3(phal chen): rnam par 'das pas the tsom bral/ /'jig rten dag tu rnam par 'phrul pa mdzad/ /g.yo ba mi mnga' skyon bral chags pa med/ /khyod kyis ye shes spyan ni rnam sbyangs pas/ /rdul gyi go la thams cad
40a4(phal chen): rdul tshad du/ /sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa mang po gzigs/ /khyod gyi sku ni chos sku'i snying po can/ /khyod kyi thugs kyang ye shes chags pa med/ /khyod ni kun tu 'od kyi snang mdzad pas/ /'jig rten skye
40a5(phal chen): bo rnams la mtha' yas snang / /sems las mtha' yas las rnams yongs su 'byung / /'jig rten thams cad las kyi rnam par bris/ /'gro ba sems kyi dngos su mkhyen gyur pas/ /rang gi sku yang
40a6(phal chen): 'gro ba snyed du bstan/ /'jig rten du ni rmi lam 'drar mkhyen nas/ /sangs rgyas kun kyang gzugs brnyan lta bu dang / /ma lus chos rnams sgra rnyan 'drar mkhyen pas/ /chags pa mi mnga' 'gro ba kun tu spyod/ /
40a7(phal chen): dus gsum gnas pa'i 'gro ba thams cad la/ /skad cig re re rang gi sku ston kyang / /khyod kyis thugs la gnyis su mi rgyu ste/ /phyogs rnams kun tu chos kyang rab tu bstan/ /rdul la 'gro ba rgya mtsho
40a8(phal chen): mtha' yas dang / /de bzhin sems can mtsho chen dpag yas dang / /mtha' dang dbus med bde gshegs gangs chen mtsho/ /kun kyang khyod kyi rnam thar dam pa'i yul/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor
40b1(phal chen): bzangs kyis mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa la/ tshul dang 'dra ba'i tshigs su bcad pa de dag gis mngon par bstod de/ lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas
40b2(phal chen): yang dang yang bltas te/ mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa'i drung nas song ngo / /sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po gsum pa/
40b3(phal chen): de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas/ sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa de ni sgom pa dang / rjes su sgom pa dang / yang dag par
40b4(phal chen): sgom pa dang / mtshan mo'i lha mo'i sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa'i gdams ngag dang / rjes su bstan pa la ni rjes su 'brang bar bya ba dang / rjes su dran par bya ba dang / khong du chud par byed/
40b5(phal chen): tshig dang yi ge re re la ni tshul du ma dang bsam pa tshad med pas chos nyid kyi tshul shes pa rjes su dran par byed cing dran pas rjes su 'brang bar bya ba dang / blo gros kyi rnam par dbye ba dang / rigs pa khong du chud par
40b6(phal chen): bya ba dang / blos shin tu yangs par bya ba dang / lus kyis regs par byas te/ rnam par spyad pa dang / rjes su 'jug par byed cing / mthar gyis mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung
40b7(phal chen): ba'i gzi brjid dpal gang na ba der phyin pa dang / mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal pad mo'i khri chen po/ nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po grong khyer dang / gnas thams
40b8(phal chen): cad rab tu snang bar byed pa'i snying po can la phyogs thams cad dang / 'gro ba thams cad la mngon sum du gyur pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi gzugs dang / mnyam pa'i lus dang sems can
41a1(phal chen): thams cad la mngon du gyur pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyis ma gos pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang rang bzhin mnyam pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad las
41a2(phal chen): mngon par 'phags pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gtul ba la 'thun pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad du sgra rab tu sgrog pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad
41a3(phal chen): du 'pho ba med pa'i lus dang / sgrib pa thams cad shin tu bcom pa'i lus dang / de bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin gyi lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad gtul bar mthar phyin par byed pa'i lus su 'dug
41a4(phal chen): cing / mtshan mo'i lha mo brjod du med pa'i 'khor gyis bskor te/ 'dug pa mthong nas/ dga' rangs nas mgu zhing nyams bde la tshim zhing yid bde ba skyes nas/ mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer
41a5(phal chen): thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrungs ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su
41a6(phal chen): bskor ba byas nas/ mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi mdun du 'dug ste/ thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces smras so/ /lha mo bdag bla na med pa
41a7(phal chen): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs na/ lha mo ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la rjes su bslabs na sems can la smin par gyur pa lags/
41a8(phal chen): ji ltar na sems can bla na med pa'i yongasu bsdu bas yongs su sdud par 'gyur/ ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pas gnang ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i las la brtson pa lags/
41b1(phal chen): ji ltar brtson par bgyis na byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi rgyal po nye bar 'gyur ba bdag la bshad du gsol/ de skad ces smras pa dang / mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung
41b2(phal chen): ba'i gzid brjid dpal gyis/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang la 'di skad ces smras so/ /rigs kyi bu khyod de ltar 'gro ba thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / rnam par gtul ba'i mthar phyin
41b3(phal chen): par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs kyi bdag por gzung ba'i sbyor ba mthar phyin par bya ba dang / phyogs 'byam klas pa thams cad rgyas par gang bar ye shes rab tu sbyar ba dang /
41b4(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la 'jug pa mngon du 'gyur ba dang / shes bya nam mkha'i dbyings dang mnyam par mtha' yas pa rgyas par dgang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi
41b5(phal chen): 'khor lo rab tu blang zhing yongasu gzung ba'i phyir 'gro ba rgya mtsho thams cad kyi bsam pa ji lta bzhin du chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa'i spyod pa'i tshul yongasu 'dri ba legaso legaso/ /rigs
41b6(phal chen): kyi bu kho mo ni byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa thob ste/ de ltar kho mo rnam par thar pa de dang ldan pas chos smra ba chen po'i go
41b7(phal chen): 'phang thogs pa med pa la dmigs pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi mdzod yongs su gtong ba'i smon lam dang ldan pa/ snying rje chen po dang byams pa chen po'i stobs
41b8(phal chen): rab tu thob pa/ sems can thams cad byang chub kyi sems la 'god pa'i phyir sems can thams cad kyi don bya ba la zhugs pa/ byang chub kyi sems kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / tshogs rab tu bstsags pa
42a1(phal chen): rgyun mi gcod pa'i phyir/ 'gro ba thams cad kha lo bsgyur ba'i sa la yang dag par gnas pa sems can thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi lam la rab tu dgod pa'i phyir/ 'jig rten gyi chos kyi sprin
42a2(phal chen): thams cad las chos kyi nyi ma yongs su 'byung ba'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa bskyed pas/ 'jig rten thams cad snang bar bya ba'i phyir/ 'gro ba thams cad la mnyam pa'i sems su
42a3(phal chen): 'jug pa rgyun mi gcod pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba mngon par 'du bya ba yongs su bsgrub pa'i sbyor ba shes par bya ba'i phyir/ sems rnam par dag pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i
42a4(phal chen): las kyi lam thams cad 'thun par bsgrub pas sems can thams cad kyi ded dpon du zhugs pa/ mi dge ba'i las kyi lam thams cad rab tu spangs pa/ sems can thams cad dge ba'i chos la rab tu
42a5(phal chen): dgod pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la lam bde ba yongasu ston pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad kyi theg pa'i rgyan kyi thog mar 'dren pa la zhugs pa/ dge ba'i chos kyi spyod
42a6(phal chen): pa thams cad la sems can rab tu dgod pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad la mi phyed par bsnyen bkur dang rim 'gro byed pa la zhugs pa/ sems can thams cad de bzhin gshegs
42a7(phal chen): pa'i stan pa la rab tu dgod pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ chos kyi sbyin pa'i sngon du 'dren cing chos dkar po thams cad yang dag par brtsam pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems bskyed pas
42a8(phal chen): mngon par 'byung bas bsam pa brtan zhing mi shigs pa/ rdo rje mthu bo che ltar brtan zhing sra bas sangs rgyas kyi stobs la dmigs pa'i sems rgya chen po'i dkyil 'khor dang ldan par dge ba'i bshes gnyen
42b1(phal chen): la rten cing rnam par spyod de/ kho mo ni nyon mongs pa dang las kyi sgrib pa thams cad kyi ri rnam par gtor ba'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshogs yang dag par rtsogs pa'o/ /
42b2(phal chen): dkar po'i chos thams cad yang dag par bsgrub pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa'o/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid mtha' dang dbus med pa mngon par 'dun cing dmigs pa'i sems kyi sbyor ba la brtson pa'o/ /rigs
42b3(phal chen): k yi bu de ltar kho mo chos snang ba'i sgo sems can thams cad yongs su ston pa rnam pa de lta bu yongs su sbyong zhing dge ba'i rtsa ba bstsags pa'i tshogs la sta gon tu gnas pas rnam pa bcus chos kyi dbyings la rnam par blta
42b4(phal chen): zhing khong du chud pa dang / rjes su gzhol bar byed do/ /bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ ye shes snang ba shin tu yangs pa thob pas chos kyi dbyings ni tshad med par khong du chud par byed do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa
42b5(phal chen): thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni mtha' dang dbus med par khong du chud par byed do/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad yongs su gnan pa dang / de bzhin
42b6(phal chen): gshegs pa mchod cing rim gror bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni mu med par khong du chud par byed do/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongasu bstan pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings
42b7(phal chen): ni sa mtshams med pa khong du chud par byed do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor tha mi dad pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir/ chos kyi dbyings ni ris chad med par khong du chud par byed do/ /
42b8(phal chen): bsam pa ji lta bar sems can thams cad kyis rnam par dmigs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung gi dkyil 'khor la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur par
43a1(phal chen): khong du chud par byed do/ /'gro ba thams cad rnam par gtul ba mthar phyin pas/ de bzhin gshegs pas sngon gyi smon lam gyi mthar thug pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir/ chos kyi dbyings
43a2(phal chen): ni rang bzhin gyi rgya cher khong tu chud par byed do/ /byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa 'byam klas pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir/ chos kyi dbyings ni 'gro ba thams cad la mnyam pa nyid du gyur
43a3(phal chen): par khong du chud par byed do/ /kun tu bzang po'i spyod pas rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyan la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni rgyan gcig tu gyur par khong du chud par byed do/ /dge ba thams cad kyi
43a4(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings rgyas par dgang zhing rnam par dag par bya ba'i chud mi za ba'i chos can du bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni thug pa med par khong du chud par bya'o/ /rigs kyi bu de ltar kho mo rnam pa bcu po de dag
43a5(phal chen): gis dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / tshogs thams cad yongs su bstsags pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba nyid la 'jug par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab pa rjes su rtogs par
43a6(phal chen): bya ba'i phyir/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad la rnam par blta'o/ /khong du chud pa dang rjes su gzhol bar byed do/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang kho mo de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i bdag nyid che ba nyid kyi rjes
43a7(phal chen): su 'brang ba'i yid la bya ba dang ldan pas/ gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyud stong phrag bcus sems can rnams la chos ston te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar chos rgya mtsho thams cad yang dag par
43a8(phal chen): 'du ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / chos thams cad byin gyis rlab pa'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / chos kyi sprin thams cad yongs su 'dzin pa'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor
43b1(phal chen): dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dgongs pa sgron ma'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / sems can thams cad kyi las rgya 'tsho rab tu snang bar byed pa'i snying po'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor
43b2(phal chen): dang / theg pa'i tshul rgya mtsho dri ma med pa thams cad yang dag par gzhol ba'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / sangs rgyas rgya mtsho thams cad kyi sgron ma'i snying po'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / de bzhin gshegs
43b3(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi mtshan gyi 'khor lo'i glong rab tu sgrog pa'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas sngon gyi smon lam rgya 'tsho bstan pa la yang dag par gzhol ba'i gzungs kyi
43b4(phal chen): dkyil 'khor dang / chos thams cad la mngon par 'khyil pa'i shugs drag po'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi shugs rab tu 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi dkyil
43b5(phal chen): 'khor dang / rigs kyi bu gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor bcu po de dag la stsogs pa gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyud stong phrag bcus sems can rnams la chos ston to/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang
43b6(phal chen): kho mo ni thos pa'i shes rab kyis sems can rnams la chos ston to/ /bsam pa'i shes rab dang / bsgom pa'i shes rab kyis sems can rnams la chos ston to/ /srid pa'i rgyud gcig las kyang
43b7(phal chen): brtsam shing sems can rnams la chos ston to/ /srid pa'i rgyud rgya mtsho thams cad las kyang brtsams shing sems can rnams la chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gis mtshan gyi 'khor lo rgya
43b8(phal chen): mtsho las kyang brtsam shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mtshan gyi 'khor lo rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gcig las kyang
44a1(phal chen): brtsams shing chos ston to/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /sangs rgyas gcig gis lung bstan pa las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin
44a2(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi lung bstan pa rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin
44a3(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi chos kyi 'khor lo las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin
44a4(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /mdo sde gcig las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi
44a5(phal chen): 'khor lo la yang dag par gzhol ba'i mdo sde las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor kun nas 'dus pa las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /
44a6(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor kyi dkyil 'khor kun nas 'dus pa rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems gcig las kyang brtsams shing
44a7(phal chen): chos ston to/ /byang chub kyi sems kyi yan lag rgya mtsho thams cad las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /theg pa gcig las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /theg pa thams cad kyi 'byung ba rgya mtsho
44a8(phal chen): las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /rigs kyi bu de ltar kho mos bstan pa'i tshul mngon par bsgrub pa brjod du med pas sems can rnams la chos ston te/ rigs kyi bu de ltar kho mo chos kyi dbyings kyi
44b1(phal chen): tshul mi tha dad pas de bzhin gshegs pa rgya mtsho la 'jug cing sems can thams cad la chos ston pas/ bla na med pa'i yongs su bsdu ba byed cing byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa la phyi
44b2(phal chen): ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa rgya mtshor gnas par bya ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa 'di la sems kyi skad cig re
44b3(phal chen): r e zhing rnam par 'phel ba'i rnam par thar pa'i yul sgom pa'i tshul gyis yongs su sgom ste rnam par thar pa'i yul sgom pa'i tshul re res kyang sems kyi skad cig re re la chos kyi dbyings
44b4(phal chen): thams cad du rgyas par 'gengs so/ /nor bzangs kyis smras pa/ lha mo byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa de/ de ltar zab mo ngo mtshar che na/ 'phags ma khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa'i
44b5(phal chen): rnam par thar pa 'di brnyes nas ji srid cig lags smras pa/ rigs kyi bu sngon 'das pa'i dus bskal pa 'jig rten gyi rgyud kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa'i pha rol gcig tu 'jig rten
44b6(phal chen): gyi khams chos kyi 'od 'phro ba'i grong khyer dpal gyi sprin ces bya ba rin po che'i spos thams cad dang ldan pa/ gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi spro ba blangs pa/
44b7(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngon gyi smon lam dbyangs su sgrog pa'i pad mos mtshams rnam par brgyan pa/ lhun sems can thams cad kyi las rgya mtshos byung ba'i nor bu rin po che'i rgyal
44b8(phal chen): po rgya mtsho las grub pa/ pad mo chen po'i dbyibs su 'dug pa/ rnam par dag cing kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa/ me tog gi 'khor yug ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis kun nas
45a1(phal chen): bskor ba/ spos kyi rin po che ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi rgyan ri rab ltar mngon par 'phags pa dang ldan pa/ gling bzhi pa chen po'i ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi rgyan
45a2(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ gling bzhi pa re re zhing yang grong brdal bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dang ldan pa byung ngo / /rigs kyi bu 'jig rten gyi khams de'i bskal pa mdog dri
45a3(phal chen): ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba byung ste/ bskal pa de la de bzhin gshegs pa ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ngo / /'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi 'od 'phro ba'i grong khyer dpal gyi sprin gyi gling bzhi
45a4(phal chen): pa dbus ma rgyan mtshan sna tshogs shes bya ba byung ste/ de'i dbus na rgyal po'i gnas rin chen me tog kun nas snang ba zhes bya ba yod par gyur te/ rgyal po'i gnas de dang ha cang yang mi ring ba zhig na snying po
45a5(phal chen): byang chub kyi chos kyi rgyal po'i pho brang rab tu snang ba zhes bya ba yod do/ /snying po byang chub de la de bzhin gshegs pa ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed po de dag gi bskal pa dang po la de bzhin gshegs pa

45a7(phal chen): chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi dbyangs 'od kyi rgyal po las mdo sde chos thams cad kyi klong rgya mtsho zhes bya ba yongs su bzung ste/ bzung nas kyang chos kyi 'khor lo rjes su bskor to/ /yongs su mya ngan las
45a8(phal chen): 'das nas kyang rab tu byung ste/ bstan pa yongasu bzung ngo / /bstan pa nub du cha ste/ bstan pa yang stong du gyis/ chos bstan pa shin tu bstan pa'i tshul ni brgya phrag bcur gyur to/ /rnyog pa'i bskal
45b1(phal chen): pa bar ma dor nye bar gnas par gyur pa'i tshe/ sems can las dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pas sgribs pa/ 'thab mo dang rtsod pa dang / dkrug ma la zhugs par gyur pa dang / dge slong sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i
45b2(phal chen): yon tan don du mi gnyer cing yul gyi dga' ba lhur len par gyur pa/ rgyal po dang rkun po'i gtam la zhugs pa/ bud med dang yul dang / rgya mtsho'i gtam la zhugs pa/ bud med dang yul dang / rgya mtsho'i gtam la mos pa 'jig rten rgyang phan
45b3(phal chen): pa'i tshig la zhugs pa rnams yongs su skyo ba bskyed pa'i phyir/ kye ma'o bskal pa du mar yongs su bsgrubs pa'i chos kyi sgron ma chen po ni nub par gyur ma khad do/ /zhes chos dang ldan pa'i 'o dod bos te/ yongs su

45b5(phal chen): gyi dra ba'i rgyan chen po kha dog sna tshogs dang ldan pa bkye nas/ 'od kha dog du ma dang ldan pas 'jig rten gyi nyon mongs pa'i gdung ba zhi bar byas te/ sems can mtha' dang dbus med pa dag
45b6(phal chen): kyang byang chub la rab tu bkod do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa de yang phyir gsal bar byas te/ lo stong phrag drug bcur gnas par gyur te/ de'i tshe 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po
45b7(phal chen): nyi ma ltar bzhin mdog dri ma med pa/ de nyid kyi bu mo dge slong ma chos kyi 'khor los sprul pa'i 'od ces bya ba dge slong ma brgya phrag stong gi 'khor dang ldan pa byung ste/ des yongs su
45b8(phal chen): skyo bar 'gyur ba'i sgra de thos nas cho 'phrul chen po de mthong ste/ 'khor dang bcas pas byang chub tu sems bskyed nas/ dge slong ma brgya phrag stong po de dag kyang bla na med
46a1(phal chen): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par byas te/ de bzhin gshegs pa mngon du 'gyur ba la yang dag par gzhol ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang rab

46a5(phal chen): pas de la de bzhin gshegs pa chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi dbyangs 'od kyi rgyal po'i rnam par 'phrul pa de dag thams cad kyang mngon du gyur to/ /rigs kyi bu de la ji snyam du sems/ de'i

46a8(phal chen): zhig yin pa snyam du sems na ni/ rigs kyi bu khyod kyi de ltar mi lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po ni de'i tshe de'i dus na 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po nyi ma ltar bzhin mdog dri ma

50a1(phal chen): pa'i 'od ces bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan yid du 'ong ba'i me tog gi yan lag shin tu rgyas pa zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin
50a2(phal chen): gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi dbang po dam pa'i 'od kyi dbyangs zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa chos thams cad ting nge 'dzin gyi 'od kyi dbyangs shes bya ba
50a3(phal chen): bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi sgo'i dbyangs mang po'i mdzod ces bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa chos 'bar ba'i 'od 'phro rgya mtsho'i
50a4(phal chen): dbyangs shes bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa dus gsum gyi mtshan ma rab tu snang ba'i gzi brjid ces bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs
50a5(phal chen): pa chos kyi dkyil 'khor dpal gyi ri bo snang ba'i 'od ces bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi seng ge'i 'od ces bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin
50a6(phal chen): gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad dpal gyi ri rab ces bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho thams cad snang bar mdzad pa'i seng ge zhes
50a7(phal chen): bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes kyi 'od kun tu snang ba zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa shes rab kyi 'od kun tu gsal
50a8(phal chen): ba'i chos kyi grong khyer rab tu snang ba zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur to/ /de ltar rigs kyi bu sangs rgyas brgya po 'di dag la stsogs pa/ bskal pa mdog dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba la de bzhin
50b1(phal chen): gshegs pa ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed gcig byung te/ rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed po de dag thams cad kyi tha mar de bzhin
50b2(phal chen): gshegs pa chos kyi grong khyer ye shes kyi 'od kyis rab tu snang ba'i rgyal po zhes bya ba byung bar gyur te/ de ltar rigs kyi bu kho mos de bzhin gshegs pa ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra
50b3(phal chen): b a snyed po de dag las chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi dbyangs kyi 'od kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba la stsogs pa tha ma chos kyi dbyings kyi grong khyer ye shes kyi 'od kyi rab tu snang ba'i bar de dag thams
50b4(phal chen): cad kho mos mchod do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad la kho mos rim gror byas so/ /thams cad kyi chos bstan pa yang thos so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams
50b5(phal chen): cad kyi bstan pa la 'ang kho mos rab tu byung ngo / /de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad kyi bstan pa yang kho mos yongs su bzung ngo / /byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar
50b6(phal chen): pa sgra yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa 'di yang de bzhin gshegs pas de dag thams cad las thob pa'i tshul rnam pa sna tshogs kyis rab tu thob bo/ /
50b7(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad kyi zhabs kyi drung du 'ang kho mos sems can rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus med pa yongs su smin par byas so/ /de tshun chad du bskal pa sangs rgyas
50b8(phal chen): kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la de bzhin gshegs pa ji snyed cig byung bar gyur pa de dag thams cad ni kho mos chos gyi nan tan gyis mchod pa byas te/ rigs kyi bu de phyin chad tu kho mos
51a1(phal chen): sems can 'khor ba'i mun pa na 'khod cing mi shes pa'i gnyid kyi logs pa rnams kyi mel tshe cher byas so/ /de dag gi sems kyi grong khyer yang yongs su bsrungs so/ /de dag
51a2(phal chen): khams gsum gyi grong khyer nas gyen du bskyod cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi grong rdal du yang rab tu bkod do/ /rigs kyi bu kho mos byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong ba
51a3(phal chen): dang / rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa 'jig rten gyi tshig khyal pa rnam par bzlog pa/ gnyis su smra ba med pa la rab tu bkod do/ /bden pa la rab tu gzhog pa'i mthar phyin pa 'di
51a4(phal chen): shes par zad na/ kho mos byang chub sems dpa' dag gi lam gyi rang bzhin thams cad thogs pa med par shes pa/ sems kyi skad cig re re la chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya
51a5(phal chen): bar dbang bsgyur ba/ sems can thams cad kyi sgra skad dang / tshig rgya mtsho la zhugs pa/ skad rgya mtsho thams cad mngon par 'du bya ba la mkhas pa/ chos thams cad kyi grangs dang ming rgya
51a6(phal chen): mtsho'i tshul dang / cho ga la mkhas pa/ chos thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba'i gzungs rgya mtsho la dbang bsgyur ba/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin tu chos kyi sprin
51a7(phal chen): mngon par bsgrub pa la mkhas pa/ sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul bar spyod pa'i mthar phyin par byed pa de dag gi spyod pa shes pa 'am/ yon tan brjod par
51a8(phal chen): 'am/ sems can thams cad yongs su sdud pa'i nan tan shes par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam bla na med par brtsams pa'i sbyor ba 'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i ye
51b1(phal chen): shes shin tu phra ba khong du chud pa 'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi gter dang / mdzod rnam par 'byed pa'i khyu mchog gis mthu 'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi stan la seng
51b2(phal chen): ge'i khri yongs su gtan par bya ba shes par nus re skan de ci'i phyir zhe na/ skyes bu dam pa de dag ni chos thams cad kyi sa'i dkyil 'khor gyi gzungs su gnon pa sha stag dag go/ /song
51b3(phal chen): rigs kyi bu bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi zhabs kyi drung 'di nyid du mtshan mo lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas par bde bar gnas pa zhes bya ba 'dug ste/ kho mo dang rgyang
51b4(phal chen): mi ring ba zhig na 'dug gis/ de'i gan du song ba la ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa dang / ji ltar nan tan du byed cing sems can thams
51b5(phal chen): cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'gro ba byed pa dris shig / de nas mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrungs ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyis de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa'i rnam
51b6(phal chen): par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa 'di nyid bstan te/ brtan pa'i phyir tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ rnam thar
51b7(phal chen): gang gis dus gsum rgyal ba ma lus dang / /chos dbyings kun tu 'byam klas mtha' dang dbus med pa/ /shes byed mtshan nyid kun gyi gzhir thug rtogs pa yi/ /rgyal sras
51b8(phal chen): rnams kyi rnam thar zab cing blta bar dka'/ /tshogs las byung ba'i rnam thar tshul ni mtha' yas te/ /chos nyid thos pas tshad med bsam du med pa yin/ /yongasu 'phel zhing kun tu chags
52a1(phal chen): med shugs drag par/ /dus gsum byams pa'i tshul gyis lam la 'jug par gyis/ /'di ltar sangs rgyas zhing rgyud rdul phran rab snyed kyi/ /bskal pa 'das pa'i snga
52a2(phal chen): rol sngon gyi zhing byung ba/ /'jig rten khams ni chos 'od sprin gyi dpal/ /bskal pa 'byung ba dri med mdog tu 'od chen no/ /bskal pa de gcig rgyal ba'i gdung ni rgyun ma chad/ /sangs
52a3(phal chen): rgyas ri rab rdul phran rab snyed byung bar 'gyur/ /bde gshegs chos kyi rgya mtsho 'od dbyangs rgyal po ni/ /thog mar byung ste de dag bskal pa dang po pa/ /rgyal ba chos sprin grong khyer 'od
52a4(phal chen): snang rgyal po ni/ /bde gshegs de dag kun gyi tha mar 'jig rten byung / /de dag kun gyi spyan sngar phyin te kho mos mchod/ /de dag kun las chos kyang dga' ba chen pos thos/ /
52a5(phal chen): kho mos thog mar mthong ba gser mdog 'od mnga' ba/ /rgya mtsho'i chos 'od sgrogs pa'i gsung gi rgyal po ste/ /mtshan rab sum bcu gnyis kyis yongs brgyan ri bo 'dra/ /mthong
52a6(phal chen): nas bdag ni bde gshegs 'gyur snyam blo gros gyur/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de ni kho mos mthong mod la/ /thams cad mkhyen nyid 'byam klas 'byung ba'i rgyu rkyen gyis/ /mkha' dbyings rnam
52a7(phal chen): yangs de bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin can/ /rgyal ba'i sems kyi dang po stobs ldan rab tu skyes/ /snying rje bdud rtsi'i rgya mtsho che las byung ba des/ /dus gsum gshegs pa'i bde bar
52a8(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kun/ /rgyal sras rgya mtshos bskor ba ma lus thams cad dang / /sems can rgya mtshor bcas pa'i rgya mtsho'i zhing yang rgyas/ /lus kyis zhing rnams thams
52b1(phal chen): cad ma lus khyab bya dang / /'gro ba kun gyi bsam pa bzhin tu lus bstan phyir/ /zhing rnams ma lus bskyod cing snang bar bya ba dang / /'gro ba smin bya'i don du bdag gis sems
52b2(phal chen): kyang bskyed/ /rgyal ba gnyis pa'i spyan sngar kho mo phyin nas kyang / /zhing rnams rgya mtsho bcu bzhugs rgyal ba'i dbang po mthong / /rgya ba tha ma mthong nas zhing gi rgya mtsho rnams/ /rgya
52b3(phal chen): mtsho'i zhing gi rdul phran rab bsnyed bzhugs pa mthong / /de yi tshu rol bskal pa zhing rgyud rtul snyed tu/ /rgyal ba 'gro ba'i sgron ma ji snyed skyes gyur pa/ /de dag thams cad
52b4(phal chen): spyan sngar kho mo phyin gyur te/ /rnam thar rgya mtsho'i tshul 'di spyod tshe mchod pa byas/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong ba dang /
52b5(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa thob pa ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus med pa la zhugs pa/ gzungs kyi sgo rgya mtsho rgya chen po las byung ba'i sems dang ldan
52b6(phal chen): pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa'i snang ba chen po rab tu thob pa/ so so yang dag par rig pa chen po rgya mtsho la zhugs pa'i/ dga' ba'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs
52b7(phal chen): pa rnam par 'phel ba'i sems dang ldan pa des/ mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba'i gzi brjid dpal la tshul dang 'thun pa'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod
52b8(phal chen): do/ /khyod kyi shes rab chos yangs rgya mtsho kun la spyod/ /srid pa'i rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus med khyod kyi sbyangs/ /ye shes lus mchog snying po tshe ring snyengs bral ba/ /lha mo khyod ni 'khor
53a1(phal chen): 'dir byon cing rnam par mdzes/ /chos kyi rang bzhin nam mkha' lta bu thugs chud do/ /dus gsum kun gyi tshul yang chags med thugs chud mdzad/ /thugs kyi skad
53a2(phal chen): cig gcig la tshad med bsam yas pa'i/ /dmigs pa thams cad rtog pa mi mngar 'jal bar mdzad/ /ye shes spyan mnga' chos nyid sems can med gzigs kyang / /sems can rgya mtsho
53a3(phal chen): mtha' yas thugs rjes gzigs pa mdzad/ /thugs kyi rnam thar shin tu yangs la 'jug mdzad cing / /sems can tshad med 'dul zhing yongs su smin par mdzad/ /khyod ni chos kyi dkyil 'khor
53a4(phal chen): rnams spyad tshul mkhyen te/ /chos kyi rang bzhin shes bya'i tshul la rnam sangs rgyas/ /'phags lam dri ma med pa thams cad yongs sgom ste/ /'gro ba ma lus rnam par sbyong zhing
53a5(phal chen): yongs su 'byung / /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dri med rtogs mdzad pa'i/ /khyod ni sems can rgya mtsho'i mchog las mngon par skyes/ /khyod ni chos dbyings khongs su sems can
53a6(phal chen): kun khyab par/ /chos rab bstan cing 'jig rten 'jigs pa zhi bar mdzad/ /khyod ni rnam par snang mdzad smon lam lam tshul gyis/ /yang dag bzhud cing chags med blo yang dri
53a7(phal chen): med ldan/ /thams cad bgrod pa'i rgyal ba'i stobs ni thugs chud cing / /zhing rnams kun gyi rgyal ba rnam par 'phrul pa gzigs/ /khyod kyi thugs ni mkha' 'dra
53a8(phal chen): thub par dka' ba ste/ /nyon mongs kun gyi dri mas ma gos snga nas dag /der ni dus gsum byung ba'i zhing rnams thams cad dang / /sangs rgyas sras
53b1(phal chen): dang bcas pa sems can kun bcas 'dus/ /skad cig gcig gis nyin mtshan yud du zla ba dang / /skad cig yud tsam lo dang 'du 'jig bskal pa dang / /bskal pa rgya mtsho mi grangs rgya mtshor bcas pa dang / /
53b2(phal chen): 'gro ba rnams kyi 'du shes rgya mtsho 'ang thugs su chud/ /phyogs rnams kun gyi sems can skye mched ji snyed dang / /gzugs yod pa dang gzugs med 'du shes yod med
53b3(phal chen): kyi/ /rnam spyod bden pa'i tshul ni thugs su chud mdzad cing / /de dag lam bstan byang chub mngon du dgod par mdzad/ /rnam par snang mdzad smon lam dri ba'i rigs las 'byung / /
53b4(phal chen): bde gshegs kun gyi sku gcig tshul las yang dag rnam par 'khrungs/ /chos sku yongs dag thugs la chags mi mnga'/ /'jig rten kun tu sku gzugs yid bzhin
53b5(phal chen): ston pa mdzad/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal la tshul dang 'dra ba'i tshigs su bcad pa de dag
53b6(phal chen): gis mngon par bstod de/ mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/
53b7(phal chen): mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas te/ /yang dang yang bltas nas
53b8(phal chen): mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi drung nas song ngo / / //sangs rgyas rmad ga cad
54a1(phal chen): ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po bzhi pa/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgo
54a2(phal chen): yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa de/ de las kyang rgya cher bsgom pa dang / yid ches par bya ba dang / shin tu rgyas par byed cing / mtshan
54a3(phal chen): mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pa gang na ba der phyin nas/ mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde gnas pa spos rin po che thams
54a4(phal chen): cad kyi shing yal ga'i khang pa brtsegs pa zhig na/ seng ge'i khri rin po che shing gi myu gu'i snying po can zhig la 'dug ste/ mtshan mo'i lha mo stong phrag bcus kun
54a5(phal chen): nas bskor cing 'dug pa mthong ngo / /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs gyis mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pa'i rkang pa gnyis la
54a6(phal chen): spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ mdun du 'dug nas thal mo sbyar te 'di skad ces smras so/ /lha mo bdag gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed na ji
54a7(phal chen): ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa dang / ji ltar spyod pa dang / ji ltar slob cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'byung ba bdag la
54a8(phal chen): bshad du gsol/ de skad ces smras pa dang / mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gshegs pas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs
54b1(phal chen): la 'di skad ces smras so/ /rig kyi bu kho mo'i mthus ni mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na nyi ma nub du cha ba'i tshe/ pad mo shin tu rgyas pa rnams kyang rnam par
54b2(phal chen): 'dzum par 'gyur ro/ /skyes pa dang bu med bza' shing gi ra ba na gnas shing / dga' bar rtse ba la brtson pa dag kyang khyim du 'dong ba'i blo bskyed do/ /lam srang
54b3(phal chen): na rgyu ba'i sems can rnams kyang zhagis gnas sems shing tshol te 'gro ba gnas thams cad du mngon par gzhol bar 'gyur ro/ /nags tshal dang gseb dang /
54b4(phal chen): phug la rten pa'i sems can rnams kyang nags tshal dang gseb dang phug du 'dong ngo / /shing la gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyang shing gi gnas la brten par mngon par
54b5(phal chen): gzhol lo/ /khung na gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyang khung du 'dong ngo grong dang grong khyer dang / ljongs dang yul la gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyang grong khyer dang ljongs dang
54b6(phal chen): yul du 'dong ngo / /chu na gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyang chur 'dong ngo / /phyogs gzhan gyi yul du phyin pa'i sems can rnams kyang nub mo bde zhing dga' bar gnas pa'i don du
54b7(phal chen): rang rang gis yul gyi phyogs kyi bsam pa bskyed do/ /rigs kyi bu gzhan yang / kho mos ni skye pa dang bu med gzhon nu dar la bab pa/ dar ba'i nyam dod kyis myos pa dang /
54b8(phal chen): glu dang gar dang rol mo'i dga' bas myos pa dang / 'dod pa'i yon tan la dga' zhing / brtson pa rnams la skye ba dang / rga shi dang / gti mug mun pa chen pos 'jig pa gnyen po dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bskyed pa'i phyir/
55a1(phal chen): brtson 'grus gyi legs pa brjod pa dang bsngags pa byed do/ /sems can ser sna dang ldan pa rnams ni sbyin pa la rab tu sbyor ro/ /sems can
55a2(phal chen): tshul khrims ngan pa can rnams ni/ tshul khrims la rab tu 'god do/ /ngan sems dang ldan pa'i sems can de rnams la ni/ byams pa'i legs pa brjod
55a3(phal chen): par byed do/ /sems 'khrugs pa'i sems can rnams ni bzod pa la rab tu 'god do/ /le lo can gyi sems can rnams ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i
55a4(phal chen): brtson 'grus brtsam pa la rab tu 'god do/ /sems can rnam par myos pa'i sems can rnams ni bsam gtan la rab tud 'god do/ /shes rab 'chal ba can gyi
55a5(phal chen): sems can rnams ni bsam gtan la rab tu 'god do/ /theg pa dma' ba la mos pa'i sems can rnams ni theg pa chen po la rab tu 'god do/ /khams gsum la
55a6(phal chen): mngon par zhen pa'i sems can rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa/ srid pa'i lam gyi rgyud mthar phyin pa'i dkyil 'khor la spyod pa la
55a7(phal chen): rab tu 'god do/ /dmigs pa'i dbang du gyur pa'i sems can las dang / nyon mongs pas rab tu mnar ba bsod nams dang / ye shes gyi stobs med pa
55a8(phal chen): rnams ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la rab tu 'god do/ /mi shes pa'i mun nag gis khebs pa'i/ sems can bdag tu bya ba dang /
55b1(phal chen): bdag gir bya bas ma rig pa'i mun nag du 'thoms pa rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la rab tu 'god de/ rigs
55b2(phal chen): kyi bu gzhan yang kho mos ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba'i 'od 'phro ba/ yangs pa yang dag par 'gyur ba thob pa'o/ /nor bzangs kyi smras
55b3(phal chen): pa/ lha mo byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa'i dga' ba'i 'od spro ba yangs pa yang dag par 'byung ba de'i yul ji lta bu zhig mchis smras pa/ rigs kyi bu rnam par thar
55b4(phal chen): pa de ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams gyis sems can yongs su sdud pa'i ye shes dang / thabs snang ba dang ldan pa ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi
55b5(phal chen): bu sems can rnams kyi bde ba nyams su myong ba ji snyed cig yod pa de dag thams cad ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams kyi mthus byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs
55b6(phal chen): pa'i gdams ngag gis tshul gyis byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung la nan tan tu byas pas byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i rjes su bslabs pas
55b7(phal chen): byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyi byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pas bstan pa'i lam la nan tan du byas pas byung ba'o/ /
55b8(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa dang tshul 'dra ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pas byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pas chos bstan pa'i mthun pa'i rgyus byung ba'o/ /de bzhin
56a1(phal chen): gshegs pa'i ye shes gyi nyi ma snang bas byung ba'o/ /rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi chos dkar po'i dkyil 'khor gyis snang
56a2(phal chen): bas ni/ sems can rnams kyi bde ba yongasu 'byung ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar rigs kyi bu kho mos byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar
56a3(phal chen): pa dga' ba'i 'od 'phro ba/ yang dag par 'byung ba 'di la 'jug pa'i tshe/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
56a4(phal chen): pa'i sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad gyi sngon gyi/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho rjes su dran par byed cing 'jug pa dang / khong tu chud par byed pa'i tshe/
56a5(phal chen): 'di ltar bcom ldan 'das sngon byang chub sems dpa'i sa la bzhugs pas/ sems can bdag tu bya ba dang / bdag gir bya ba la mngon par zhen pa/ ma rig
56a6(phal chen): pa'i mun pas 'thoms pa/ lta ba'i thibs po'i dgon par 'khyams pa/ srid pa'i dbang du gyur pa/ 'dod chags kyi bcings pas glags pa/ zhe sdang gis
56a7(phal chen): khong khro ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ gti mug gis sems kyi rgyud 'khrugs par gyur pa/ phrag dog dang ser snas kun nas 'khor ba/ nyon mongs pas rab tu dkrugs
56a8(phal chen): pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal chen po nyams su myong bar gyur pa/ 'khor ba na 'phongs pa'i sdug bsngal gyis rab tu gzir ba/ sangs rgyas
56b1(phal chen): blta ba las phyir phyogs par gyur pa/ thams cad gzigs nas thugs rje chen po'i dgongs pa skyes par gyur to/ /sems can thams cad kyis don du
56b2(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad la yo byad dang / rin po che yongs su bsdu zhing / yongs su bsdud pa'i dgongs pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi mkho ba'i yo byad yongs
56b3(phal chen): su bsgrubs pa'i dgongs pa dang / dngos po thams cad la chags pa mi mnga' ba'i dgongs pa dang / yul thams cad la yi brngam pa mi mnga' ba'i dgongs pa dang /
56b4(phal chen): dga' ba thams cad la chags pa mi mnga' ba'i dgongs pa dang / longs spyod thams cad la yongs su ma zhen pa'i dgongs pa dang / sbyin pa thams cad la rnam par
56b5(phal chen): smin pa la re ba med pa'i dgongs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi phun sum tshogs pa thams cad la bzhed pa mi mnga' ba'i dgongs pa dang / rgyu dang rkyen la ma rmongs pa'i
56b6(phal chen): dgongs pa dang / legs par 'tshal ba'i chos la yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du mkhyen pa'i dgongs pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi don la gzhol bar bya
56b7(phal chen): ba la mngon par bsgrub pa'i dgongs pa yang dag par skyes par gyur te/ de de ltar chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin la yang dag par zhugs pa'i dgongs pa dang

57a1(phal chen): ba'i sbyor ba mnga' ba sems can gyi 'jig rten thams cad kun nas khebs pa'i chos kyi gdugs chen po'i dkyil 'khor mnga' ba/ sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i
57a2(phal chen): ri rnam par 'joms pa'i ye shes rdo rje'i mtshon cha mnga' ba/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi bde ba yongs su bsgrub pas dgyes pa'i shugs rnam par 'phel ba'i dgongs pa mnga' ba/
57a3(phal chen): sems can thams cad la bde ba phul du phyin pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i smon lam gyi dgongs pa mnga' ba/ bsam pa dang smon pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems can thams cad la nor gyi
57a4(phal chen): char rab tu dbab pa'i dgongs pa mnga' ba/ sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong zhing snyoms par sbyar ba'i dgongs pa mnga' ba/ 'phags pa'i nor gyis sems can thams
57a5(phal chen): cad tshim par mdzad pa'i dgongs pa mnga' ba/ stobs bcu'i ye shes rin po che phul du dri ma med pa thob par mdzad pa'i dgongs pa mnga' ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes
57a6(phal chen): p a chen po'i stobs dang shugs rab tu brnyes pa de byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul ba sna tshogs kyi sprin chen pos sems can gyi khams chos kyi dbyings kyi klas pa nam mkha'i mthas
57a7(phal chen): gtugs pa thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ sems can thams cad la mngon par gyur par bzhugs shing sbyin pa'i dmigs pa thams cad kyi sprin kyi char chen po rnam pa thams cad du dbab pa dang /
57a8(phal chen): rin po che'i rgyan thams cad kyi sprin chen po'i char mngon par 'bebs pa mdzad de/ 'di ltar sems can thams cad so so'i tshul dang ji ltar 'thun pas longs spyod par bya ba'i phyir dngos
57b1(phal chen): po rnam pa tha dad pa mtha' yas pa yongs su gtang ba dang yo byad rnam pa tha dad pa tshad med pa la spyod pa bya ba dang sbyin pa rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad kyis yongs su bsdu ba'i tshul dang / dngos po yongs su gtang ba rnam pa
57b2(phal chen): du ma la yongs su spyod pa dang / yo byad kyi rnam pa dang / rgyan gyi 'du byed brjod du med pa dang / sbyin pa'i tshogs rnam pa sna tshogs mtshan nyid sna tshogs dang ldan pa/ sems can rnams bsam pa ci
57b3(phal chen): l ta ba bzhin du yongs su tshim par bya ba'i sbyin pa'i tshul mtha' yas pa thugs su chud pas sems can gyi bsam pa ci lta ba bzhin du yongs su tshim par bya bar mngon par bsgrub pa'i dngos po thams
57b4(phal chen): cad btang ba dang / yongs su gtang ba dang / sbyin par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal rgyun mi chad pa las yongs su skyob pa'i tshul du bya ba rnams/ sems
57b5(phal chen): can thams cad la lan la re ba mi mnga' ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad la mnyam pa nyid du byung ba'i dgongs pa mnga' bas/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi sems rin po che yongs su sbyong ba mdzad cing sangs
