57b8(phal chen): smyin par bya ba dang / gdul ba gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir mngon par bsgrub par mdzad pa dang / dgongs pa'i skad
58a1(phal chen): c ig re re la zhing gcig nas gcig tu bsgyur ba ma lus pa thams cad sangs rgyas kyi zhing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa'i bla na med pa'i rgyan rnam par dag pas rnam par klub
58a2(phal chen): cing rab tu brgyan pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la chos kyi tshul rgya mtsho ma lus pa thams cad rgyas par dgang ba rnams dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la nam mkha'i
58a3(phal chen): dbyings kyis gtugs pa ma lus pa thams cad rgyas par dgang ba'i ye shes kyi tshul yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la sems can dang dus ma lus pa
58a4(phal chen): thams cad la 'jug cing ye shes kyi tshul rnam par dag par bya ba dang / dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad rnam par 'dul ba'i ye shes kyi tshul snang ba rab tu
58a5(phal chen): thob par bya ba dang / dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la dus ma lus pa thams cad du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba las phyir mi ldog par bya ba dang / dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la thams cad
58a6(phal chen): mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi byin gyis brlabs la mkhas pa ma lus par yongs su bstan pas 'gro ba thams cad la thogs par bya ba dang / dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la 'jig rten gyi khams
58a7(phal chen): ma lus pa'i grangs su bya ba'i rgyud dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad mngon par bstan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su 'du ba/ 'jig rten gyi
58a8(phal chen): khams 'byam klas pa sna tshogs brjod du yod pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud rnam par gnas pa sna tshogs kyi mtshams rnam par brgyan pa/ gzhi sna tshogs dang lhun du mar brjod du yod pa rnam par
58b1(phal chen): phye ba sna tshogs kyis bskal pa rnam pa tha dad pa bstan du yod pa/ kun nas nyon mongs shing rnam par dag pa dang rnam par dag cing kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / gcig tu yongs su dag pa dang gcig tu kun nas
58b2(phal chen): nyon mongs pa dang che ba dang yangs pa dang / tshad med pa dang dog pa dang phra ba dang rgya che ba dang / gzhi mnyam pa dang snrel gzhi dang spyi'u tshugs dang / phyogs dang phyogs mtshams su mngon par bltas pa dang /
58b3(phal chen): phyogs rgya mtsho sna tshogs su gzhol ba sgo sna tshogs nas bstan cing sgo mtha' yas pa'i dbyibs rnam pa sna tshogs su 'dug pa'i rnam par phye ba sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
58b4(phal chen): rnams su byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyad de/ byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa yongs su mnan nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pas rgyas par dgang par bya ba dang /
58b5(phal chen): dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las ma lus pa thams cad sems can pha rol gyi sems dang bsam pas rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i phyir 'gro ba thams
58b6(phal chen): cad la thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams rgya mtsho'i shugs rnam par 'phel bar mdzad de/ mngon par bsgrub pa mdzad par gyur pa mngon par shes so rjes su dran no/ /rigs kyi bu de ltar
58b7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mdzad pa'i tshe/ 'jig rten gnas pa bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs dang bral ba/ sems
58b8(phal chen): can byas pa drin du mi gzo bas yongs su gang ba/ mi shes pa'i mun pas chod pa/ bdag tu bya ba dang / bdag gir bya ba la mngon par zhen pa ma rig pa'i mun pa dang rab rib kyis bsgribs pa
59a1(phal chen): tshul bzhin ma yin par rnam par rtog pa la zhugs pa/ lta ba thibs po'i dgon par mgo rlag pa/ rgyu dang 'bras bu la mgo rmongs pa nyon mongs pa dang las kyi dbang du gyur pa 'khor ba'i
59a2(phal chen): mya ngan chen po'i sdug bsngal gyi sa'i 'og tu ltung ba/ phongs pa'i sdug bsngal nyams su myong bar gyur pa rnams la thugs rje chen po bskyed de/ pha rol tu phyin pa spyad pa'i sprin rgya chen po mngon
59a3(phal chen): par bsgrubs te dge ba'i rtsa ba la brten par gnas pa yongs su bsngags pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi 'khor ba'i phongs pa'i sdug bsngal rnam par bzlog pa dang / bsod nams dang ye shes kyi
59a4(phal chen): tshogs chen po la mngon par mos par bya ba dang / rgyu'i dkyil 'khor gyi phyogs mngon par bstan pa dang / las dang chos su mi 'gal ba'i phyogs rab tu brjod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi
59a5(phal chen): chos kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su bsdus pa'i phyogs snang bar bya ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi mos pa'i phyogs rab tu brjod par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi zhing
59a6(phal chen): yongs su bsgrub pa'i phyogs legs par bstan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs mi gcod pa'i phyogs kyi rjes su 'brang bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyis
59a7(phal chen): bstan pa'i phyogs yongs su gzung ba dang / myi dge ba'i chos thams cad kyi phyogs rnam par bzlog pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshogs kyi phyogs yongs su brjod pa mdzad de/
59a8(phal chen): pha rol tu phyin pa'i sprin chen pos sems can gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ mngon par bsgrubs nas bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems can tshim par 'gyur bar chos
59b1(phal chen): gyis shin tu bsdu ba la sems can rab tu dgod par mdzad do/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshogs la yang dag par bskul to/ /byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa chen po la rab tu btsud do/ /

59b8(phal chen): thams cad kyi sdug bsngal dang yid mi bde ba rab tu zhi bar bya ba la zhugs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i nan tan la mngon par mos pa/ chos thams cad kyi rang
60a1(phal chen): bzhin nges par rtogs pa nam mkha'i spyod yul dang ldan pa/ mos pa yangs pa'i lam gyis rnam par dag pa/ 'khor ba'i rgyun las phyir phyogs pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes
60a2(phal chen): rgya mtsho la mngon par mos pa chos kyi grong khyer du 'gro bar gcig tu chad pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul yongs su gnon pa'i brtson 'grus can/ sangs rgyas kyis sa'i rgyud rnam par gnon pa
60a3(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i stobs yongs su rdzogs par bya ba la mngon par mos pa/ stobs bcu rab tu thob par bya ba'i mthar thug pa rnams kyi bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs yangs pas nye bar
60a4(phal chen): brten pa'i sems dang bsam pa rnam par dag pa dang ma zhum pa dang nyon mongs pa med pa dang ma yo ba dang ma nyams pa dang / ma 'chums pa dang mun pa med pa'i sems dang ye shes kyi snang ba kun tu snang bas
60a5(phal chen): snang bar 'gyur ba'i sems dang / sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde bar bya bar shin tu 'dun pa'i sems dang / bdud kyi 'khor dang / nyon mongs pa thams cad kyis mi thub pa'i sems
60a6(phal chen): dang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi ye shes thob par bya bar skabs phye ba'i sems kyis khong du chud pa dang yid ches par bya ba dang / gzung ba dang rjes su 'brang bar bya ba 'am shes par bya bar mi nus
60a7(phal chen): so/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu gnas 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi yul te byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis kyang yongs su ma non na/ sems can gzhan thams cad
60a8(phal chen): k yis lta ci zhig smos 'on kyang sems can cang shes rnams kyi bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang dge ba'i rtsa ba la spyod pa'i sems can rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam
60b1(phal chen): pa dbang du 'gyur bar bya ba dang / khyod kyis bsam pa thag pa nas yongs su dris pa'i lung bstan pa'i chos nyid rab tu 'byung ba thob par bya ba'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi brlabs kyis bstan
60b2(phal chen): to/ /de nas mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pas de'i tshe don de nyid la brten te bstan pa'i phyir dus gsum du byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul la
60b3(phal chen): rnam par bltas te/ /tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sangs rgyas sras po khyod kyis gang dris pa/ /de ni bsam yas zab mo sangs rgyas yul/ /bsam yas zhing gi rdul phran
60b4(phal chen): rab snyed kyi/ /bskal pa mang pos de kun brjod myi nus/ /sems can 'dod pa'i sems ldan sdang ba dang / /de bzhin gti mug mun pas bsgribs pa dang / /'chab dang dregs pas bsam

60b7(phal chen): 'du shes phyin ci log gyur pas/ /zhi ba'i sa 'di shes par mi nus so/ /rgyal ba'i yul ni shes dka' zhi ba ste/ /rang bzhin dri med rnam par rtog pa med/ /srid par rten cing 'khor la chags pa

61a1(phal chen): 'dzin pa/ /drang srong de dag yul ni 'di yin no/ /dkar chos rgya mtshos mi ngoms sems ldan zhing / /gang rnams dge ba'i bshes kyis yongs bzung ste/ /thub pa'i stobs la dmigs
61a2(phal chen): pa'i sems sprin can/ /de dag 'di thos bzod pa thob par 'gyur/ /gang rnams bsam pa dri med rnam rtog med/ /bar snang mkha'i bzhin phyogs dang phyogs mtshams su/ /mun pa rnam
61a3(phal chen): bsal blo gros sgron ma'i sprin/ /dri med de dag spyod yul 'di yin no/ /snying rje'i bsam pas 'gro ba rgya mtsho rnams/ /dus gsum byung ba gang rnams rgyas byed cing / /sems can ma lus rjes

61a5(phal chen): la mnyam par zhugs gyur pa/ /chags pa med de spyod yul sa 'di yin/ /nyon mongs med sems skyon med spyod ldan zhing / /gang rnams 'gyod pa rnam bstsal sems ldan te/ /sangs rgyas
61a6(phal chen): gdams ngag nan tan byed ldan pa/ /dri med de dag spyod yul 'di yin no/ /gang rnams mi sgul sems ldan mi bskyod sems/ /chos kyi rang bzhin rtogs pa'i sems ldan zhing / /las kyi rgya
61a7(phal chen): mtsho mi 'gal sems ldan pa/ /mi zad de dag rnam thar 'di yin no/ /gang rnams mi skyo'i sems dang mi ldog sems/ /brtson 'grus mthu dang rtsal du ldan pa rnams/ /thams cad
61a8(phal chen): mkhyen tshogs brtson 'grus mtha' yas pa/ /brtul zhugs bzang ldan de dag yul 'di yin/ /zhi ba'i sems ldan mnyam par bzhag pa gang / /shin tu zhir gyur rims dang bral ba
61b1(phal chen): rnams/ /kun nas bsam gtan yan lag 'tshor spyod pa/ /rab tu zhi ba de dag tshul 'di yin/ /gang rnams chags pa kun las sems grol zhing / /chos kyi rang bzhin khong du chud
61b2(phal chen): sems can/ /rgyal ba'i chos dbyings rtogs par khong chud pa/ /shes rab sgron ma de dag tshul 'di yin/ /sems can rang bzhin rtogs sems ldan gyur cing / /gang rnams srid pa'i
61b3(phal chen): mtsho la chags med sems/ /sems can sems la gzugs brnyan zla 'char ba/ /lam mkhan de dag rnam thar 'di yin no/ /dus gsum 'byung ba'i rgyal ba rgya mtsho rnams/ /
61b4(phal chen): smon lam gangs chen mtsho rgyud skyes pa yi/ /zhing rnams kun tu phyi ma'i mthar spyod pa/ /kun tu bzang po de dag tshul 'di yin/ /gang rnams chos dbyings tshul rnams rgya mtsho yis/ /
61b5(phal chen): 'gro ba rgya mtsho 'du dang 'jig pa yi/ /bskal par bcas pa khong du chud legs rnams/ /rtog med de dag rnam thar 'di yin no/ /zhing rnams kun gyi rdul phran thams cad la/ /sangs
61b6(phal chen): rgyas grangs med shing rgyal drung bzhugs shing / /byang chub 'tshang rgya 'gro 'dul mthong ba yi/ /chags med mig can de dag tshul 'di yin/ /khyod ni bskal pa rgya mtsho rgya chen du/ /dge ba'i
61b7(phal chen): bshes gnyen mang po bsnyen bkur te/ /chos 'dod chos tshol mi skyo 'dir phyin pa/ /thos nas de ni yongs su gzung bar nus/ /khyod kyi bsam pa yongs su sbyang ba'i phyir/ /bde gshegs
61b8(phal chen): byin brlab bsam gyis mi khyab pas/ /rnam par snang mdzad tshad med yul 'di yang / /kho mo'i tshig las chags pa med par 'byung / /rigs kyi bu sngon 'das pa'i dus bskal pa 'jig rten
62a1(phal chen): gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol de'i yang pha snga zhig tu 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gser rin po che'i ri spo rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba byung ste/ rigs kyi bu 'jig rten gyi
62a2(phal chen): khams rgya mtsho'i gser rin po che'i ri spo rnam par snang ba der de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes ri bo'i 'od chos kyi dbyings su snang ba'i gzigs brjid rgyal ba zhes bya ba byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs
62a3(phal chen): pa ye shes kyi ri bo'i 'od chos kyi dbyings su snang ba'i gzi brjid rgyal po de/ sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mdzad pa'i tshe 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gser rin po che'i ri spo rnam par snang
62a4(phal chen): ba zhes bya ba 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i sa dang / ri rdul shin tu phra ba snyed gyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa bstan du yod pa dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud re re zhing yang
62a5(phal chen): b skal pa'i grangs shin tu bstan pa 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang ldan pa bskal pa re re zhing yang bskal pa bar ma shin tu bstan pa du ma dang ldan pa bskal pa bar ma re re zhing yang
62a6(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rnam pa tha dad du bya ba bstan pa du ma dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba dang / rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs bstan du yod pa de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba re re zhing yang mdo sde
62a7(phal chen): yang dag par bstan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed brjod du yod pa mdo sde re re la yang byang chub sems dpa'i lung bstan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i rdul
62a8(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed bstan du yod pa sems can 'dul ba mtha' dang dbus med pa shin tu bstan pa/ theg pa tha dad pa'i tshul gyis bsgrubs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa dang cho 'phrul sna tshogs
62b1(phal chen): gyis rnam par 'dul ba dang ldan pa yongs su sbyangs te/ rigs kyi bu 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gser rin po che'i ri spos rnam par snang ba der/ 'jig rten gyi khams bar ma'i rgyud phyogs kun
62b2(phal chen): tu mngon par ltas pa'i sgo rgyal mtshan gyis rnam par brgyan pa zhes bya ba byung ste/ rigs kyi bu 'jig rten gyi khams bar ma'i rgyud phyogs kun tu mngon par bltas pa rgyal mtshan gyis rnam par
62b3(phal chen): brgyan pa der/ 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che thams cad kyi mdog kun tu snang ba'i dpal zhes bya ba 'jig rten gyi khams kyi gzhi dang / mtshams kyi rgyan rin po che'i rgyal po de dag de bzhin gshegs
62b4(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi snying po byang chub rab tu snang ba las byas pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi me tog rgya mtsho la gnas pa/ lhun rin po che'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sprul pa'i gzugs
62b5(phal chen): brnyan rab tu ston pa las bsgrubs pa/ lha'i grong khyer gyi dbyibs su 'dug pa rnam par dag cing kun nas nyon mongs pa byung bar gyur te/ 'jig rten gyi khams der gling bzhi pa'i 'jig
62b6(phal chen): rten gyi khams ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung bar gyur te/ gling bzhi pa ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed po de dag gi gling bzhi la dbu ma rin po che sna tshogs kyi rtse mo'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya
62b7(phal chen): ba byung ste/ gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che sna tshogs kyi rtse mo'i rgyal mtshan der gling chu zheng du dpag tshad rgya phrag stong yod pa bzhi byung nas gling re re yang grong khyer chen
62b8(phal chen): po stong phrag re re byung ngo / /gling bzhi pa de'i 'dzam bu gling gi dbus su rgyal po'i gnas rin po che'i sa las rnam par rgyan pa/ sprin gyi sgron ma zhes bya ba grong khyer stong phrag
63a1(phal chen): bcu'i 'khor dang ldan pa byung ngo / /de'i 'dzam bu'i gling de'i myi rnams kyang tshe'i tshad lo stong phrag bcu thub par gyur to/ /rgyal po'i gnas rin po che'i sa las rnam par brgyan pa sprin
63a2(phal chen): kyi sgron ma der 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa zhes bya ba byung ste/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i
63a3(phal chen): gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa de'i blon po ni lnga brgya byung ngo / /btsun mo ni stong phrag drug bcu byung ngo / /sras ni kun kyang dpa' ba brtul phod pa/ yan lag dam pa'i gzugs dang ldan
63a4(phal chen): pa/ blta na sdug pa gzi brjid che ba/ stobs che ba brgya phrag bdun byung ngo / /rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa de'i tshe la 'dzam bu'i gling thams cad kyang
63a5(phal chen): gdugs cig gis kyang bskyangs par gyur te/ pha rol gyi 'khor dang dgra thams cad kyang shin tu choms par gyur to/ /de'i tshe 'jig rten gyi khams der skal pa bar ma ni zad du nye/ rnyog pa lnga ni
63a6(phal chen): 'jig rten du byung / dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam ni nub par gyur nas/ sems can mi dge ba bcu'i lam la spyod pa phal cher ngan song du yang 'dong bar gyur te/ de dag myi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam
63a7(phal chen): yongs su 'dzin pa'i rgyus tshe thung ba dang longs spyod chung ba dang gzugs ma legs pa dang / kha dog mi sdug pa dang lus ma legs pa dang / bde ba'i rnam pa nyung ba dang sdug bsngal nyams su myong
63a8(phal chen): ba'i rnam pa mang po dang / phan tshun bslu zhing 'drid pa'i rang bzhin can dang phan tshun dbye ba la zhugs pa dang / zhe gcod pa'i tshigs la spyod pa dang / 'chal ba'i tshig tu smra ba dang / 'dod pa
63b1(phal chen): mi bzad pas zil gyis gnon pa dang zhe sdang ba'i yid gyi rtog pa dang ldan pa dang / lta ba'i thibs po sna tshogs gyi mya ngan du 'khyams par gyur nas de dag chos ma yin pa'i 'dod chags la zhen
63b2(phal chen): cing 'dod pa mi bzad pas zil gyis non la/ log pa'i chos kyis kun nas 'khor bas sa la shing rtsi dang lo zas skye bar 'gyur ba'i char yang dus su mi 'bab par gyur te/ sems can de dag kyang rtsa
63b3(phal chen): dang gel ba dang sman dang nags tshal dang bza' shing ra ba dang sdong po dag kyang skams par gyur nas/ nad sna tshogs gyis thebs shing phyogs dang phyogs mtshams su skyabs med pas/ phan tshun
63b4(phal chen): khod mi snyom zhing g.yen spyod par gyur te de dag kun kyang gcig tu 'dus nas rgyal po'i gnas rin po che sa las rnam par brgyan pa sprin gyi sgron ma gang na ba der dongs ste/ kun nas bskor nas/ la la
63b5(phal chen): ni lag pa gyen du sgreng / la la ni thal mo sbyor/ la la ni lus shin tu 'dar/ la la ni 'gyel/ la la ni bub/ la la ni lus thams cad kyis phab cing phyag 'tshal/ la la ni pus mo sa la
63b6(phal chen): 'dzugs/ la la ni lag pa nam mkha'i dbyings su g.yo ba/ la la ni gos med cing sgren mor 'khod/ la la ni kha mig myi sdug par gyur cing / rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil
63b7(phal chen): 'khor rab tu sgrog pa la mngon tu bltas shing / snying rje rje skad du 'o dod chen po 'bod de/ lha chen po bdag cag ni nyam thag go/ /bkres pa dang skom pa'i sdug bsngal gyis rab tu gzir to/ /'jigs
63b8(phal chen): pa sna tshogs gyis g.yen spyod do/ /bdag cag la skyabs ma mchis so/ /bdag cag la mgon dang dpung gnyen ma mchis so/ /sdug bsngal gyi shing thags kyis 'khor to/ /srog chad la thug
64a1(phal chen): go/ /'chi bar gyur ma khad do/ /zhes te smre sngags sna tshogs su bla zhing dbyangs kyi rnam pa sna tshogs dang / tshig sna tshogs kyis kha gdong mi sdug par gyur par 'du shes dang tshig
64a2(phal chen): sna tshogs kyi tha snyad dang / cho 'brang ba dang skad kyi gdangs don sna tshogs brjod pa'i tshig dang / ngag gis 'o dod bos so/ /rgyal po'i gnas de'i skyes pa dang bu med dang khye'u dang / bu mo bkres
64a3(phal chen): pa dang skom pas mnar ba lus la rgyan med pa sgren mo gos med pa/ kha dog dang mdog mi sdug pa lus sra shing rtsub pa/ sdug bsngal zhing yid mi bde la/ mi dga' ba de dag thams cad kyang bde ba ni
64a4(phal chen): mngon par 'dod/ /sdug bsngal gyi 'jigs pas ni brla khyer nas rgyal po shes pa'i skyes bu chen po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa/ de la bde ba thams
64a5(phal chen): cad thob par bya ba'i 'du shes dang / sdug bsngal thams cad dang mi 'grogs par bya ba'i 'du shes dang / 'tsho ba'i bsam pa dang ldan zhing gter thob par bya ba'i 'du shes dang / mu stegs mthong bar
64a6(phal chen): bya ba'i 'du shes dang / lam chen po la nan tan du bya ba'i 'du shes dang / gru chen po'i 'du shes dang / ye shes kyi gling chen po'i 'du shes dang / don chen po rab tu thob par bya ba'i 'du shes dang /
64a7(phal chen): mtho ris kyi dga' ba dang bde ba thams cad rab tu thob par bya ba'i 'du shes kyis mgon dang skyabs tshol bar gyur to/ /rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu
64a8(phal chen): sgrogs pas 'khor kun nas slong ba mang po snying rje rje skad du 'bod pa'i 'o dod chen po de thos nas/ de snying rje chen po'i sgo brgya stong grangs med pa phrag bcu la zhugs par gyur to/ /de snying rje chen po'i
64b1(phal chen): tshul yid la bab pa'i sems su gyur nas/ yud tsam zhig rtse gcig tu bsams te snying rje chen po dang ldan pa'i tshig bcu brjod do/ /bcu gang zhe na/ kye hud kye sems can 'di dag ni 'khor
64b2(phal chen): ba'i g.yang sa chen por lhung yang skyabs med pa lta na/ bdag nam zhig 'khor ba'i g.yang sa chen por lhung ba'i sems can rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa la 'khod pas gnas
64b3(phal chen): su 'gyur kyi hud kye sems can 'di dag nyon mongs pa'i gnon pas gtses shing skyabs med pa lta na/ nam zhig bdag sems can nyon mongs pa sna tshogs kyis 'jigs pa dang / gnod pas
64b4(phal chen): gtses te skyabs med pa rnams kha na ma tho ba med pa'i las kyi mtha' la 'god pas skyabs su 'gyur/ kyi hud kye sems can 'di dag 'jig rten na rga shi'i 'jigs pas tshar chod
64b5(phal chen): cing mgon med pa lta na nam zhig bdag sems can mgon med pa rnams kyi 'khor ba'i 'jigs pa thams cad rnam par sel bas mgon du 'gyur/ kyi hud kye sems can 'di dag
64b6(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi 'jigs pa sna tshogs kyis gtses te/ rten med pa lta na nam zhig bdag sems can 'jig rten gyi 'jigs pa sna tshogs kyis gtses pa rnams shin tu bde zhing skyon
64b7(phal chen): med pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam la 'god pas rten du 'gyur/ kyi hud kye sems can 'di dag 'jig rten na ma rig pa'i mun par 'thoms te the tsom dang yid gnyis kyi rab
64b8(phal chen): rib gyis bsgribs pa lta na/ nam zhig bdag sems can thams cad gyi ma rig pa'i mun pa rnam par sel bas sgron mar gyur par 'ong / kyi hud kye sems can 'di dag ni
65a1(phal chen): snang ba dang bral ba lta na nam zhig bdag ye shes kyi sgo rab rib med par yongs su ston pas ye shes chen po'i snang ba 'byin par 'gyur/ kyi hud kye sems can 'di dag ni phrag
65a2(phal chen): dog dang 'jungs pa dang / g.yo dang sgyu'i rnyog pas bsam pa rnyog pa can du gyur te/ ye shes kyi mdog gsal ba med pa lta na/ nam zhig bdag sems can thams cad shin tu dag pa la rab
65a3(phal chen): tu 'god cing bla na med pa'i ye shes kyi mdog rab tu gsal bar byed par 'gyur/ kyi hud kye sems can gyi 'jig rten ni 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho'i yul gyi rgyud du zhugs shing 'dren pa med pa lta na/
65a4(phal chen): nam zhig bdag sems can thams cad chos rgya mtsho'i tshul la 'dzud cing 'dren par 'gyur bar 'ong / kyi hud kye sems can gyi 'jig rten ma lus zhing rnam par 'dren pa med pa lta
65a5(phal chen): na/ nam zhig bdag sems can thams cad rnam pa thams cad du yongs su smyin par bya ba dang / rnam par gdul ba la de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs gyi dus las mi 'da'
65a6(phal chen): zhing rnam par 'dren par 'gyur bar 'ong / /kyi hud kye sems can gyi 'jig rten ni dmus long du gyur te/ yongs su 'dren pa med pa lta na/ nam zhig bdag sems can thams cad sgrib
65a7(phal chen): p a med pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi tshul la 'dzud cing yongs su 'dren par 'gyur de skad du des snying rje chen po dang ldan pa'i tshig rnam pa bcu brjod nas rgyal po'i gnas der dril
65a8(phal chen): bu chen po brdungs te/ gtong ba chen po'i rnga bo che yang yongs su brdungs nas/ su ci 'dod pa de la de sbyin gyis 'gro ba thams cad kyang yongs su tshim par bya'o zhes sgra brjod do/ /des
65b1(phal chen): 'dzam bu'i gling thams cad gyi rgyal po'i gnas thams cad dang / grong dang grong khyer dang ljongs dang / yul dang grong rdal thams cad du yo byad thams cad kyi mdzod phye ste/ lam gyi bzhi mdo dang /
65b2(phal chen): lam gyi sum mdo dang srang thams cad du yang yo byad sna tshogs kyi rnam pa mang po bkod de 'gro ba thams cad nye bar 'tsho bar bstabs so/ /mdzod dang bang ba thams cad kyang phye ste/ rin po che'i gter
65b3(phal chen): chen po dang tshogs kyang yongs su bstan to/ /rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs kyi phung po du ma yang spungs so/ /zas dang skom dang / gos dang bzhon pa dang me tog dang / phreng ba dang bdug pa dang byug pa
65b4(phal chen): dang / phye ma dang gos rin po che kha dog sna tshogs kyi mdzod phye nas/ khang pa dang gzhal med khang dang / khyim mang po mal cha dang / stan dang gos kyis yongs su bstan te/ nor dang dbyig thams cad
65b5(phal chen): phun sum tshogs par byas nas/ nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po snang ba'i gzi brjid rnam par bkod pas mun pa rnam par sel ba bshams nas/ des sems can de dag ci 'dod pa'i bsam pa
65b6(phal chen): thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir/ khyim de dag re re yang rang gi lus dang 'dra ba'i sprul pa'i lus mngon par sprul pa kun tu bkod do/ /sems can thams cad kyi nad thams cad gso
65b7(phal chen): ba'i phyir sman pa dang sman dang / rim gro ba dang / 'tsho ba'i yo byad sna tshogs kyi rkyen phun sum tshogs pa yongs su bshams so/ /rin po che sna tshogs gyis ci rigs su bkang
65b8(phal chen): ba dag kyang nye bar bkod do/ /'di ltar rin po che rdo rje'i snod ni spos gyis nor bu rin po che sna tshogs gyis yongs su bkang /
66a1(phal chen): spos kyi nor bu rin po che sna tshogs kyi snod ni gos kha dog dam pa sna tshogs kyis yongs su bkang ngo / /shing rta mang po dbyibs dang / mdog sna tshogs su 'dug pa/ rin po che sna
66a2(phal chen): tshogs gyis rab tu brgyan pa/ rta dang glang po dang ba lang cang shes dang bcas pa/ rin po che shing rta sna tshogs rgyal po'i rkyen du rung ba/ rin po che thams cad kyi rgyan gyis longs spyod dang
66a3(phal chen): ldan pa/ stan sna tshogs bting ba/ rin po che sna tshogs gyis rnam par brgyan pa/ bla re sna tshogs bres pa/ rin po che'i dril bu'i dra ba 'bres pa/ gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang ba dan
66a4(phal chen): bsgreng bas brgyan pa dag gis kyang / yul gyi phyogs gang bar bkod do/ /grong dang grong khyer dang / ljongs dang yul thams cad sbyin par yang 'o dod kyis bsgo'o/ /bza' shing gi ra ba dang /
66a5(phal chen): kun dga' ra ba dang / dka' thub kyi nags tshal sna tshogs yongs su gtang ba dang / khyim dang chung ma dang bu dang bu mo thams cad yongs su gtang ba dang / rin po che rin thang
66a6(phal chen): med pa thams cad yongs su gtang ba dang / rang gi snying dang rkang dang rgyu ma dang mkhal ma dang tshil dang / sha dang khrag dang pags pa dang rka lag dang rna ba dang / mig dang sna dang lce dang so dang /
66a7(phal chen): mchu dang mgo yongs su btang ba dang / phyi nang gi dngos po thams cad rnam pa thams cad du yongs su gtang bar yang 'o dod kyis bsgo'o/ /des yo byad de lta bu yongs su gtang ba'i rnam pa
66a8(phal chen): mang po bshams te bstsogs nas rgyal po'i gnas rin po che'i sa las rnam par brgyan pa/ sprin gyi sgron ma de'i shar phyogs logs na grong khyer rin po che rtse mo'i gzi brjid ces bya ba'i
66b1(phal chen): mdun rol nas gzhi mnyam pa'i phyogs yangs pa chu zheng du rgya che zhing mnyam pa mtho dman med pa/ rnam par dag cing gzhi mnyam pa ngam grog dang g.yang sa dang sdong dum dang / tsher ma dang /
66b2(phal chen): gseg ma dang / gyo mo thams cad med pa rin po che thams cad kyi khams las grub pa gzhi rin po che thams cad las byas shing / rin po che'i rgyal po thams cad bkram pa/ nor bu rin
66b3(phal chen): po che'i rgyan rnam pa du mas brgyan pa rin po che'i me tog sna tshogs gyis gang ba phye ma sna tshogs dri shin tu zhim pa'i rdul ltar bdug spos sna tshogs gyis bdug pa/ rin po che'i
66b4(phal chen): sgron ma dpal gyi gzi brjid can rab tu 'bar ba/ spos dang bdug spos thams cad kyi na bun dang / sprin kyi nam mkha' kun tu khebs pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi shing gi
66b5(phal chen): phreng ba legs par bkye bas mdzes par brgyan pa/ khang pa dang gzhal med khang dang khang pa brtseg pa sna tshogs kyis yongs su brgyan pa/ gdugs dang rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan bsgreng ba rin
66b6(phal chen): po che'i snam bu lding ba/ rnam par snang ba rin po che sna tshogs kyi me tog gi dra bas kun nas khebs pa/ rin po che spos thams cad kyi rgyal po'i dra ba'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor can/
66b7(phal chen): gser gyi dra ba las rin po che'i dril bu 'khrol ba dang ldan pa/ bla re rin po che sna tshogs kyis rnam par mdzes par byas pas khebs par bres pa/ spos kyi rgyal po sna tshogs kyi phye
66b8(phal chen): ma rnam par bkram pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi me tog sil mas dga' dga' ltar gang ba rol mo brdungs pa dang / dkrol ba bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gi sgra skad yid du 'ong ba 'byung ba/
67a1(phal chen): rin po che thams cad kyi rgyan sna tshogs rnam par dag pas rnam par brgyan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i las rnam par smyin pas mngon par grub pa zhig yod pa/ de'i dbus su seng ge'i khri
67a2(phal chen): chen po rin po che sna bcu las grub pa'i sa'i gzhi sna tshogs la gnas pa/ rin po che'i khri 'phang sna tshogs bcu'i 'khor gyis rnam par mdzes par byas pa/ rin po che'i shing yal ga can
67a3(phal chen): bcus stegs bu'i mtshams rnam par grub par klubs pa'i rgyan mdzes pa dang ldan pa/ rdo rje'i 'khor lo'i sa'i gzhi mi shigs pa la rkang pa rab tu rten pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi gzugs dang /
67a4(phal chen): mdog yongs su 'dzin pa'i stan gyi 'khor lo can/ rin po che du ma las byas pa'i spog re'i rgyan brgya phrag du mas brgyan pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi tshom bu rnam pa tha dad pa'i rgyan gyis shin tu
67a5(phal chen): brgyan pa rin po che'i rgyal mtshan kun nas rnam par phye ste/ 'brel bar bsgreng ba rin po che sna tshogs kyi ba dan spyangs pa/ rnam pa tha dad pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ rin po che'i dril bu'i dra bas brgyan
67a6(phal chen): pa'i lha rdzas kyi rin po che sna tshogs dang / gser gyi dra ba sna tshogs rnam par bres pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi me tog gi dra ba dang / rin po che'i rgyal po chen po'i dra ba dang / gos rin po che sna tshogs
67a7(phal chen): dang / rin po che'i dra bas ci rigs su kun nas bkab cing mdzes par byas pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ spos rin po che rnam pa tha dad pa'i tshogs las snyim pas bcus shing spos kyi sprin mngon par
67a8(phal chen): gtor ba/ rin po che'i rgyal po kha dog dang dri bsam gyis mi khyab pa las byung ba'i dbyibs yid du 'ong ba sna tshogs dang / spos thams cad kyi na bun dang sprin 'byung ba/ gam yo nas lha rdzas kyi spos dang /
67b1(phal chen): bdug spos sna tshogs kyis rab tu bdugs pa/ lha rdzas las kyang 'das pa'i stan reg na bde ba kha dog bzang po du ma can legs par gting ba/ lha rdzas kyi rol mo dang glu snyan pa du ma yid du 'ong ba brgya
67b2(phal chen): stong du ma'i sgra kun nas 'byung ba/ rin po che sna tshogs gyi them skas kyi phreng ba ba dan gyis rnam par klubs pas/ rab tu brgyan pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ rin po che'i 'bru'i gzugs rin po che sna tshogs
67b3(phal chen): kyis spras pa rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs kyis rnam par snang bar byed pa'i 'od dang ldan pa mngon par grub ste/ de la rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa/
67b4(phal chen): gzugs bzang ba shin tu mdzes pa/ blta na sdug pa kha dog bzang po dam pa rgyas pa dang ldan pa mi chen po'i mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis rnam par dag pa rab tu thob pa/ rin po che rnam par snang ba'i cod
67b5(phal chen): pan can/ rdo rje mthu bo che ltar 'khrigs shing mi shigs pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ rtsib ma'i mtshams thags bzang zhing brten par 'brel ba/ yan lag dang nying lag thams cad yongs su bzang
67b6(phal chen): ba kun nas bzang ba/ kun nas mdzes pa kun nas sdug pa/ rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa/ chos gyi rgyal po chen po'i rigs su byung ba/ yo byad thams cad la dbang rab tu thob pa/

73b1(phal chen): 'khor lo yang / /khyod kyis byin gyis dril rnams rab tu sgrog /khyod kyi dril sgra thogs pa ma mchis par/ /tshangs dbang lha dbang 'gro ba'i bdag po rnams/ /rang rang las gyi tshul ni
