240b3(phal chen): nyon mongs pa'i 'dam gyi skyon thams cad kyis kun nas nyon mongs par mi 'gyur ro/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ shing gi gzugs mgo gzer gyis btab pa ni yongs su 'gyes par
240b4(phal chen): mi 'gyur te/ bya ba thams cad kyang byed do/ /de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du smon pa'i ye shes kyi lus kyi spyi bor byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i smon lam gyis gzer gyi btab pa yang byang chub
240b5(phal chen): sems dpa'i bya ba thams cad la mthu yod de/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi smon lam gyi ye shes las lus su grub pa yin pas yongs su 'gyes par mi 'gyur ro/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na
240b6(phal chen): gzer dang mi ldan pa'i 'khrul 'khor ni shing gi yan lag de nyid yin yang dgos pa bya ba'i mthu med do/ /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i lhag pa'i bsam
240b7(phal chen): pa dang myi ldan na/ byang chub kyi yan lag gi tshogs de nyid yin yang sangs rgyas kyi chos bsgrub pa la mthu med do/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po la rin po che'i a ga
240b8(phal chen): ru nag po glang po'i snying po zhes bya ba yod pa des bdugs ma thag tu rgyal po'i 'khor los bsgyur ba'i yan lag bzhi'i dpung gis tshogs thams cad kyang nam mkha' la gnas par 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin du
241a1(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa a ga ru bdug pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyang khams gsum pa thams cad las rnam par 'das te/ de bzhin
241a2(phal chen): gshegs pa'i ye shes nam mkha'i spyod yul 'dus ma byas pa thams cad kyi mthar thug par 'gyur ro/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje ni rin po che ma rabs kyi 'byung khung nas mi 'byung
241a3(phal chen): gi rdo rje'i 'byung khungs ngam gser gyi 'byung khung nas 'byung ngo / /de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rdo rje lta bur 'ang sems can gyi bsam pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba ma rabs kyi rin po
241a4(phal chen): c he'i 'byung gnas nas mi skye ste gzhan du na sems can yongs su skyob pa'i snying rje chen po'i rdo rje'i 'byung khungs de thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la lhag par dmigs pa'i gser gyi 'byung khungs
241a5(phal chen): chen po nas 'byung ngo / /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ shing gis rigs rtsa ba med pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de'i rtsa ba mthar thug pa mi dmigs mod kyi shing rnams la yal ga dang lo ma dang 'dab
241a6(phal chen): ma dang me tog shin tu rgyas pa dra ba lta bur gyur pa yang snang ngo / de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i mthar thug pa'ang mi dmigs mod kyi 'jig rten gyi skye
241a7(phal chen): gnas thams cad du yang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bsod nams dang ye shes dang mngon par shes pa'i me tog shin tu rgyas pa smon lam chen po'i dra bar gyur pa yang yongs su snang ngo / /rigs
241a8(phal chen): kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje ni snod ngan pa'i gzhi la 'dug na mdzes par mi snang ngo / /snod ma rdol ba ma gtog par snod rdol ba dang / bu ga can gyis gzung bar mi nus so/ /de bzhin du thams
241b1(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i rdo rje chen po yang sems can mos pa zhan pa'i snod dang / ser sna can nam tshul khrim ngan nam gnod sems can nam/ le lo can nam/ dran pa 'khrug
241b2(phal chen): pa 'am/ shes rab 'chal pa can rnams la mi mdzes te/ byang chub sems dpa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa rin po che'i snod ma gtog par sems can lhag pa'i bsam pa log pa la zhugs pa
241b3(phal chen): blo mi brtan pa'i snod kyis kyang gzung bar mi nus so/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje ni rin po che thams cad 'bugs so/ /de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i rdo rje
241b4(phal chen): yang sangs rgyas kyi chos rin po che thams cad phugs par khong du chud par byed do/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje ni brag thams cad shigs par 'joms so/ /de bzhin du thams cad
241b5(phal chen): mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i/ rdo rje yang lta ba'i rnam pa thams cad kyi brag shigs par 'joms so/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje rin po che ni chag kyang thams cad las khyad
241b6(phal chen): par du 'phags pa'i gser gyi rgyan zil gyi gnon to/ /de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rdo rje rin po che bsam pa log par zhugs pas chag par gyur kyang nyan thos dang
241b7(phal chen): rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yon tan gyi gser gyi rgyan zil gyi gnon to/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje rin po che ni chags kyang phongs pa thams cad rnam par sel to/ /de bzhin du
241b8(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rdo rje rin po che nan tan med pas chag par gyur kyang / 'khor ba'i 'phongs pa thams cad rnam par sel to/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ /
242a1(phal chen): rdo rje'i khams ni ji tsam zhig tu chung yang nor bu dang rdo thams cad gcog pa'i mtshan nyid do/ /de bzhin du dmyigs pa ji tsam du chung ba la zhugs kyang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed
242a2(phal chen): pa rdo rje'i khams ni mi shes pa thams cad 'jig par byed pa'i mtshan nyid do/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje rin po che ni skye bo ma rabs kyi lag tu phyin par mi 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin du thams
242a3(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa/ rdo rje rin po che yang ma rabs kyi bsam pa dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba ngan ngon can gyi lha dang myi'i lag tu phyin par mi 'gyur ro/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/
242a4(phal chen): rin po che yongs su brtag pa la mi mkhas pa'i skyes bu ni rdo rje rin po che'i yon tan mi shes pas de'i yon tan nyams su myong bar myi 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin du shes rab 'chal pa'i ngang tshul dang ldan
242a5(phal chen): pa'i skyes bu gang zag kyang byang chub kyi sems rdo rje rin po che chen po'i yon tan la mi mkhas pas kyang de'i yon tan gyi khyad par nyams su myong bar myi 'gyur ro/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje
242a6(phal chen): ni zhu bar mi nus so/ /de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rgyur gyur pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa rdo rje yang zhu bar mi nus so/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje'i lag cha chen
242a7(phal chen): po ni gzhan du na mthu bo che chen po'i stobs ltar khyad par du 'phags pa'i mthu stobs kyi shugs drag po ma gtog par stobs po chen pos kyang gzung bar mi nus so/ /de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen
242a8(phal chen): p a nyid du sems bskyed pa'i rdo rje'i lag cha chen po yang gzhan du na byang chub sems dpa' chen po thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rgyu'i stobs kyi brtan pa dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa'i mthu bo che chen
242b1(phal chen): po'i stobs ltar khyad par du 'phags pa stobs kyi shugs chen po rab tu thob pa ma gtogs par nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas stobs chen po che thams cad kyis kyang yongs su gzung bar mi nus so/ /rigs
242b2(phal chen): kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ mtshon cha thams cad kyis mi tshugs pa gang du yang rdo rje mi tshugs pa med pa de kha mi 'bab po/ /de bzhin du sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / dul ba 'am/ dus gsum gyi
242b3(phal chen): b skal par spyad pa'i sdug bsngal dang 'grogs par bya ba gang du nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi smon lam dang ye shes kyi mtshon chas bdug pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i rdo rje'i
242b4(phal chen): mtshon cha chen po thogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yongs su skyo ba'i yid myed pas ni mi bzod pa med de/ kha mi 'bab po/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje ni gzhan du na rdo rje nyid las
242b5(phal chen): gyur pa'i gzhi ma gtogs par sa'i phyogs gang gis kyang gzung bar mi nus so/ /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i 'byung ba'i smon lam gyi tshogs rdo rje ni gzhan du na lhag pa'i bsam pas byang
242b6(phal chen): chub tu sems bskyed pa rdo rje brtan pa'i sa'i gzhi ma gtogs par nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis gzung bar mi nus so/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rgya mtsho chen po'i
242b7(phal chen): snod rdo rje'i gzhi sra zhing gseb med pas chu gseng du 'dzag par mi 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba byang chub kyi sems rdo rje gseb myed pa yongs su bsngos pa'i gzhi can
242b8(phal chen): la gnas pa yang srid par skyes pa thams cad kyis zad par mi 'gyur ro/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje'i gzhi la brten pa'i sa chen po ni 'jig par mi 'gyur ro/ /dma' bar mi 'gyur ro/ /
243a1(phal chen): de bzhin du byang chub tu sems bskyed pa rdo rje sra ba'i gzhi la rten pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam rnams kyang khams gsum thams cad du 'jig par mi 'gyur/ dma' bar mi 'gyur ro/ /
243a2(phal chen): rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje ni chus bangs pa 'am/ rul bar mi 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin du byang chub tu sems bskyed pa rdo rje yang las dang nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi chur bskal par gnas
243a3(phal chen): kyang rul bar mi 'gyur/ bangs par mi 'gyur ro/ /rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje ni mye thams cad kyis drod kyis kyang tshig par mi 'gyur/ yongs su gdung bar yang mi 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin
243a4(phal chen): du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rdo rje yang 'khor ba thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi mye'i drod thams cad kyis mi tshig go/ /nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi mye'i gdung bas tshig par mi 'gyur ro/ /
243a5(phal chen): rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas snying po byang chub la bzhugs shing / bdud rgol tu bzhug par mdzad pa dang / thams cad mkhyen
243a6(phal chen): p a nyid du mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba rnams kyi gdan ni gzhan du na stong gsum gyis stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdo rje'i lte ba'i sa'i gzhi ma gtog par sa'i phyogs gzhan
243a7(phal chen): gyis gzung bar mi nus so/ /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu smon lam 'debs pa dang / spyad pa spyod pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par
243a8(phal chen): byed pa dang / bzod pa la 'jug pa dang / sa thob par byed pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dang / lung bstan pa yongs su nod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam gyi tshogs
243b1(phal chen): thams cad nye bar ston pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mchod pa byed pa dang / chos kyi sprin chen po yongs su 'dzin pa rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i stobs dang / shugs dang drag
243b2(phal chen): s hul dang de dag kyang gzhan du na thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa smon lam thams cad kyis ye shes rdo rje sra ba'i lte ba can ma gtogs par sems can gzhan gyi yongs su gzung bar
243b3(phal chen): mi nus so/ /rigs kyi bu de ltar thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa ni yon tan de dag dang gzhan tshad myed pa nas/ yon tan gyis khyad par brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dang
243b4(phal chen): ldan pa ste/ sems can gang gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa de dag kyang yon tan gyi chos de lta bu dang ldan par gyur to/ /ldan par 'gyur ro/ /de bas na rigs
243b5(phal chen): kyi bu de ltar khyod bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed de/ yon tan 'di dag rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su tshol ba ni khyod kyis
243b6(phal chen): thob par bya ba legs par thob po/ /rigs kyi bu khyod de ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la spyad par bya/ ji ltar nan tan du bya zhes zer na/ rigs kyi bu khang pa brtsegs pa chen po rnam par
243b7(phal chen): snang mdzad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i snying po 'di nyid kyi nang du song ste ltos shig dang / der khyod kyis ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la slab par bya ba dang / bslabs nas
243b8(phal chen): kyang yon tan ji lta bu yongs su 'grub par 'gyur ba shes par 'gyur ro/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis byang chub sems dpa' byams pa la g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas te 'di skad
244a1(phal chen): ces smras so/ /'phags pa pho brang brtsegs pa'i chab sgo dbyer gsol nang du mchi'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' byams pas khang pa brtsegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi rgyan gyi
244a2(phal chen): brgyan pa'i snying po'i sgo drung du phyin te/ lag pa g.yas pa'i se gol gtog te/ sgra phyung ba dang / de'i sgo de yang rang bye bar gyur pa dang / des smras pa/ rigs kyi bu de khang pa brtsegs pa 'dir song
244a3(phal chen): shig / de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs ngo mtshar chen po thob par gyur te/ khang pa brtsegs pa de'i nang du phyin pa dang / phyin ma thag tu sgo de yang rang chad par gyur to/ /des mthong ba khang pa brtsegs
244a4(phal chen): pa shin tu rgya che zhing yangs la rgyar dpag tshad brgya stong mang po dang ldan pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi tshad kyis gzhal ba/ 'khor thams cad du nam mkha'i dbyings ltar yangs pa/ gdugs
244a5(phal chen): dang rgyal mtshan dang ba dan gyi rgya ni grangs med pas brgyan pa rin po che grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ mu tig gi phreng ba grangs med pa rab tu spyangs pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i
244a6(phal chen): phreng ba grangs med pa rab tu spyangs pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ mu tig dmar po'i phreng ba grangs med pa rab tu sbyangs pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ seng ge'i mu tig gi phreng ba grangs med pa rab tu
244a7(phal chen): spyangs pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ seng ge'i rgyal mtshan grangs med pa'i rgyan gyi brgyan pa/ zla ba dang zla gam grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ dar gyi lda ldi sna tshogs grangs med pa rab tu
244a8(phal chen): spyangs pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ dar gyi ba dan sna tshogs grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che mang po grangs med pa'i 'od kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ gser gyi dra ba grangs med pa'i
244b1(phal chen): rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i snam bu grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ gser gyi lcags phod rin po ches spras pa grangs med pa'i brgyan gyi brgyan pa/ dril bu sgra snyan pa 'byung
244b2(phal chen): ba grangs med pa'i rgyan gyi brgyan pa/ rin po che'i dril bu g.yer kha'i dra ba bskyod na yid du 'ong ba'i sgra 'byung ba/ grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ lha rdzas kyi me tog mang po'i char mngon
244b3(phal chen): par 'bab pa/ grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ lha rdzas kyi phreng ba'i lda ldi mngon par spyangs pa grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ gam yo nas spos kyi snod nas bdug spos kyis
244b4(phal chen): 'thul ba'i yo byad grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ gser phye ma'i char rab tu 'bab pa grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ pu shu'i dra ba grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ skar
244b5(phal chen): khung grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rta bab grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ ba gam grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ mye long gi dkyil 'khor grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/

244b7(phal chen): gos kyi sprin grangs med pa'i rgyan gyi brgyan pa/ rin po che'i shing grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i khri 'phangs grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i lam grangs med
244b8(phal chen): pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che grangs med pa'i bad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ sa'i gzhi rgyan sna tshogs grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che grangs med pa las brtsegs pa'i rgyan
245a1(phal chen): gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i khri grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i bu mo grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i snam bu grangs med pa bting ba'i 'chag sa'i rgyan

245a3(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i lus grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ bya'i tshogs sna tshogs yid du 'ong ba'i sgra 'byin pa grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i pad mo grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis
245a4(phal chen): brgyan pa/ rin po che'i srog shing 'dzin pa grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rdzing bu grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ me tog pun da ri ka grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i
245a5(phal chen): them skas grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i stegs bu rnam par bkod pa grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ sa rin po che sna tshogs grangs med pas spras pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/
245a6(phal chen): nor bu rin po che chen po'i 'od grangs med pa rab tu 'gyed pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che thams cad rnam par phye ba grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ yon tan dang legs pa phun sum tshogs
245a7(phal chen): pa grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan par 'dug pa mthong ste/ khang pa brtsegs pa de'i nang na yang khang pa brtsegs pa gzhan brgya stong 'di lta bu'i rgyan dang lhab lhub kyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i gdugs dang /
245a8(phal chen): rgyal mtshan dang / lha'i ba dan grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa nas/ yon tan dang legs pa phun sum tshogs pa grangs med pa'i bar gyis rgyan gyis brgyan pas gang bar mthong ngo / /khang pa
245b1(phal chen): brtsegs pa de dag thams cad kyang de ltar rgya che zhing yangs la de ltar tshad med de/ nam mkha'i mdzod du gyur pa/ kun nas shin tu spa bar 'khod par mthong ngo / /des khang pa brtsegs pa rnam par phye ba
245b2(phal chen): de dag thams cad kyang dmigs pa gcig la phan tshun ma 'dres pa dang / phan tshun ma 'dzings pa dang / phan tshun sal sal por 'dug par gzugs brnyan gyi tshul du de la snang bar gyur te/ dmyigs
245b3(phal chen): pa gcig la ji lta ba de bzhin du dmyigs pa ma lus pa de dag thams cad la yang snang bar mthong ngo / /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis khang pa brtsegs pa chen po rnam par snang mdzad kyis rgyan
245b4(phal chen): gyis brgyan pa'i snying po'i yul dang / rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnam pa de lta bu dag mthong nas dga' ba'i shugs dpag tu med pa rnam par 'phel ba'i spro ba dang / mos pa chen pos lus
245b5(phal chen): dang sems mngon par brlan pa dang / 'du shes kyi rnam pa thams cad rnam par bsil ba'i yid dang / sgrib pa thams cad rnam par zlog pa'i sems dang / rmongs pa thams cad rnam par grol ba dang /
245b6(phal chen): 'khrug pa med pa'i phyogs la rab tu gzhol ba dang / sgra thams cad la thogs pa med pa'i dran pas rnam par dmigs pa'i rna ba dang ldan pa dang / yid la bya ba'i rnam par 'khrug pa thams cad dang
245b7(phal chen): bral ba dang / rnam par thar pa sgrib pa med pa'i tshul gyi rjes su 'brang ba'i blo dang / dmigs pa thams cad la sgrib pa med par myig rab tu 'gro bar gyur nas phyogs kyi rgyud thams cad la mngon du bltas pa'i
245b8(phal chen): lus kyis phyag bya bar mngon par bsgrub pa'i stobs thams cad du khyab pa dang ldan pa'i lus thams cad kyis phab ste/ phyag byas so/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis phyag byas ma thag tu byang
246a1(phal chen): chub sems dpa' byams pa'i byin gyi brlabs kyis mthus khang pa brtsegs pa de dag thams cad kyi nang du bdag nyid phyin par shes par gyur to/ /khang pa brtsegs pa de dag thams cad du yang
246a2(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i yul can rnam pa sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad pa mang po yang mthong bar gyur te/ khang pa brtsegs pa la lar ni byang chub sems dpa' byams pas thog ma
246a3(phal chen): rigs ni gang du skyes ste/ mying ni ci zhes bya bar gyur pa zhig gi dge ba'i rtsa ba gang dang yongs su bskul ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gang gi yang dag par bskul ba dang tshe'i tshad ni ci tsam zhig du/

262b1(phal chen): bzang po'i spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor la 'jug par bya ba dang / ji ltar mngon par bsgrub pa dang / ji ltar smon par bya ba dang / ji ltar rgyas par bya ba dang / ji ltar rjes su 'brang bar bya ba dang / ji ltar yongasu rdzogs
262b2(phal chen): par sbyang bar bya ba dang / ji ltar yongasu rdzogs par bya ba dris shig dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen des khyod la ston par 'gyur ro/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas spyod pa mngon par bsgrub
262b3(phal chen): pa de lta bu'i smon lam gyi khyad par ni byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag stong la yang med do/ /'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa ni tshad med do/ /'jam dpal gzhon nur
262b4(phal chen): gyur pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan gyi khyad par tshad med do/ thams cad bsgrub pa ni tshad med do/ /'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa ni sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag stong gi yum lta bu'o/ /'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa
262b5(phal chen): ni byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag stong la gdams ngag ston pa'o/ /'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa ni sems can gyi khams thams cad yongasu smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba la rab tu brtson pa'o/ /'jam dpal gzhon
262b6(phal chen): nur gyur pa ni phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khamasu mying gi 'khor los rnam par rgyas par gyur pa'o/ /'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du gtam gyi skye bur gyur pa'o/ /'jam
262b7(phal chen): dpal gzhon nur gyur pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bsngags shing bstod pa'o/ /'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa ni chos thams cad yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du mthong ba ste/ chos zab mo'i ye shes la rnam par spyod
262b8(phal chen): pa'o/ /'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i rnam par thar pa thams cad kyi tshul thams cad la ring du song ba'i spyod yul dang ldan pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa kun tu bzang po la zhugs pa'o/ /rigs kyi bu dge ba'i bshes
263a1(phal chen): gnyen de ni khyod de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su bskyed pa'o/ /dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su 'phel bar byed pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs mang po rab tu sgrub pa'o/ /yang dag pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen ston pa'o/ /
263a2(phal chen): yon tan thams cad la yang dag par bskul ba'o/ /smon lam chen po'i dra ba thams cad du 'jug pa'o/ /smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa thams cad la rab tu gzhog pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi gsang ba
263a3(phal chen): thos par byed pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa'i bsam gyis mi khyab pa thams cad yang dag par ston pa'o/ /sngon gyi tshe'i gnas su skal ba 'thun par spyad pa'o/ /rigs kyi bu de bas na khyod da ltar yang 'jam dpal gyi
263a4(phal chen): rkang pa'i drung na 'dug gis yon tan gyi gdams ngag thams cad thob par bya ba la yongs su skyo ba ma bskyed cig yongs su sgyid lug par ma byed cig / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ nor bzangs khyod kyis dge ba'i bshes gnyen ji
263a5(phal chen): snyed cig mthong ba dang / spyod pa'i sgo ji snyed cig thos pa dang / rnam par thar pa'i tshul ji snyed cig la zhugs pa dang / smon lam gyi khyad par ji snyed cig khong du chud pa de dag thams cad kyang 'jam dpal gzhon
263a6(phal chen): nur gyur pa'i mthu dang byin gyi rlabasu blta ste/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa ni thams cad la'ang pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog thob pa'o/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis/ byang chub
263a7(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ yang dang yang bltas te/ byang chub sems dpa'
263a8(phal chen): byams pa'i drung nas song ngo / /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs grong khyer brgya rtsa bcu kun tu rgyus te/ phyogs kyi gnas yid bde ba mngon du 'gyur ba zhes bya ba zhig na 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la
263b1(phal chen): sems shing rnams par lta bas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa mthong bar mos shing / smon la phrad par dga' bas sdod cing 'dug pa dang / de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas/ dpag tshad brgya rtsa bcu'i
263b2(phal chen): pha rol nas lag pa brkyang ste/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs grong khyer yid bde ba mngon du 'gyur ba na 'dug pa'i spyi bor bzhag ste/ 'di skad ces smras so/ /rigs kyi bu legs so legs so/ /dad pa'i dbang
263b3(phal chen): po dang myi ldan pa sems skyo ba can/ bsam pa zhum pa can sbyor ba bor ba/ brtson 'grus ldog pa/ yon tan chung zad kyis dga' bar rtsi ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba gcig la zhen par gnas pa/ spyod pa dang smon lam mngon
263b4(phal chen): par bsgrub pa la myi mkhas pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongasu ma bzungs ba/ sangs rgyas kyis ma dgongs pa rnams kyis ni chos nyid 'di lta bu yongs su shes par bya ba dang tshul 'di lta bu dang / spyod yul
263b5(phal chen): 'di lta bu dang / gnas 'di lta bu yongs su shes par bya ba 'am/ rnam par shes par bya ba 'am/ khong du chud par bya ba 'am/ 'jug par bya ba 'am/ yid ches par bya ba 'am/ brtag par bya ba 'am/ rtogs
263b6(phal chen): par bya ba 'am/ thob par bya bar myi nus so/ /zhes te des de la chos kyi gtam gyis yang dag par bstan pa dang / yang dag par bskul ba dang / gzengs bstod pa dang / dga' bar byas te chos kyi sgo grangs myed pa dang
263b7(phal chen): ldan par byas nas ye shes mtha' yas pa'i snang ba chen po thob par byas te/ byang chub sems dpa'i gzungs dang / spobs pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / mngon par shes pa dang / ye shes mtha' yas pa'i byin gyis rlabs
263b8(phal chen): par byas te/ kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor la bzhag nas/ bdag gi yul la'ang rab tu bzhag ste/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyi drung nas song ngo / /
264a1(phal chen): shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba las sdong pos brgyan pa'i le'u ste/ bzhi bcu rtsa lnga pa'o// //sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen
264a2(phal chen): po'i mdo/ bam po bcu drug pa/ de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs dge ba'i bshes gnyen stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bsnyen bkur ba/ thams
264a3(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa nyid du tshogs bsags pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad kyi gdams ngag dang rjes su bstan pa la 'thun par 'dzin pas zhugs pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad kyi
264a4(phal chen): drung du bsam pa mnyam pa ste/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad dga' bar bya ba ste/ yid mi 'byung ba'i blo dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad kyi gdams ngag dang rjes su bstan pa'i tshul rgya mtsho'i
264a5(phal chen): rjes su song ba snying rje chen po'i bsam pa rgya mtsho las yang dag par byung ba'i snying po dang ldan pa/ byams pa chen po'i tshul gyi sprin gyis 'gro ba thams cad rnam par snang bar byas pa/ dga' ba chen po'i shugs rnam
264a6(phal chen): par 'phel ba'i lus dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa rgya chen po la rab tu zhi bar rnam par dpyod pa/ sgo thams cad nas lhug par 'phro ba'i gtong ba'i myig dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa
264a7(phal chen): thams cad kyi yon tan rgya mtsho'i nan tan rab tu rdzogs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mos pa'i lam du zhugs pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshogs la brtson 'grus kyi shugs rnam par 'phel ba
264a8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi sems dang bsam pas shin tu sbyangs pa'i blo dang ldan pa/ dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa la zhugs pa sangs rgyas
264b1(phal chen): thams cad kyi chos kyi tshul rgya mtsho khong du chud pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo'i tshul rgya mtsho'i rjes su song ba/ 'jig rten gyi skye gnas thams cad du gzugs brnyen yongs su ston pa'i
264b2(phal chen): spyod yul dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi smon lam gyi tshul rgya mtsho la zhugs pa/ bskal pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la rab tu zhugs pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi yul snang ba
264b3(phal chen): rab tu thob pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i dbang po thams cad rnam par 'phel ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam snang ba rab tu thob pa/ phyogs thams cad du sgrib pa med pa'i snang ba rab tu thob pa/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi tshul
264b4(phal chen): la rab tu zhugs pa'i blo dang ldan pa/ zhing gi tshul thams cad la snang ba rab tu grub pa sems can 'byam klas pa thams cad kyi don bya ba la rgyud dang mi 'thun pa myed pa rjes su song ngo / /sgrib pa'i g.yang sa'i ri thams cad rnam par
264b5(phal chen): 'thor ba/ sgrib pa med pa'i chos nyid kyi rjes su song ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sa'i gzhi kun tu gnas pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyi snying po can la rab tu zhi bar rnam par dpyod pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyod
264b6(phal chen): yul rjes su tshol ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyis rlabs pa de/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod yul la rnam par dpyod cing 'dug par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang
264b7(phal chen): po'i mying thos pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thos pa dang / smon lam gyi khyad par thos pa dang / tshogs yongs su bsgrub pa la 'jug pa dang gnas pa'i khyad par thos pa dang / mngon par bsgrub pa dang / 'byung ba'i lam
264b8(phal chen): gyi khyad par thos pa dang / kun tu bzang po'i sa'i tshul gyi rgyud thos pa dang / sa'i tshogs thos pa dang / sa thob par byed pa'i shugs thos pa dang / sa yongs su gnon pa thos pa dang / sa la gnas pa thos pa dang / sa sngon du
265a1(phal chen): 'dor bas rnam par gnon pa thos pa dang / sa'i spyod yul thos pa dang / sa'i byin gyis rlabs thos pa dang / sa la yang dag par gnas pa thos nas/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mthong bar dga' zhing sgom ste/
265a2(phal chen): nam mkha'i dbyings ltar shin tu yangs pa'i sems mngon par zhen pa thams cad las gyen du 'phags pa dang / zhing gi 'du shes shin tu bsgom pa dang / chags pa thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa'i sems chos thams
265a3(phal chen): cad las sgrib pa med pa'i spyod yul can dang / thogs pa myed pa'i sems phyogs rgya mtsho thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / sgrib pa med pa'i sems thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi yul yongs su gnon pa dang / shin tu rnam par dag
265a4(phal chen): pa'i sems snying pa byang chub kyi rgyan lhag mthong gis yongs su dag pa dang / shin tu rnam par phye ba'i sems sangs rgyas kyi chos rgya mtsho la zhugs pa dang / shin tu yangs pa'i sems sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs
265a5(phal chen): su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / shin tu phye ba'i sems sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad yongs su dag par byed pa dang / tshad med pa'i sems sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du gzugs brnyan rab tu 'byung
265a6(phal chen): ba dang / bskal pa thams cad du gnas pas myi zad cing mthar thug pa med pa'i sems de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi stobs dang mi snyings pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa'i mthar thug pas/ snying po byang chub rdo rje dam pa'i
265a7(phal chen): snying po can de la pad mo'i stan rin po che thams cad kyi lhun can zhig la de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdan seng ge'i khri la mngon par bltas te 'dug go/ /de ltar tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs de lta bu'i bsam pa dang / yid la bya ba la brtson
265a8(phal chen): par gnas pa'i sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i rlan dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po dang sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i bskal pa 'thun pas byang chub sems dpa' kun
265b1(phal chen): tu bzang po mthong bar 'gyur bar sngon gyi ltas bcu byung ngo / /bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po byang chub kyi rgyan rnam par dag pas rnam par dag par 'gyur ro/ sangs
265b2(phal chen): rgyas kyi zhing thams cad mi khom pa dang / ngan song dang / ngan 'gro'i lam thams cad rnam par bstsal bas rnam par dag par gyur to/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad pad mo'i tshul gyi rgyan ltar sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pas rnam
265b3(phal chen): par dag par gyur to/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad sems can thams cad kyi lus dang sems dga' zhing sim par byed pas/ rnam par dag par gyur to/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rin po che thams cad kyi rang bzhin du gnas
265b4(phal chen): pas rnam par dag par gyur to/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad sems can gyi khams kun mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos rab tu brgyan par kun nas gnas pas rnam par dag par gyur to/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rgyan dang lhab lhub
265b5(phal chen): kyi sprin gyis kun tu khebs par kun nas rnam par dag par gyur to/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad sems can gyi khams thams cad phan tshun byams pa'i sems dang / gnod sems med pa'i sems dang ldan par kun nas
265b6(phal chen): gnas pas rnam par dag par gyur to/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad snying po byang chub kyi rgyan gyis brgyan par kun nas gnas pas rnam par dag par gyur to/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad sems can thams cad sangs
265b7(phal chen): rgyas rjes su dran par yid la bya ba la brtson par kun nas gnas pas rnam par dag par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po mthong bar gyur to/ /sngon gyi ltas bcu po de dag byung bar gyur to/ /
265b8(phal chen): gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po mthong bar 'gyur ba'i sngon gyi ltas snang ba chen po bcu byung bar gyur te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu
266a1(phal chen): phra ba rnams las rdul shin tu phra ba re re zhing yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi dra ba mang po rnam par snang bar gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba rnams las rdul shin tu phra ba re re
266a2(phal chen): las kyang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor mang po 'thon te/ kha dog gcig pa dang kha dog sna tshogs dang kha dog brgya stong du mar chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par 'gengs par gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rdul shin tu
266a3(phal chen): phra ba rnams las/ rdul shin tu phra ba re re las kyang rin po che thams cad kyi sprin de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan rnam par dmyigs par byed pa mang po 'thon te/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par 'gengs
266a4(phal chen): par gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba rnams las rdul shin tu phra ba re re las kyang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba'i 'khor lo dang dkyil 'khor gyi sprin mang po 'thon te/ chos kyi
266a5(phal chen): dbyings thams cad rgyas par 'gengs par gyur te/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba rnams las rdul shin tu phra ba re re las kyang spos dang / me tog dang phreng ba dang byug pa dang bdug pa'i sprin mang po
266a6(phal chen): 'thon te/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i yon tan gyi chos rgya mtsho'i sprin thams cad kyi 'brug sgra rab tu sgrog cig phyogs bcu'i chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par 'gengs par gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams
266a7(phal chen): cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba rnams las rdul shin tu phra ba re re las kyang nyi ma dang zla ba dang skar ma'i sprin mang po 'thon te/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i 'od rab tu 'gyed cing / chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par
266a8(phal chen): 'gengs par gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba rnams las rdul shin tu phra ba re re las kyang lus thams cad kyi dbyibs ltar 'dug pa'i mar mye'i sprin mang po 'thon nas/ sangs rgyas kyi 'od
266b1(phal chen): gzer ltar rab tu snang bar byed cing chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par 'gengs par gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba rnams las rdul shin tu phra ba re re las kyang nor bu rin po che'i gzugs de bzhin
266b2(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi skur snang ba'i sprin mang po 'thon nas/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par 'gengs par gyur to/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba rnams las rdul shin tu phra ba
266b3(phal chen): re re las kyang 'od gzer gyi gzugs de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i dbyibs su snang ba'i sprin mang po 'thon te sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs dang smon lam gyi sprin gyi char mngon par 'bebs shing / chos

266b5(phal chen): thams cad kyi kha dog du snang ba'i sprin rgya mtsho sems can thams cad gdon pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa sems can thams cad kyi chos kyi bsam pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i bsgrub pa mang po 'thon te/ chos kyi dbyings
266b6(phal chen): thams cad rgyas par 'gengs par gyur to/ /byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mthong bar gyur ba'i sngon gyi ltas snang ba chen po bcu po de dag byung bar gyur to/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs gyis sngon gyi ltas su
266b7(phal chen): snang ba bcu po de dag mthong nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mthong bar gyur pa'i skabs ni bye/ rang gi dge ba'i rtsa bas ni brtan de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyis ni rlabs/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi
266b8(phal chen): chos kyi snang ba ni yang dag par skyes/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa la ni mngon du gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i smon lam gyi byin gyis ni byin du brlabs/ de bzhin gshegs pa
267a1(phal chen): thams cad kyi spyod yul la ni mngon par mos/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod yul rlabs po che la shin tu nges pa'i stobs dang / shugs ni rab tu thob/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mthong na/ thams cad
267a2(phal chen): mkhyen pa nyid thob pa dang 'dra bar ni sems/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mthong bar bya ba la dbang po ni mngon du gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mthong bar bya ba la brtson 'grus kyi shugs chen po ni thob/ byang
267a3(phal chen): chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po yongasu btsal ba la brtson 'grus phyir mi ldog pa'i sbyor ba dang ni ldan/ phyogs thams cad du mngon du gyur pa'i 'khor lo dang / kun tu lta bas yul yongs su gnon pa'i byang chub sems
267a4(phal chen): dpa'i lus dang sangs rgyas ma lus pa'i zhabs kyi drung na byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po 'dug pa'i rjes su 'brang ba'i sems de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dmyigs par bya ba la yang dag par btang ba dang / byang chub
267a5(phal chen): sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i dmigs pa yongs su btsal ba dang mi 'bral ba'i bsam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mthong bar bya ba'i 'du shes kyi rnam pa'i snying po dang ldan pa'i ye shes kyi myig byang chub sems dpa'
267a6(phal chen): kun tu bzang po'i lam la zhugs pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings ltar yangs pa'i bsam pa dang / snying rje chen po'i rdo rje thogs pa'i bsam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i rjes su 'brang bar smon pa/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i
267a7(phal chen): mur thug par byin gyis bslabs pa dang / yongs su gnon pa'i rtsal rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i sa la gnas pa'i ye
267a8(phal chen): shes la rnam par dpyod pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul la yang dag par gnas pa dang mi ldan pa des byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid rjes su thob pa/ dus gsum

267b2(phal chen): zil gyis ma non pa/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi rjes su 'brang ba/ mngon par 'phags pa'i yul dang ldan pa de/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi spyan sngar byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor

272b4(phal chen): g.yas pa brkyang ste bzhag par gyur to/ /de ltar tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyi spyi bo la byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos lag pa bzhag ma thag tu de'i mod la des ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo sangs rgyas kyi zhing
